3 启用行动：工具使用

3 Enabling actions: Tool use
3 启用行动：工具使用
Source
3 Enabling actions: Tool use
本章内容涵盖
Source
This chapter covers
LLM的局限性及其为何需要工具
Source
LLM limitations and why they need tools
工具调用与执行
Source
Tool calling and execution
构建和集成自定义工具
Source
Building and integrating custom tools
MCP用于工具标准化
Source
MCP for tool standardization
仅凭自身，大语言模型无法访问外部数据或与外部系统交互。
它们需要工具，以及选择和运用这些工具的能力，这对于实现智能体至关重要。
一个基本的智能体通过反复选择下一步要执行的操作来逐步完成任务，而工具使这成为可能。
Source
On their own, LLMs can't access external data or interact with external systems. They need tools and the ability to select and utilize those tools, which is central to implementing agents. A basic agent performs tasks step by step by repeatedly selecting the next action to take, and tools make this possible.
现在，让我们探索如何构建工具，并告知LLM如何使用它们。
我们还将学习LLM如何为给定任务选择合适的工具，并将工具执行结果反馈给LLM。
接着，我们将探讨Anthropic提出的模型上下文协议（MCP），这是一项旨在标准化工具开发与使用的倡议，如图3.1所示。
Source
Now, let’s explore how to build tools and inform the LLM how to use them. We'll also learn how the LLM chooses the appropriate tool for a given task and relays tool executions back to the LLM. Then we'll examine the Model Context Protocol (MCP) by Anthropic, an initiative that standardizes the development and use of tools, as shown in figure 3.1.
图3.1 书籍结构概览——聚焦第3章。
Source
Figure 3.1 Book structure overview - Chapter 3 in focus.
如图3.2所示，我们将构建一个利用工具执行现实世界操作的LLM系统，重点关注工具调用和工具执行组件。
我们将为LLM提供包含可用工具及其使用信息的上下文（在图中标记为“tool_info”）。
如果LLM确定需要使用工具（1），则执行该工具（2），并将结果添加到LLM的上下文中（3）。
如果LLM随后得出结论，认为无需进一步使用工具，可以直接生成最终答案，则输出该响应（4），该响应既会添加到上下文中，也会返回给用户（5）。
Source
As shown in figure 3.2, we'll construct an LLM system that takes real-world actions using tools, focusing on tool calling and tool execution components. We'll provide the LLM with context that includes information about the available tools and their usage (labeled as "tool_info" in the figure). If the LLM determines that a tool is needed (1), the tool is executed (2), and the result is added to the LLM's context (3). If the LLM then concludes that no further tool use is necessary and it can generate a final answer directly, it outputs that response (4), which is both added to the context and returned to the user (5).
图3.2：LLM接收用户输入，进行推理，选择必要工具，接收执行结果，并生成最终响应。
Source
Figure 3.2 The LLM receives user input, reasons about it, selects the necessary tool, receives the execution result, and produces a final response.
那么，要让一个大型语言模型成为能够与外部世界互动并实现目标的智能体，需要具备哪些条件呢？
让我们更仔细地看看那些帮助大型语言模型克服其局限性的工具类型。
Source
So, what does it take for an LLM to become an agent that interacts with the external world and achieves goals? Let's take a closer look at the types of tools that help LLMs overcome their limitations.
3.1 LLM工具
Source
3.1 LLM tools
尽管大型语言模型（LLM）能力令人印象深刻，但它们存在固有的局限性，使其无法作为完全自主的智能体运行。
这些局限性可分为三类：时间性、交互性和功能性。
Source
Despite their impressive capabilities, LLMs have inherent limitations that prevent them from functioning as fully autonomous agents. These limitations fall into three categories: temporal, interaction, and functional.
首先，LLM面临时间限制——它们无法访问超出其训练数据的信息，也无法检索实时变化的数据。
这使得它们在需要最新知识的任务中不可靠，例如回答关于近期事件或实时市场状况的问题。
Source
First, LLMs face a temporal limitation—they cannot access information beyond their training data or retrieve data that changes in real time. This makes them unreliable for tasks requiring current knowledge, such as answering questions about recent events or live market conditions.
其次，大语言模型存在交互限制——它们无法直接影响外部世界。
虽然它们可以生成描述某个动作的文本，但无法实际预订航班、发送电子邮件或控制设备。
Source
Second, LLMs have an interaction limitation—they cannot directly influence the external world. While they can generate text describing an action, they cannot actually book a flight, send an email, or control a device.
第三，大语言模型在专业领域存在功能局限性。
需要精确计算、代码执行或媒体生成的任务，通常超出了语言模型仅通过文本预测所能可靠完成的范围。
工具可以解决上述各项局限性。
Source
Third, LLMs suffer from functional limitations in specialized domains. Tasks requiring precise computation, code execution, or media generation often exceed what language models can reliably accomplish through text prediction alone. Tools address each of these limitations.
3.1.1 为什么我们需要LLM工具？
Source
3.1.1 Why do we need LLM tools?
信息增强工具通过向智能体上下文注入最新知识，弥合了时间差距。
这类工具包括网络搜索引擎、arXiv等特定领域检索系统或自定义数据库、用于获取天气或股价的实时API，以及查询公司知识库的内部知识系统。
如图3.2所示，这些工具提供的工具结果将LLM的认知范围扩展至其训练截止日期之后。
Source
Information-augmenting tools bridge the temporal gap by injecting up-to-date knowledge into the agent's context. These include web search engines, domain-specific retrieval systems like arXiv or custom databases, real-time APIs for weather or stock prices, and internal knowledge systems that query company repositories. As illustrated in figure 3.2, these tools deliver Tool Results that extend the LLM's awareness beyond its training cutoff.
行动执行工具通过使智能体能够影响现实世界，从而克服了交互限制。
示例包括酒店和航班的预订系统、用于邮件和日历管理的通信工具、用于文档生成的自动化工具，以及用于智能设备的物联网控制器。
这些工具触发行动并接收观察结果作为回报，从而与环境形成反馈循环。
Source
Action-executing tools overcome the interaction limitation by enabling agents to affect the real world. Examples include booking systems for hotels and flights, communication tools for emails and calendar management, automation tools for document generation, and IoT controllers for smart devices. These tools trigger Actions and receive Observations in return, forming a feedback loop with the environment.
领域专用工具通过处理大语言模型不擅长的任务，弥补了其功能上的局限性。
计算器、代码解释器、格式转换器、图像生成器和语音合成引擎等工具，使得混合式问题解决成为可能——将大语言模型的推理能力与特定领域的可靠执行相结合。
Source
Domain-specialized tools address functional limitations by handling tasks where LLMs fall short. Calculators, code interpreters, format converters, image generators, and voice synthesis engines allow hybrid problem-solving—combining the LLM's reasoning with reliable execution in specialized domains.
3.1.2 LLM工具类型
Source
3.1.2 Types of LLM tools
工具可分为开发者自定义构建或LLM提供商预定义两种类型。
定制工具由开发者开发或调整，以适应特定环境。
例如，包括与公司内部系统集成的API，或用于专业数据分析的脚本。
定制工具可以根据项目需求进行完全定制。
然而，这也意味着开发者需要负责构建、维护和保障工具的安全性——漏洞和安全问题由开发者承担。
Source
Tools are categorized as custom-built by the developer or predefined by the LLM provider. Custom tools are developed or adapted by the developer to fit a specific environment. Examples include APIs that integrate with internal company systems or scripts for specialized data analysis. Custom tools can be fully tailored to project requirements. However, this also means the developer is responsible for building, maintaining, and securing them—bugs and security issues are the developer’s responsibility.
非定制工具是由LLM提供商直接提供的预定义工具。
例如，OpenAI的网页搜索功能和Anthropic的网页搜索工具。
这些工具可以立即使用，无需任何开发工作，且由提供商负责稳定性和性能管理。
其代价在于它们不易修改或扩展，且提供商可自行决定更改或移除。
可用的非定制工具列表可在LLM提供商的官方文档中找到。
Source
Non-custom Tools are predefined and offered directly by the LLM provider. Examples include OpenAI’s web search feature and Anthropic’s web search tool. These tools can be used immediately without any development effort, and the provider manages stability and performance. The trade-off is that they cannot be easily modified or extended, and they can be changed or removed at the provider’s discretion. The list of available non-custom tools can be found in the official documentation of the LLM provider.
LLM提供商正在持续扩展其内置工具产品。
OpenAI通过其Assistants API提供代码解释器、文件搜索和网页浏览功能。
Anthropic提供计算机使用和网页搜索工具。
Google的Gemini包含代码执行和Google搜索集成功能。
这些工具已可用于生产环境，维护良好，且无需实施工作。
鉴于这一趋势，您可能会疑惑：为何还要构建自定义工具？
Source
LLM providers are continuously expanding their built-in tool offerings. OpenAI provides code interpreter, file search, and web browsing capabilities through their Assistants API. Anthropic offers computer use and web search tools. Google's Gemini includes code execution and Google Search integration. These tools are production-ready, well-maintained, and require no implementation effort. Given this trend, you might wonder: why build custom tools at all?
本书聚焦于自定义工具，主要有两个原因。
首先，理解工具的内部工作原理对于调试智能体故障至关重要。
当智能体产生意外结果时，你需要判断问题出在工具实现、LLM的工具选择还是结果处理方式上。
内置工具是黑盒，掩盖了这些细节。
其次，现实世界中的智能体通常需要服务商未提供的专门能力。
查询公司内部数据库、集成专有API或实现领域特定逻辑，都需要自定义工具。
Source
This book focuses on custom tools for two reasons. First, understanding how tools work internally is essential for debugging agent failures. When an agent produces unexpected results, you need to know whether the issue lies in the tool's implementation, the LLM's tool selection, or the way results are processed. Built-in tools are black boxes that obscure these details. Second, real-world agents often require specialized capabilities that providers don't offer. Querying your company's internal database, integrating with proprietary APIs, or implementing domain-specific logic all require custom tools.
话虽如此，提供商工具自有其用武之地。
对于快速原型设计，或者当内置工具符合需求时，使用提供商工具是合理的选择。
开发定制工具所培养的技能，将帮助你评估何时应该自行构建，何时应该利用现有工具。
Source
That said, provider tools have their place. For rapid prototyping or when a built-in tool matches your needs, using provider tools makes sense. The skills you develop building custom tools will help you evaluate when to build versus when to use what's already available.
3.2 大型语言模型如何使用工具
Source
3.2 How LLMs use tools
一个只能生成文本的模型，究竟是如何选择并执行工具的呢？
答案在于一种称为工具调用的机制。
为了更好地理解工具调用，不妨想象这样一个比喻：将大语言模型看作一位被锁在房间里、没有任何工具的智者。
尽管它从海量文本中学到了丰富的知识，却只能通过门缝下递纸条的方式与人交流。
它不知道外面有哪些工具、这些工具如何运作，也无法直接使用它们。
这时就需要我们介入——我们递进一张纸条，说明可用的工具有哪些、每个工具的功能是什么，以及需要完成什么任务。
Source
How does a model that can only generate text actually select and execute a tool? The answer lies in a mechanism called Tool Calling. To better understand Tool Calling, consider this metaphor: imagine the LLM as a wise sage locked in a room with no tools. Though it has learned a vast amount from countless texts, it can only communicate by passing notes under the door. It doesn’t know what tools exist outside, how they work, or how to use them directly. That’s where we come in—we send a note explaining what tools are available, how each one functions, and what task needs to be completed.
我们可以将这个说明视为工具定义，即一个结构化的描述，告诉LLM哪些工具（函数、API或操作）是可访问的、它们需要什么参数以及它们的功能是什么。
一旦LLM接收到这些信息，它就可以开始推理对于给定任务哪个工具是合适的以及如何使用它，这一切都通过文本生成来完成。
在LLM确定需要哪个工具后，它会生成一个工具调用——这是一个结构化输出，包含工具名称以及调用该工具所需的参数。
然后，这个工具调用会被传递给外部执行器，由它在现实世界中实际运行该工具或API。
Source
We can think of this note as a tool definition, a structured description that tells the LLM what tools (functions, APIs, or actions) are accessible, what parameters they expect, and what they do. Once the LLM receives this information, it can begin reasoning about which tool is appropriate for a given task and how to use it, purely through text generation. After the LLM decides which tool is needed, it generates a tool call—a structured output that includes the name of the tool and the arguments required to invoke it. Then, this tool call is passed to an external executor, which actually runs the tool or API in the real world.
现在，让我们更仔细地看看工具定义的结构、如何提供给模型，以及工具调用生成和执行过程的工作原理。
本节所有代码示例均可在我们的GitHub仓库中找到，地址为https://github.com/shangrilar/ai-agent-from-scratch。
Source
Now, let’s take a closer look at how a tool definition is structured, how it is provided to the model, and how the tool call generation and execution process works. You can find all the code examples for this section in our GitHub repository at https://github.com/shangrilar/ai-agent-from-scratch.
3.2.1 工具调用的工作原理
Source
3.2.1 How tool calling works
工具调用涉及一个多步骤的过程，如图3.3所示。
要启动工具使用，开发者需向LLM发送一条消息（代表用户输入）以及工具定义，这是步骤1。
Source
Tool calling involves a multi-step process, as illustrated in figure 3.3. To initiate tool usage, the developer sends a message (representing user input) to the LLM, along with tool definitions, which is step 1.
需要指出一个重要事实：LLM本身并不执行工具。
相反，它会生成一个文本规范，指明应该调用哪个工具以及使用什么参数。
从这个意义上说，LLM充当用户请求与可用工具之间的中介。
基于LLM的应用或智能体负责实际执行工具——这对应图中第3步。
工具执行后，结果会返回给LLM，LLM解释输出并继续对话。
最终给用户的响应会包含这个结果。
Source
One important thing to note is that the LLM does not execute the tools itself. Rather, it generates a textual specification indicating which tool should be called and with what parameters. In this sense, the LLM acts as a mediator between the user's request and the available tools. The LLM-based application or agent handles the actual execution of the tool—this corresponds to step 3 in the diagram. Once the tool is executed, the result is returned to the LLM, which interprets the output and continues the conversation. The final response to the user incorporates this result.
图3.3 工具调用的关键步骤——工具定义、交付和LLM工具选择，来源：https://platform.openai.com/docs/guides/function-calling?api-mode=responses。
Source
Figure 3.3 Key steps in tool calling – tool definition, delivery, and LLM tool selection, source: https://platform.openai.com/docs/guides/function-calling?api-mode=responses.
因此，要实现工具调用，我们必须：
Source
Therefore, to enable tool calling, we must:
定义提供给LLM的工具定义。
Source
Define the tool definitions provided to the LLM.
定义实际工具。
Source
Define the actual tools.
向LLM提供要执行的任务以及步骤1中的工具定义。
Source
Provide the LLM with the task to perform and tool definitions from step 1.
构建一个能够根据大语言模型生成的工具调用执行工具的系统。
Source
Build a system that can execute the tools based on the tool calls generated by the LLM.
将执行结果反馈回LLM的上下文中。
Source
Reflect the execution results back into the LLM’s context.
现在，让我们来看看如何实现这些步骤中的每一个。
Source
Now, let’s take a look at how each of these steps can be implemented.
步骤1：指定工具定义
Source
Step 1: Specify tool definitions
第一步是创建一个结构化的定义，告诉LLM有哪些工具可用以及如何使用它们。
可以将其视为LLM的使用说明书。
让我们通过从外到内查看一个计算器工具定义来了解这是如何工作的：
Source
The first step is to create a structured definition that tells the LLM what tools are available and how to use them. Think of this as an instruction manual for the LLM. Let's examine how this works by looking at a calculator tool definition from the outside in:
从最外层开始，我们指定 "type": "function" 来表示这是一个可调用的工具。
在内部，我们定义函数对象，它包含三个基本组成部分：
Source
Starting at the outermost level, we specify "type": "function" to indicate this is a callable tool. Inside, we define the function object with three essential components:
工具的标识符，LLM将使用它来调用该工具（“计算器”）
Source
name: The tool's identifier that the LLM will use to call it ("calculator")
何时以及为何使用此工具（“执行基本算术运算”）
Source
description: When and why to use this tool ("Perform basic arithmetic operations")
参数：使用工具所需的输入规范
Source
parameters: The specification of inputs needed to use the tool
参数部分采用JSON Schema格式，定义了工具期望的每个输入。
对于我们的计算器，我们需要三个输入：一个运算符（通过枚举约束限制为加、减、乘或除）和两个数字。
必填字段确保LLM始终提供所有必要的输入。
Source
The parameters section follows a JSON Schema format, defining each input the tool expects. For our calculator, we need three inputs: an operator (limited to add, subtract, multiply, or divide through the enum constraint), and two numbers. The required field ensures the LLM always provides all necessary inputs.
清单3.1 计算器工具定义模式
Source
Listing 3.1 Calculator tool definition schema
代码保持原样
calculator_tool_definition = { "type": "function", "function": { "name": "calculator", "description": "Perform basic arithmetic operations.", "parameters": { "type": "object", "properties": { "operator": { "type": "string", "description": "Arithmetic operation to perform", "enum": ["add", "subtract", "multiply", "divide"] }, "first_number": { "type": "number", "description": "First number for the calculation" }, "second_number": { "type": "number", "description": "Second number for the calculation" } }, "required": ["operator", "first_number", "second_number"], } } }
第二步：设置工具
Source
Step 2: Set up the tool
可以定义一个Python函数，例如calculator()，以匹配之前提供的输入模式。
基于LLM生成的函数名和参数，我们调用正确的函数并传入适当的参数。
Source
A Python function, such as calculator(), can be defined to match the input schema provided earlier. Based on the function name and arguments generated by the LLM, we invoke the correct function with the appropriate parameters.
清单3.2 计算器函数实现
Source
Listing 3.2 Calculator function implementation
代码保持原样
def calculator(operator: str, first_number: float, second_number: float): if operator == 'add': return first_number + second_number elif operator == 'subtract': return first_number - second_number elif operator == 'multiply': return first_number * second_number elif operator == 'divide': if second_number == 0: raise ValueError("Cannot divide by zero") return first_number / second_number else: raise ValueError(f"Unsupported operator: {operator}")
步骤3：执行工具调用
Source
Step 3: Executing the tool calling
现在，LLM接收工具定义和用户问题，并决定是否需要工具以及如果需要，使用哪个工具。
例如，考虑两个查询：“韩国的首都是什么？”和“1234乘以5678等于多少？”。使用定义了计算器的工具定义，LLM对第一个查询以纯文本回答，而对第二个查询则生成工具调用，包括正确的运算符（乘法）和操作数（1234、5678）。
Source
Now, the LLM receives the tool definitions and the user’s question, and decides whether a tool is needed and, if so, which one. For example, consider two queries: “What’s the capital of South Korea?” and “What is 1234 x 5678?” Using a tool definition that defines a calculator, the LLM responds to the first with a plain text answer, but responds to the second by generating a Tool Call, including the correct operator (multiply) and operands (1234, 5678).
清单3.3 工具调用执行示例
Source
Listing 3.3 Tool calling execution example
代码保持原样
tools = [calculator_tool_definition] response_without_tool = completion( model='gpt-5-mini', messages=[{"role": "user", ➥"content": "What is the capital of South Korea?"}], tools=tools ) print(response_without_tool.choices[0].message.content) print(response_without_tool.choices[0].message.tool_calls) response_with_tool = completion( model='gpt-5-mini', messages=[{"role": "user", "content": "What is 1234 x 5678?"}], tools=tools ) print(response_with_tool.choices[0].message.content) print(response_with_tool.choices[0].message.tool_calls) The output is as follows: # Capital question doesn’t need tool call The capital of South Korea is Seoul. None # Multiplication question needs tool call None [ChatCompletionMessageFunctionToolCall(id='call_viaOEiQJ5VEB9YvKl95qlDjM', function=Function(arguments='{"operator":"multiply","first_number":1234,"second_number":5678}', name='calculator'), type='function')]
从输出结果可以看出，该模型展示了智能化的工具选择能力。
对于首都问题，模型直接提供了答案（"韩国的首都是首尔"），没有调用任何工具——这通过tool_calls为None来指示——因为该信息已存在于其训练数据中。
相比之下，对于乘法问题，模型识别出需要计算辅助，并生成了包含适当参数的工具调用，同时content字段变为None。
这种选择性行为表明，大语言模型能够辨别何时需要工具辅助，何时可以直接基于其知识库回答问题。
Source
As you can see from the output, the model demonstrates intelligent tool selection. For the capital question, the model provides a direct answer ("The capital of South Korea is Seoul") without invoking any tools—indicated by tool_calls being None—since this information is already present in its training data. In contrast, for the multiplication question, the model recognizes it needs computational assistance and generates a tool call with the appropriate parameters, while the content field becomes None. This selective behavior shows that LLMs can discern when tools are necessary versus when they can answer directly from their knowledge base.
步骤4：运行工具
Source
Step 4: Running the tool
现在，大语言模型请求的工具需要被执行。
由于大语言模型本身无法运行任何代码，我们必须作为宿主系统来执行这个操作。
Source
Now, the tool that the LLM has requested needs to be executed. Since the LLM itself cannot run any code, we—as the host system—must perform the execution.
通过工具调用，从LLM返回的函数名称和参数被提取出来——即function_name和function_args。
如果选定的函数是计算器，则通过传入LLM生成的参数来执行计算器函数。
Source
The function name and arguments returned by the LLM through Tool Calling are extracted—function_name and function_args. If the selected function is the calculator, the calculator function is executed by passing in the arguments generated by the LLM.
清单3.4 从响应中提取并执行工具
Source
Listing 3.4 Extract and execute tool from response
代码保持原样
ai_message = response_with_tool.choices[0].message if ai_message.tool_calls: for tool_call in ai_message.tool_calls: function_name = tool_call.function.name function_args = json.loads(tool_call.function.arguments) if function_name == "calculator": result = calculator(**function_args)
步骤5：将结果反馈给LLM
Source
Step 5: Feeding results back to the LLM
最后，我们将工具的执行结果反馈给LLM。
具体做法是在对话中追加一条角色为“工具”的新消息，并将输出内容包含在其中。
更新后的上下文随后传回给LLM，由其生成最终响应。
Source
Finally, we feed the result of the tool back into the LLM. This is done by appending a new message to the conversation with a role of "tool" and including the output in the content. The updated context is then passed back to the LLM, which generates the final response.
清单3.5 将工具结果反馈给LLM
Source
Listing 3.5 Feed tool results back to LLM
代码保持原样
ai_message = response_with_tool.choices[0].message messages.append({ #A "role": "assistant", #A "content": ai_message.content, #A "tool_calls": ai_message.tool_calls #A }) if ai_message.tool_calls: for tool_call in ai_message.tool_calls: function_name = tool_call.function.name #B function_args = json.loads(tool_call.function.arguments) #B if function_name == "calculator": result = calculator(**function_args) #B messages.append({ #C "role": "tool", #C "tool_call_id": tool_call.id, #C "content": str(result) #C }) final_response = completion( model='gpt-5-mini', messages=messages ) print(“Messages: “, messages) print("Final Answer:", final_response.choices[0].message.content)
输出如下：
Source
The output is as follows:
代码保持原样
Messages: [{'role': 'user', 'content': 'What is 1234 x 5678?'}, ➥{'role': 'assistant', 'content': None, 'tool_calls': ➥[ChatCompletionMessageFunctionToolCall(id='call_TN8z8oUZ4g8hLwRfYTYFhDGD', ➥function=Function(arguments='{"operator":"multiply", ➥"first_number":1234,"second_number":5678}', name='calculator'), ➥type='function')]}, ➥{'role': 'tool', 'tool_call_id': 'call_TN8z8oUZ4g8hLwRfYTYFhDGD', ➥'content': '7006652'}] Final Answer: 1234 × 5678 = 7,006,652
执行遵循一个三步反馈循环。
首先，将助手的工具调用请求添加到消息历史中。
然后，使用解析出的参数（乘法，1234，5678）执行计算器函数，返回结果7006652。
该结果作为一条“工具”角色消息，并附上匹配的tool_call_id，被追加到消息历史中。
当这个完整的对话历史被发送回LLM时，它会解释原始结果，并将其格式化为清晰、人类可读的答案，并采用适当的数字格式。
Source
The execution follows a three-step feedback loop. First, the assistant's tool call request is added to the message history. Then, the calculator function is executed with the parsed arguments (multiply, 1234, 5678), returning 7006652. This result is appended as a "tool" role message with the matching tool_call_id. When this complete conversation history is sent back to the LLM, it interprets the raw result and formats it into a clear, human-readable answer with proper number formatting.
在我们的计算器示例中，计算器得出的结果就是最终答案，因此将结果反馈给LLM可能显得多余。
然而，对于更复杂的工具——例如网络搜索——这一点则至关重要。
例如，搜索结果必须返回给LLM，以便它能够从相关来源综合出最终回答。
这种调用→执行→返回→推理的循环对于实现一致的工具使用至关重要。
Source
In our calculator example, the result from the calculator is the final answer, so feeding the result back to the LLM may seem redundant. However, for more complex tools—such as web search—it is crucial. For example, search results must be returned to the LLM so it can synthesize the final response from relevant sources. This loop of call → execute → return → reason is essential to consistent tool use.
3.2.2 LLM如何选择工具
Source
3.2.2 How can an LLM choose tools
那么，LLM是如何学会选择工具并生成所需输入的呢？
答案在于LLM是如何通过工具使用示例进行训练的。
Source
So, how does the LLM learn to select tools and generate the required inputs? The answer lies in how the LLM is trained on tool usage examples.
在训练过程中，大型语言模型会接触到包含工具定义与相应工具调用配对的训练数据集。
例如，当接收到类似“请将客厅百叶窗设置为75%开合度”的请求时，训练数据会向模型展示：它应当调用`set_blind_openness`函数，并传入参数`room='living room'`和`openness_percentage=75`。
Source
During training, LLMs are exposed to datasets containing tool definitions paired with appropriate tool calls. For example, given a request like "Please set the living room blinds to 75% openness," the training data shows the model that it should call the `set_blind_openness` function with arguments `room='living room'` and `openness_percentage=75`.
通过学习这些示例，模型能够发展出以下能力：
Source
By learning from such examples, the model develops the ability to:
根据用户请求识别何时需要使用工具
Source
Recognize when a tool is needed based on the user's request
从可用选项中选择合适的工具
Source
Select the appropriate tool from the available options
从用户输入中提取正确的参数值
Source
Extract the correct parameter values from the user's input
按照预期的结构格式化工具调用
Source
Format the tool call in the expected structure
这种训练过程类似于大型语言模型如何通过在海量数据中进行模式识别来学习其他能力。
关键区别在于，工具调用要求模型输出结构化数据（函数名称和参数），而非自由形式的文本。
Source
This training process is similar to how LLMs learn other capabilities through pattern recognition across large amounts of data. The key difference is that tool calling requires the model to output structured data (function names and arguments) rather than free-form text.
如果你好奇训练数据的具体样貌，可以探索HuggingFace上的数据集，例如NousResearch的hermes-function-calling-v1（https://huggingface.co/datasets/NousResearch/hermes-function-calling-v1），其中包含用于训练函数调用模型的工具定义及对应工具调用示例。
Source
If you're curious about what this training data looks like, you can explore datasets like NousResearch's hermes-function-calling-v1 on HuggingFace (https://huggingface.co/datasets/NousResearch/hermes-function-calling-v1), which contains examples of tool definitions and corresponding tool calls used to train models for function calling.
3.2.3 有效工具调用的指南
Source
3.2.3 Guidelines for effective tool calling
以下最佳实践改编自OpenAI官方文档中关于函数调用的内容。
为了让LLM能够可靠地调用工具，工具的架构必须明确说明何时、什么以及如何操作。
下面的每对示例展示了一个有问题的模式、其修正版本，以及简要说明为何修正有效。
Source
The following best practices are adapted from OpenAI's official documentation on function calling. For LLMs to call tools reliably, a tool’s schema must make when, what, and how crystal clear. Each pair of examples below illustrates a problematic schema, its corrected version, and a brief explanation of why the fix is effective.
清晰且明确的函数定义
Source
Clear and explicit function definitions
LLM通过函数名称和参数描述来学习何时以及如何使用工具。
明确界定工具的用途、参数类型和预期输出。
一个好的经验法则是：如果实习生仅凭模式就能理解并使用工具，那么LLM也能做到。
Source
LLMs learn when and how to use tools based on function names and parameter descriptions. Define the tool’s purpose, parameter types, and expected outputs explicitly. A good rule of thumb: if an intern can understand and use the tool from the schema alone, so can an LLM.
清单3.6 反模式：模糊的工具定义
Source
Listing 3.6 Anti-pattern: vague tool definition
代码保持原样
{ "name": "book", "description": "Book something", "parameters": { "type": "object", "properties": { "when": { "type": "string" } } } }
该模式隐藏了动作的对象（例如，“预订什么？”），省略了必填字段，并且未指定时间格式。
模型无法推断哪些输入是必需的，或者如何格式化它们。
Source
This schema hides the object of the action (e.g., 'book what?'), omits required fields, and leaves the time format unspecified. The model can’t infer which inputs are mandatory or how to format them.
清单3.7 改进：显式工具定义
Source
Listing 3.7 Improved: explicit tool definition
代码保持原样
{ "name": "reserve_table", "description": "Create a restaurant table reservation.", "parameters": { "type": "object", "properties": { "restaurant_id": { "type": "string", "description": "Internal ID, e.g., rst_123" }, "datetime": { "type": "string", "format": "date-time", "description": "ISO-8601 in the user's local time" }, "party_size": { "type": "integer", "minimum": 1, "maximum": 20 }, "notes": { "type": "string", "description": "Allergies, occasion, etc. Optional." } } "required": ["restaurant_id", "datetime", "party_size"], } }
改进版本通过名称和描述明确陈述其意图，区分必需参数和可选参数，约束格式和范围以使输入可预测，并定义明确的错误代码，使模型能够一致地呈现或处理这些错误。
Source
The improved version states its intent plainly through the name and description, distinguishes between required and optional parameters, constrains formats and ranges to make inputs predictable, and defines explicit error codes that the model can surface or handle consistently.
应用软件工程最佳实践
Source
Apply software engineering best practices
避免使用模糊或逻辑冲突的参数（例如，toggle_light(on: bool, off: bool) 允许矛盾的输入）。
将互斥的布尔值替换为单个枚举。
同时，在模式中验证范围和格式，以便能够通过清晰的错误代码尽早拒绝。
Source
Avoid ambiguous or logically conflicting parameters (e.g., toggle_light(on: bool, off: bool) allows contradictory inputs). Replace mutually exclusive booleans with a single enum. Also, validate ranges and formats in the schema so that you can reject early with clear error codes.
清单3.8 反模式：参数冲突
Source
Listing 3.8 Anti-pattern: conflicting parameters
代码保持原样
{ "name": "toggle_light", "parameters": { "type": "object", "properties": { "on": { "type": "boolean" }, "off": { "type": "boolean" } } } }
在这里，模型可能会产生不可能的组合，例如同时设置为“开”和“关”。
这种模糊性迫使需要额外的提示逻辑，并增加了调用失败的可能性。
Source
Here, the model can produce impossible combinations, such as on=true and off=true. That ambiguity forces extra prompt logic and increases the likelihood of call failures.
清单3.9 改进版：单一枚举参数
Source
Listing 3.9 Improved: single enum parameter
代码保持原样
{ "name": "toggle_light", "description": "Control the light state", "parameters": { "type": "object", "properties": { "state": { "type": "string", "enum": ["on", "off"], "description": "The desired state of the light" } } "required": ["state"], } }
该设计通过将状态建模为单一枚举来消除矛盾，通过亮度范围检查实现确定性早期拒绝，并提供具体的错误代码，这些代码清晰地映射到恢复策略，例如重试、用户引导或备用方案。
Source
This design removes contradiction by modeling state as a single enum, enables deterministic early rejection through brightness range checks, and provides concrete error codes that map cleanly to recovery strategies, such as retries, user guidance, or fallbacks.
降低模型负载并有效使用代码
Source
Reduce model load and use code effectively
不要让模型重新提供你已经拥有的标识符。
让代码记住上下文，让模型专注于决策本身。
Source
Do not make the model resupply identifiers you already have. Let code remember context, and let the model focus on the decision itself.
让模型重新生成已获取的信息是低效的。
例如，如果在前一步骤中已获取了order_id，那么提供一个无参数的函数（如submit_refund()），并通过代码自动传递order_id，比要求模型调用一个需要order_id作为输入的函数更高效。
Source
It is inefficient to have the model regenerate information that has already been obtained. For example, if an order_id was retrieved in a previous step, it's more efficient to provide a parameterless function, such as submit_refund(), and pass the order_id automatically through code, rather than asking the model to call a function that requires order_id as an input.
清单3.10 反模式：模型提供的标识符
Source
Listing 3.10 Anti-pattern: model-supplied identifiers
代码保持原样
{ "name": "submit_refund", "parameters": { "type": "object", "required": ["order_id", "reason"], "properties": { "order_id": { "type": "string", "description": "The order ID to refund" }, "reason": { "type": "string", "description": "Reason for the refund" } } } }
这种方法迫使模型在每次调用时都必须正确回忆并传递order_id，这会增加错误风险和令牌使用量，尤其是在多步骤流程中，标识符可能会漂移或混淆。
Source
This approach forces the model to recall and pass order_id correctly on every call, which increases error risk and token usage, especially in multi-step flows where identifiers can drift or be confused.
清单3.11 改进版：仅决策参数
Source
Listing 3.11 Improved: decision-only parameters
代码保持原样
{ "name": "submit_refund", "parameters": { "type": "object", "required": ["reason"], "properties": { "reason": { "type": "string", } } } }
现在模型仅提供决策输入——即理由——而调用代码则从上下文中注入正确的order_id。
这降低了错误退款的可能性，减少了提示成本，并提高了多轮工作流程的成功率。
Source
Now the model supplies only the decision input—the reason—while the calling code injects the correct order_id from context. This reduces the chance of refunding the wrong order, lowers prompt cost, and improves success rates across multi-turn workflows.
限制功能数量
Source
Limit the number of functions
作为一般准则，请将工具数量保持在20个以下。
使用过多工具可能导致选择错误。
如果您的任务需要大量工具或复杂逻辑，可考虑微调模型以提高工具调用的准确性。
Source
As a general guideline, keep the number of tools under 20. Using too many tools can lead to selection errors. If your task requires many tools or complex logic, consider fine-tuning the model to improve Tool Calling precision.
3.3 为大型语言模型构建工具与工具定义
Source
3.3 Building tools and tool definitions for LLMs
既然我们已经理解了工具调用的工作原理，现在让我们从头开始构建一个真正的工具。
我们将实现一个网络搜索工具，这是任何研究智能体最核心的能力之一。
通过这个过程，你将亲身体验打造一个生产就绪的工具需要付出什么。
Source
Now that we understand how tool calling works, let's build a real tool from scratch. We'll implement a web search tool, one of the most essential capabilities for any research agent. Through this process, you'll experience firsthand what it takes to create a production-ready tool.
3.3.1 实现网络搜索工具
Source
3.3.1 Implementing a web search tool
对于网络搜索，我们将使用Tavily而非Google Search API或Bing API等替代方案，因为它针对LLM进行了优化，提供的结果更易于处理。
要使用Tavily，首先需要在 https://www.tavily.com/ 注册。
然后，从 https://app.tavily.com/home 获取您的API密钥。
Tavily每月提供最多1,000次免费API调用。
Source
For web search, we’ll use Tavily over alternatives like Google Search API or Bing API, because it’s optimized for LLMs, delivering results that are easier to process. To use Tavily, first you need to sign up at https://www.tavily.com/. Then, retrieve your API key from https://app.tavily.com/home. Tavily allows up to 1,000 free API calls per month.
在继续之前，请先安装Tavily Python客户端：
Source
Before continuing, install the Tavily Python client:
代码保持原样
uv add tavily-python
然后，将您的API密钥存储在.env文件中，使用TAVILY_API_KEY变量。
Source
Then, store your API key in a .env file using the TAVILY_API_KEY variable.
代码保持原样
TAVILY_API_KEY=<Your Tavily API KEY>
从简单开始
Source
Starting simple
让我们从最简单的实现开始，以验证一切正常运作。
现阶段的目标是确认能够连接到API并获取结果。
我们将保持配置的简洁性，仅在必要时增加复杂度。
Source
Let's start with the simplest possible implementation to verify everything works. At this stage, our goal is just to confirm that we can connect to the API and retrieve results. We'll keep the configuration minimal and add complexity only when needed.
代码遵循一种直接的模式。
首先，我们使用load_dotenv()加载环境变量，它会从.env文件中读取我们的API密钥。
然后我们使用该密钥创建一个TavilyClient实例。
search_web函数本身非常简洁：它接收一个查询字符串，调用Tavily API的search()方法，然后返回结果。
我们将max_results默认设置为2，以便在开发过程中保持响应简洁并降低API成本。
Source
The code follows a straightforward pattern. First, we load environment variables using load_dotenv(), which reads our API key from the .env file. Then we create a TavilyClient instance with that key. The search_web function itself is minimal: it takes a query string, calls the Tavily API's search() method, and returns the results. We default max_results to 2 to keep responses concise during development and reduce API costs.
清单3.12 使用Tavily的基本网络搜索功能
Source
Listing 3.12 Basic web search function using Tavily
代码保持原样
import os from tavily import TavilyClient from dotenv import load_dotenv load_dotenv() tavily_client = TavilyClient(os.getenv("TAVILY_API_KEY")) def search_web(query: str, max_results: int = 2) -> list: response = tavily_client.search(query, max_results=max_results) return response.get("results")
让我们尝试搜索基普乔格的马拉松纪录，以检查search_web功能是否有效。
每个结果都包含标题、URL、内容摘要和相关度分数。
第一个结果是他的维基百科页面，第二个是BBC的一篇文章。
从这些摘要中，我们可以看到他的官方马拉松最佳成绩是2:01:09（2022年柏林马拉松）。
我们的基础工具运行正常。
Source
Let’s try searching for Kipchoge’s marathon record to check if search_web works. Each result includes a title, URL, content snippet, and relevance score. The first result is his Wikipedia page, and the second is a BBC article. From these snippets, we can see his official marathon best time is 2:01:09 (Berlin 2022). Our basic tool works.
清单 3.13 测试网页搜索功能
Source
Listing 3.13 Testing the web search function
代码保持原样
search_web("Kipchoge's marathon world record")
输出如下：
Source
The output is as follows:
代码保持原样
[ { 'title': 'Eliud Kipchoge - Wikipedia', 'url': 'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eliud_Kipchoge', 'content': 'Eliud Kipchoge is a Kenyan long-distance runner who ➥competes in the marathon and formerly specialized in the 5000 metres. ➥Kipchoge is the 2016 and 2020 Olympic marathon champion, and was the ➥world record holder in the marathon from 2018 to 2023, until that ➥record was broken by Kelvin Kiptum at the 2023 Chicago Marathon. ➥Kipchoge has run 4 of the 10 fastest marathons in history... ➥Personal bests Marathon: 2:01:09 (Berlin 2022)...', 'score': 0.92125154, 'raw_content': None }, { 'title': 'Eliud Kipchoge breaks two-hour marathon mark by 20 seconds', 'url': 'https://www.bbc.co.uk/sport/athletics/50025543', 'content': 'Eliud Kipchoge has become the first athlete to run a ➥marathon in under two hours, beating the mark by 20 seconds. The ➥Olympic champion - who holds the official marathon world record of ➥2:01:39, set in Berlin, Germany in 2018 - missed out by 25 seconds ➥in a previous attempt at the Italian Grand Prix circuit at Monza in ➥2017...', 'score': 0.9014448, 'raw_content': None } ]
添加搜索选项
Source
Adding search options
我们的基础功能可以获取结果，但实际使用中往往需要更多控制。
考虑以下场景：用户只想获取某个主题的最新新闻文章，或者他们需要特定国家的结果，又或者他们希望进行更深入的研究并获得更多结果。
每个需求都需要额外的参数。
Source
Our basic function retrieves results, but real-world usage often demands more control. Consider these scenarios: a user wants only recent news articles about a topic, or they need results specifically from their country, or they want deeper research with more results. Each requirement needs additional parameters.
Tavily的API通过可选参数支持这些功能。
让我们扩展函数以暴露最常用的选项。
我们添加了四个新参数。
topic参数允许用户聚焦特定内容类型：“general”用于广泛的网络搜索，“news”用于近期文章，或“finance”用于金融信息。
time_range参数按时效性筛选结果，当用户需要最新信息而非历史内容时非常有用。
Source
Tavily's API supports these through optional arguments. Let's expand our function to expose the most commonly needed options. We've added four new parameters. The topic parameter lets users focus on specific content types: "general" for broad web search, "news" for recent articles, or "finance" for financial information. The time_range parameter filters results by recency, useful when users need current information rather than historical content.
清单3.14 带有附加选项的网络搜索函数
Source
Listing 3.14 Web search function with additional options
代码保持原样
def search_web( query: str, max_results: int = 2, topic: str = "general", time_range: str | None = None, country: str | None = None, ) -> list: response = tavily_client.search( query, max_results=max_results, topic=topic, time_range=time_range, country=country, ) return response.get("results")
但这只是触及了表面。
Tavily的API支持近20个参数，包括按特定域名筛选（包含或排除某些网站）、控制搜索深度（基础版与高级版）、在结果中包含图像、检索原始HTML内容等。
每个参数都需要理解其用途、有效值以及它如何与其他选项交互。
你暴露的参数越多，工具定义就越复杂，大型语言模型就越难正确使用。
Source
But this is just scratching the surface. Tavily's API supports nearly 20 parameters, including filtering by specific domains (including or excluding certain websites), controlling the depth of search (basic vs. advanced), including images in results, retrieving raw HTML content, and more. Each parameter requires understanding its purpose, valid values, and how it interacts with other options. The more parameters you expose, the more complex your tool definition becomes, and the harder it is for the LLM to use correctly.
优雅地处理错误
Source
Handling errors gracefully
到目前为止，我们一直假设一切运行完美。
但如果出现问题会怎样？
无效的API密钥会返回401身份验证错误。
超出月度使用限制会触发429速率限制错误。
网络问题会导致连接超时。
API可能返回格式错误的数据，或者服务可能暂时不可用。
Source
So far, we've assumed everything works perfectly. But what happens when things go wrong? An invalid API key returns a 401 authentication error. Exceeding your monthly usage limit triggers a 429 rate limit error. Network issues cause connection timeouts. The API might return malformed data, or the service could be temporarily unavailable.
一种极简方法会捕获所有异常并返回错误信息。
此实现将API调用包裹在try-except块中，并在出现任何问题时返回错误字符串。
返回类型现在为list | str，表示函数返回结果列表或错误信息字符串。
这种方法简单且能确保智能体在搜索失败时仍能继续运行。
Source
A minimal approach catches all exceptions and returns an error message. This implementation wraps the API call in a try-except block and returns an error string if anything goes wrong. The return type is now list | str, indicating the function returns either a list of results or an error message string. This approach is simple and ensures the agent can continue operating even when the search fails.
清单3.15 带错误处理的网络搜索函数
Source
Listing 3.15 Web search function with error handling
代码保持原样
def search_web( query: str, max_results: int = 5, topic: str = "general", time_range: str | None = None, ) -> list | str: try: response = tavily_client.search( query, max_results=max_results, topic=topic, time_range=time_range, ) return response.get("results") except Exception as e: return f"Error: Search failed - {e}"
然而，这种一刀切的方法将所有错误都同等对待。
在生产系统中，不同类型的错误通常需要不同的响应方式。
身份验证错误（401）可能表明存在需要人工关注的配置问题。
速率限制错误（429）可能适合采用带退避机制的自动重试。
超时错误可能适合使用更简单的查询进行重试。
网络错误可能需要与API错误不同的处理方式。
Source
However, this catch-all approach treats every error the same way. In production systems, different errors often require different responses. Authentication errors (401) might indicate a configuration problem that needs human attention. Rate limit errors (429) might benefit from automatic retry with backoff. Timeout errors might warrant a retry with a simpler query. Network errors might need different handling than API errors.
就我们的学习目的而言，这种简单的错误处理已经足够。
但当你为生产环境中的智能体构建工具时，很可能需要区分不同类型的错误，并对每种错误进行适当的处理。
健壮的错误处理的复杂性是工具开发的另一个维度，它超越了简单地调用API。
Source
For our learning purposes, this simple error handling suffices. But as you build tools for production agents, you'll likely need to distinguish between error types and handle each appropriately. The complexity of robust error handling is yet another dimension of tool development that goes beyond simply calling an API.
3.3.2 转换为工具定义
Source
3.3.2 Converting to tool definitions
到目前为止，我们已经创建了一个网络搜索工具。
在本章早些时候，我们还构建了一个用于执行计算的计算器函数。
为了让LLM能够使用这些工具，我们需要使用标准化的工具定义格式来定义它们。
Source
So far, we’ve created a web search tool. Earlier in this chapter, we also built a calculator function for performing computations. To make these tools accessible to an LLM, we need to define them using a standardized tool definition format.
由于我们编写的函数较为简单，手动将它们转换为工具定义不会花费太多时间。
然而，在开发过程中，函数可能会频繁变更或变得更加复杂，这使得手动更新容易出错且效率低下。
为了解决这个问题，我们可以创建并使用一个实用函数，自动将Python函数转换为工具定义。
Source
Since the functions we've written are simple, converting them into tool definitions manually won’t take much time. However, during development, functions may change frequently or grow more complex, making manual updates error-prone and inefficient. To address this, we can create and use a utility function that automatically converts a Python function into a tool definition.
要从函数生成工具定义，我们需要提取函数的名称、文档字符串和参数详细信息。
在Python中，这可以通过使用inspect模块来完成。
Source
To generate a tool definition from a function, we need to extract the function's name, docstring, and parameter details. In Python, this can be done using the inspect module.
为了说明这一过程，让我们考虑一个名为example_tool的示例函数。
该函数接受两个输入：input_1（一个字符串）和input_2（一个默认值为1的整数）。
Source
To illustrate the process, let’s consider a sample function called example_tool. This function takes two inputs: input_1, which is a string, and input_2, which is an integer with a default value of 1.
清单3.16 使用inspect提取工具元数据
Source
Listing 3.16 Extract tool metadata using inspect
代码保持原样
import inspect def example_tool(input_1:str, input_2:int=1): """docstring for example_tool""" return print(f"function name: {example_tool.__name__}") print(f"function docstring: {example_tool.__doc__}") print(f"function signature: {inspect.signature(example_tool)}")
输出如下：
Source
The output is as follows:
代码保持原样
function name: example_tool function docstring: docstring for example_tool function signature: (input_1: str, input_2: int = 1)
我们可以使用 __name__ 属性提取函数的名称，并使用 __doc__ 属性提取其描述。
参数类型及其是否为必需参数，可以通过 inspect.signature 来确定。
从输出中可以看出，input_1 是一个必需的字符串参数，而 input_2 是一个可选的整数参数，默认值为 1。
Source
We can extract the function’s name using the __name__ attribute and its description using the __doc__ attribute. The parameter types and whether they’re required can be determined using inspect.signature. From the output, we can see that input_1 is a required string, and input_2 is an optional integer with a default value of 1.
利用这些信息，我们可以如下实现一个实用函数。
Source
Using this information, we can implement a utility function as follows.
清单3.17 函数到工具模式转换器
Source
Listing 3.17 Function to tool schema converter
代码保持原样
def function_to_input_schema(func) -> dict: type_map = { str: "string", int: "integer", float: "number", bool: "boolean", list: "array", dict: "object", type(None): "null", } try: signature = inspect.signature(func) #A except ValueError as e: raise ValueError( f"Failed to get signature for function {func.__name__}: ➥{str(e)}" ) parameters = {} for param in signature.parameters.values(): try: param_type = type_map.get(param.annotation, "string") #B except KeyError as e: raise KeyError( f"Unknown type annotation {param.annotation} for parameter ➥{param.name}: {str(e)}" ) parameters[param.name] = {"type": param_type} #B required = [ param.name #C for param in signature.parameters.values() #C if param.default == inspect._empty #C ] return { "type": "object", "properties": parameters, "required": required, }
通过查看示例代码，我们可以看到如何使用inspect.signature来提取函数参数，并将其类型转换为适合工具定义的格式。
它会检查每个参数是否有默认值，以确定是否为必需参数，并将必需参数存储在一个列表中。
最后，它会按照标准工具定义格式组织所有信息。
Source
Looking at the example code, we can see how inspect.signature is used to extract function parameters and convert their types into the appropriate format for a tool definition. It checks whether each parameter has a default value to determine if it's required and stores the required arguments in a list. Finally, it organizes all the information according to the standard tool definition format.
为验证function_to_tool_definition实用工具是否正常工作，我们可以尝试转换我们的网络搜索工具。
Source
To verify that the function_to_tool_definition utility works correctly, we can try converting our web search tool.
清单 3.18 函数到工具模式转换器
Source
Listing 3.18 Function to tool schema converter
代码保持原样
def format_tool_definition(name: str, description: str, parameters: dict) -> dict: return { "type": "function", "function": { "name": name, "description": description, "parameters": parameters, }, } def function_to_tool_definition(func) -> dict: return format_tool_definition( func.__name__, func.__doc__ or "", function_to_input_schema(func) ) function_to_tool_definition(search_web) # {'type': 'function', 'function': {'name': 'search_web', # ➥'description': 'Search the web for the given query.', # ➥'parameters': {'type': 'object', 'properties': # ➥{'query': {'type': 'string'}}, 'required': ['query']}}}
生成的模式应包含函数名称和描述，以及参数类型和每个参数是否为必需项——正如预期的那样。
Source
The resulting schema should include the function name and description, along with parameter types and whether each is required—just as expected.
代码保持原样
search_tool_definition = function_to_tool_definition(search_web) print(search_tool_definition)
输出如下。
Source
The output is as follows.
代码保持原样
{'type': 'function', 'function': {'name': 'search_web', 'description': 'Search the web for the given query.', 'parameters': {'type': 'object', 'properties': {'query': {'type': 'string'}, 'max_results': {'type': 'integer'}, 'topic': {'type': 'string'}, 'time_range': {'type': 'string'}}, 'required': ['query']}}}
现在，我们可以利用这个工具将迄今为止创建的所有工具转换为模式，并准备解决我们的目标问题。
Source
Now we can convert all the tools we've created so far into schemas using this utility and prepare to solve our target problem.
3.3.3 端到端工具执行
Source
3.3.3 End-to-end tool execution
现在让我们把所有内容整合起来。
我们有一个可用的网络搜索功能，以及一个将其转换为工具定义的实用程序。
最后一步是构建执行基础设施，将LLM的工具调用连接到实际的函数执行。
Source
Now let's put everything together. We have a working web search function and a utility to convert it into a tool definition. The final piece is building the execution infrastructure that connects the LLM's tool calls to actual function execution.
我们需要两个组件：一个根据LLM输出执行工具的函数，以及一个管理LLM与工具之间对话的控制循环。
Source
We need two components: a function to execute tools based on LLM output, and a control loop that manages the conversation between the LLM and tools.
构建工具执行系统
Source
Building the tool execution system
首先，我们定义一个执行工具并返回其结果的实用函数。
该函数接收一个工具箱（将工具名称映射到函数的字典）和大语言模型的工具调用，然后使用提供的参数执行相应的函数。
该函数从大语言模型的响应中提取工具名称和参数，在工具箱中查找对应的函数，并使用解析后的参数调用该函数。
只要工具已在工具箱中注册，这种简单模式就适用于任何工具。
Source
First, we define a utility function that executes a tool and returns its result. This function takes a toolbox (a dictionary mapping tool names to functions) and a tool call from the LLM, then executes the appropriate function with the provided arguments. The function extracts the tool name and arguments from the LLM's response, looks up the corresponding function in the toolbox, and calls it with the parsed arguments. This simple pattern works for any tool as long as it's registered in the toolbox.
清单 3.19 工具执行实用函数
Source
Listing 3.19 Tool execution utility function
代码保持原样
def tool_execution(tool_box, tool_call): function_name = tool_call.function.name function_args = json.loads(tool_call.function.arguments) tool_result = tool_box[function_name](**function_args) return tool_result
接下来，我们构建一个控制循环来管理LLM与工具之间的交互。
该函数将用户的问题连同可用的工具定义一起发送给LLM。
如果LLM请求调用工具，我们就执行该调用并将结果反馈到上下文中。
这个循环会持续进行，直到LLM返回最终响应且不再请求任何工具。
Source
Next, we build a control loop to manage the interaction between the LLM and tools. This function sends the user's question to the LLM along with available tool definitions. If the LLM requests a tool call, we execute it and feed the result back into the context. This cycle continues until the LLM returns a final response without requesting any tools.
让我们来追踪这个循环中会发生什么：
Source
Let's trace through what happens in this loop:
LLM接收系统提示、用户问题以及可用工具定义。
Source
The LLM receives the system prompt, user question, and available tool definitions
如果LLM确定需要外部信息，它会生成一个工具调用。
Source
If the LLM determines it needs external information, it generates a tool call
我们将助手的消息（包含工具调用）附加到对话历史中
Source
We append the assistant's message (containing the tool call) to the conversation history
我们执行所请求的工具，并将结果作为“工具”消息附加
Source
We execute the requested tool and append the result as a "tool" message
循环持续进行，将更新后的对话发送回LLM
Source
The loop continues, sending the updated conversation back to the LLM
当LLM拥有足够的信息来回答时，它会直接返回响应而不调用工具，然后我们退出循环。
Source
When the LLM has enough information to answer, it returns a response without tool calls, and we exit the loop
清单3.20 用于工具执行的简单代理循环
Source
Listing 3.20 Simple agent loop for tool execution
代码保持原样
from litellm import completion def simple_agent_loop(system_prompt, question): tools = [search_web] tool_box = {tool.__name__: tool for tool in tools} tool_definitions = [function_to_tool_definition(tool) for tool in tools] messages = [ {"role": "system", "content": system_prompt}, {"role": "user", "content": question} ] while True: response = completion( model="gpt-5-mini", messages=messages, tools=tool_definitions ) assistant_message = response.choices[0].message if assistant_message.tool_calls: messages.append(assistant_message) for tool_call in assistant_message.tool_calls: tool_result = tool_execution(tool_box, tool_call) messages.append({ "role": "tool", "content": str(tool_result), "tool_call_id": tool_call.id }) else: return assistant_message.content
测试代理循环
Source
Testing the agent loop
让我们用一个需要当前信息的问题来测试我们的系统。
Source
Let's test our system with a question that requires current information.
清单 3.21 测试代理循环
Source
Listing 3.21 Testing the agent loop
代码保持原样
system_prompt = """You are a helpful assistant. Use the search tool when you need current information.""" result = simple_agent_loop( system_prompt, "Who won the 2025 Nobel Prize in Physics?" ) print(result)
输出如下。
Source
The output is as follows.
代码保持原样
The 2025 Nobel Prize in Physics was awarded jointly to John Clarke, Michel H. Devoret, and John M. Martinis. They were recognized for experiments demonstrating macroscopic quantum tunnelling and energy quantisation in electric circuits — work underpinning superconducting quantum technologies (announced Oct. 7, 2025)
当LLM识别到需要其训练数据中未包含的最新信息时，它会调用search_web工具并传入适当的查询，接收搜索结果，并综合生成最终答案。
如果没有工具，LLM将不得不承认自己不知道相关信息，或者冒着提供过时信息的风险。
Source
The LLM recognizes it needs current information that isn't in its training data, calls the search_web tool with an appropriate query, receives the search results, and synthesizes a final answer. Without the tool, the LLM would have to admit it doesn't know or risk providing outdated information.
3.3.4 自定义工具的挑战
Source
3.3.4 The challenges of custom tools
构建第3.3.1节中的网络搜索工具是直截了当的。
我们安装了Tavily客户端，编写了一个简单函数，并将其转换为工具定义。
整个过程只花了几分钟。
然而，这种简单性具有欺骗性。
随着你开发更多工具并扩展到实际项目中，一些挑战会浮现出来，使得定制工具开发出人意料地困难。
Source
Building the web search tool in section 3.3.1 was straightforward. We installed the Tavily client, wrote a simple function, and converted it to a tool definition. The entire process took just a few minutes. However, this simplicity is deceptive. As you develop more tools and scale to real-world projects, several challenges emerge that make custom tool development surprisingly difficult.
理解陌生的API
Source
Understanding unfamiliar APIs
Tavily是专门为LLM应用设计的，这使得集成变得容易。
其API简单，响应格式已针对RAG优化，且文档简洁明了。
但大多数你想要集成的服务在设计时并未考虑LLM。
Source
Tavily was designed specifically for LLM applications, which made integration easy. The API is simple, the response format is already optimized for RAG, and the documentation is concise. But most services you want to integrate are not built with LLMs in mind.
试想构建一个工具来搜索公司的Slack工作区、从Google Drive检索文件或查询Salesforce数据库。
每项服务都有其独特的API约定、速率限制策略、分页模式和响应格式。
在编写任何代码之前，您需要花费数小时阅读文档、理解数据模型，并弄清楚如何将响应转换为对LLM有用的内容。
这种前期投入会随着您需要构建的每个新工具而成倍增加。
Source
Consider building a tool that searches your company's Slack workspace, retrieves files from Google Drive, or queries a Salesforce database. Each service has its own API conventions, rate limiting policies, pagination patterns, and response formats. Before writing any code, you need to spend hours reading documentation, understanding the data models, and figuring out how to transform responses into something useful for an LLM. This upfront investment multiplies with every new tool you need to build.
稳健地处理错误
Source
Handling errors robustly
回顾一下我们的search_web函数。
它的错误处理能力非常有限。
在生产环境中，这将是远远不够的。
现实世界中的工具必须优雅地处理网络超时，通过适当的退避策略管理API速率限制，应对服务中断，在发起请求前验证输入，并提供有意义的错误信息，帮助LLM（最终是用户）理解问题所在。
Source
Look back at our search_web function. It has minimal error handling. In a production environment, this would be inadequate. Real-world tools must handle network timeouts gracefully, manage API rate limits with appropriate backoff strategies, deal with service outages, validate inputs before making requests, and provide meaningful error messages that help the LLM (and ultimately the user) understand what went wrong.
实现健壮的错误处理通常比核心功能本身需要更多的代码。
一个简单的网页搜索功能可能只需10行代码，但一个生产就绪的版本，包含完善的错误处理、重试机制和日志记录，则可能轻松达到50行甚至更多。
Source
Implementing robust error handling often requires more code than the core functionality itself. A simple web search function might be 10 lines, but a production-ready version with proper error handling, retries, and logging could easily be 50 lines or more.
团队间重复劳动
Source
Duplicated efforts across teams
在任何构建AI智能体的组织中，多个团队往往需要类似的能力。
营销团队希望为其内容生成智能体配备网络搜索工具。
客户支持团队需要为其FAQ机器人配备网络搜索功能。
研究团队的分析流程也需要这一功能。
Source
In any organization building AI agents, multiple teams often need similar capabilities. The marketing team wants a web search tool for their content generation agent. The customer support team needs a web search for their FAQ bot. The research team requires it for their analysis pipeline.
由于缺乏标准化的工具共享方式，每个团队都构建自己的实现。
它们各自独立解决相同问题，犯类似错误，并维护独立的代码库。
从组织角度来看，这种重复浪费了大量工程资源。
同一工具在公司内部可能存在三到四个略有差异的版本。
Source
Without a standard way to share tools, each team builds its own implementation. They solve the same problems independently, make similar mistakes, and maintain separate codebases. From an organizational perspective, this duplication wastes significant engineering resources. The same tool might exist in three or four slightly different versions across the company.
代码复用比看起来要困难得多。
Source
Code reuse is harder than it looks
你可能会认为解决方案很简单：一个团队构建工具，其他团队复用。
在实践中，这很少能顺利运作。
不同团队对其工具定义的结构方式各不相同。
有些使用字典，有些则使用Pydantic模型。
执行模式在同步和异步实现之间有所不同。
返回格式不一致。
文档质量差异巨大。
Source
You might think the solution is simple: one team builds the tool, others reuse it. In practice, this rarely works smoothly. Different teams structure their tool definitions differently. Some use dictionaries, others use Pydantic models. Execution patterns vary between synchronous and asynchronous implementations. Return formats are inconsistent. Documentation quality differs dramatically.
当你尝试采用另一个团队的工具时，你往往需要花费比从头开始构建更多的时间来使其适应你的代码库。
依赖项会发生冲突，接口不匹配，代码中嵌入的假设也不适用于你的使用场景。
集成过程中的摩擦往往超过了重用的好处。
Source
When you try to adopt a tool from another team, you often spend more time adapting it to your codebase than you would have spent building it from scratch. Dependencies conflict, interfaces do not match, and assumptions embedded in the code do not apply to your use case. The friction of integration often outweighs the benefit of reuse.
持续的维护负担
Source
Ongoing maintenance burden
构建工具不是一劳永逸的事情。
API会不断演进，你的工具也必须随之演进。
服务会弃用端点、改变响应格式，并引入新的必需参数。
依赖项中的安全漏洞需要更新。
用户会请求新功能，并报告你未曾预料到的边缘情况。
Source
Building a tool is not a one-time effort. APIs evolve, and your tools must evolve with them. Services deprecate endpoints, change response formats, and introduce new required parameters. Security vulnerabilities in dependencies require updates. Users request new features and report edge cases you did not anticipate.
当你维护一两个工具时，这是可以管理的。
但智能体通常需要许多工具：网络搜索、文件操作、数据库查询、电子邮件、日历以及特定领域的集成。
每个工具都成为一项维护责任。
随着工具集合的增长，累积的维护负担会变得相当可观。
Source
When you maintain one or two tools, this is manageable. But agents typically need many tools: web search, file operations, database queries, email, calendar, and domain-specific integrations. Each tool becomes a maintenance responsibility. As your tool collection grows, the cumulative maintenance burden becomes substantial.
标准化的必要性
Source
The need for standardization
这些挑战并非LLM工具所独有。
软件行业此前已通过标准化解决了类似问题。
REST API 标准化了网络服务之间的通信方式。
包管理器标准化了代码的共享与版本管理方式。
容器化技术标准化了应用程序的部署方式。
Source
These challenges are not unique to LLM tools. The software industry has solved similar problems before through standardization. REST APIs standardized how web services communicate. Package managers standardized how code is shared and versioned. Containerization standardized how applications are deployed.
LLM工具生态系统需要类似的标准化：一种通用的方式来定义工具、跨项目共享它们，并且无论使用哪个LLM提供商都能集成它们。
这正是模型上下文协议（MCP）所提供的。
Source
The LLM tool ecosystem needs similar standardization: a common way to define tools, share them across projects, and integrate them regardless of which LLM provider you use. This is exactly what MCP, the Model Context Protocol, provides.
3.4 MCP：标准化工具
Source
3.4 MCP: Standardizing tools
正如我们在3.3节亲身经历的那样，开发可供LLM智能体使用的工具非常耗时，而且实现过程中的不一致性使得这些工具难以复用。
Source
As we experienced firsthand in section 3.3, developing tools that LLM agents can use is time-consuming, and inconsistencies in implementation make them difficult to reuse.
2024年11月，Anthropic推出了MCP（模型上下文协议），旨在为LLM工具集成领域带来类似的变革。
如果说API为开发者与服务之间的通信建立了一种通用语言，那么MCP则为LLM智能体与工具之间的通信建立了一种通用语言。
正如您可以使用相同的HTTP模式调用任何REST API一样，兼容MCP的智能体也可以使用任何兼容MCP的工具，而无需编写自定义集成代码。
Source
In November 2024, Anthropic introduced MCP (Model Context Protocol) to bring a similar transformation to the world of LLM tool integration. If APIs established a common language for developers to communicate with services, MCP establishes a common language for LLM agents to communicate with tools. Just as you can call any REST API using the same HTTP patterns, an MCP-compatible agent can use any MCP-compatible tool without custom integration code.
自发布以来，MCP在2025年初获得了越来越多的关注。
这为开发者打开了大门，使他们能够使用由公司或社区构建的工具，而无需从头开始构建所有工具。
如图3.4所示，借助MCP，智能体可以轻松集成来自Google Drive、Slack、Tavily、Brave Search、GitHub和Figma等服务的工具，而无需编写自定义工具包装器。
Source
Since its release, MCP has gained growing attention throughout early 2025. It opened the door for developers to use tools built by companies or communities without having to build them all from scratch. As shown in figure 3.4, with MCP, agents can easily integrate tools from services like Google Drive, Slack, Tavily, Brave Search, GitHub, and Figma without needing to write custom tool wrappers.
图3.4：MCP通过集成第三方工具，轻松扩展智能体的工具集。
Source
Figure 3.4 MCP makes it easy to extend an agent’s toolset by integrating third-party tools.
3.4.1 MCP的核心：服务器-客户端架构
Source
3.4.1 The core of MCP: server–client architecture
MCP的核心在于通过三组件架构——主机、客户端和服务器——将智能体的“大脑”与其“四肢”（即工具）分离开来。
Source
At its core, MCP separates the "brain" of the agent from its "arms and legs" (tools) through a three-component architecture: Host, Client, and Server.
理解这三个组成部分
Source
Understanding the three components
图3.5展示了这些组件如何协同工作。
我们来明确一下每个角色的作用：
Source
Figure 3.5 illustrates how these components work together. Let's clarify each role:
主机是负责与用户交互、利用大语言模型进行决策的应用程序。
它接收用户输入，进行推理，并决定何时使用哪些工具。
可以把它想象成系统的“大脑”。
例如Claude Desktop、集成AI功能的IDE，或者你正在构建的智能体应用。
Source
The Host is the application that interacts with users and makes decisions using an LLM. It receives user input, performs reasoning, and decides which tools to use and when. Think of it as the "brain" of the system. Examples include Claude Desktop, an IDE with AI features, or the agent application you're building.
MCP客户端充当主机与MCP服务器之间的桥梁。
当主机决定需要某个工具时，客户端负责处理通信：向服务器请求可用的工具定义，并转发工具执行请求。
每个客户端维持与一个MCP服务器的连接。
Source
The MCP Client acts as a bridge between the Host and MCP Servers. When the Host decides it needs a tool, the Client handles the communication: requesting available tool definitions from servers and forwarding tool execution requests. Each Client maintains a connection to one MCP Server.
MCP服务器托管实际工具，并按需执行它们。
它响应两种类型的请求："你有什么工具？"（返回工具定义）和"用这些参数执行这个工具"（运行工具并返回结果）。
服务器可以连接到外部服务，如数据库、API。
Source
The MCP Server hosts the actual tools and executes them on demand. It responds to two types of requests: "what tools do you have?" (returning tool definitions) and "execute this tool with these arguments" (running the tool and returning results). Servers can connect to external services like databases, APIs.
图3.5 MCP服务器-客户端架构。主机包含用于推理和用户交互的LLM，通过MCP客户端连接，后者管理服务器通信。MCP服务器公开工具定义并处理执行，可选择与数据库和API等外部服务集成。
Source
Figure 3.5 MCP server-client architecture. The Host contains the LLM for reasoning and user interaction, connecting through MCP Clients that manage server communication. MCP Servers expose tool definitions and handle execution, optionally integrating with external services like databases and APIs.
MCP的范畴不仅限于工具
Source
MCP's scope beyond tools
实际上，MCP定义了服务器可提供的三种能力类型：工具（大语言模型可调用的函数）、提示（可复用的提示模板）和资源（大语言模型可访问的数据）。
在本书中，我们专注于工具，因为它们是构建智能体最核心的能力。
Source
MCP actually defines three types of capabilities that servers can provide: tools (functions the LLM can call), prompts (reusable prompt templates), and resources (data the LLM can access). In this book, we focus exclusively on tools since they're the most essential capability for building agents.
两个标准化接口
Source
Two standardized interfaces
无论使用哪种传输方式，MCP都标准化了两个关键接口：
Source
Regardless of which transport you use, MCP standardizes two key interfaces:
工具发现：在第3.3节中，我们为每个工具手动定义了模式。
通过MCP，客户端可以请求可用的工具定义，服务器会以标准化格式返回这些定义。
工具开发者只需实现一次模式定义，任何兼容MCP的客户端都能自动检索并使用它。
Source
Tool Discovery: In section 3.3, we manually defined schemas for each tool. With MCP, the client can request available tool definitions, and the server returns them in a standardized format. Tool developers implement the schema once; any MCP-compatible client can automatically retrieve and use it.
工具执行：此前，我们自行构建了tool_execution函数，以桥接LLM输出与实际函数调用。
MCP也对此进行了标准化。
客户端向服务器发送工具执行请求，服务器处理执行并以一致的格式返回结果。
Source
Tool Execution: Previously, we built our own tool_execution function to bridge LLM output and actual function calls. MCP standardizes this too. The client sends a tool execution request to the server, which handles execution and returns the result in a consistent format.
传输机制
Source
Transport mechanisms
MCP支持三种传输机制，用于客户端与服务器之间的通信：
Source
MCP supports three transport mechanisms for communication between clients and servers:
stdio（标准输入/输出）是最简单的方法，客户端将服务器作为子进程启动，并通过标准输入/输出流进行通信。
由于所有操作都在同一台机器上本地运行，因此没有网络开销。
这对于本地开发非常理想，也适用于无需跨机器共享工具的场景。
Source
stdio (Standard I/O) is the simplest approach, where the client launches the server as a subprocess and communicates through standard input/output streams. Since everything runs locally on the same machine, there's no network overhead. This is ideal for local development, and when tools don't need to be shared across machines.
HTTP支持通过网络进行远程通信。
客户端通过HTTP发送请求，服务器则流式返回响应。
当服务器需要在不同的机器上运行或需要被多个客户端共享时，这种方式效果很好。
Source
HTTP enables remote communication over the network. The client sends requests via HTTP, and the server streams responses back. This works well when servers need to run on separate machines or be shared across multiple clients.
WebSocket 提供完全的双向通信，允许客户端和服务器都能主动发送消息。
这在服务器需要主动向客户端推送更新时非常有用。
Source
WebSocket provides full bidirectional communication, allowing both client and server to initiate messages. This is useful when servers need to push updates to clients proactively.
在本章中，我们将使用stdio传输方式，因为它设置最简单，足以学习MCP概念。
当您在生产环境中需要远程或共享工具服务器时，可以切换到HTTP或WebSocket，而无需更改工具实现。
Source
Throughout this chapter, we'll use the stdio transport since it's the simplest to set up and sufficient for learning MCP concepts. When you need remote or shared tool servers in production, you can switch to HTTP or WebSocket without changing your tool implementations.
3.4.2 动手实践：运行MCP服务器
Source
3.4.2 Hands-on: Running an MCP server
在深入探讨实现细节之前，让我们通过运行一个现有的服务器来亲身体验MCP。
我们将使用官方的Tavily MCP服务器，它提供了我们在第3.3节中手动构建的相同网络搜索能力，但已打包成一个可直接使用的MCP服务器。
Source
Before diving into implementation details, let's experience MCP firsthand by running an existing server. We'll use the official Tavily MCP server, which provides the same web search capability we built manually in section 3.3, but packaged as a ready-to-use MCP server.
生态系统中的MCP服务器通常以npm包的形式分发，并使用npx运行。
如果您尚未安装Node.js，则需要先安装它。
对于macOS和Windows，只需从https://nodejs.org/下载适用于您操作系统的安装程序，然后按照安装步骤操作即可。
Source
MCP servers in the ecosystem are typically distributed as npm packages and run using npx. If you don't have Node.js installed, you'll need to install it first. For both macOS and Windows, simply download the installer for your operating system from https://nodejs.org/ and follow the installation steps.
通过检查版本号来验证您的安装。
Source
Verify your installation by checking the version.
代码保持原样
node --version
如果显示了Node版本，则安装成功。
Source
If the Node version is displayed, the installation was successful.
运行Tavily MCP服务器
Source
Running the Tavily MCP server
安装Node.js后，我们可以通过一条命令启动Tavily MCP服务器。
首先，将你的Tavily API密钥设置为环境变量。
Source
With Node.js installed, we can launch the Tavily MCP server using a single command. First, set your Tavily API key as an environment variable.
代码保持原样
export TAVILY_API_KEY=<your tavily api key>
现在启动服务器，使用MCP Inspector——一个基于浏览器的工具，用于测试MCP服务器。
Source
Now launch the server with the MCP Inspector, a browser-based tool for testing MCP servers.
代码保持原样
npx @modelcontextprotocol/inspector npx -y tavily-mcp@latest
此命令一次性完成多项操作。
`npx` 命令无需全局安装即可运行 npm 包。
`@modelcontextprotocol/inspector` 包提供了一个用于与 MCP 服务器交互的 Web 界面。
`-y` 标志会自动确认所有提示。
最后，`tavily-mcp@latest` 是官方的 Tavily MCP 服务器包。
Source
This command does several things at once. The `npx` command runs npm packages without installing them globally. The `@modelcontextprotocol/inspector` package provides a web interface for interacting with MCP servers. The `-y` flag automatically confirms any prompts. Finally, `tavily-mcp@latest` is the official Tavily MCP server package.
图3.6 MCP检查器启动日志，显示服务器初始化和连接URL。

如果URL中包含会话令牌，您无需额外配置即可连接。
