相比之下，在第3.3节中，我们花费了大量精力才实现了基本的搜索功能。
Tavily MCP服务器包含多种工具、稳健的错误处理和优化的响应格式，所有这些都无需编写任何代码即可直接使用。
Source
Compare this to Section 3.3, where we spent considerable effort implementing just the basic search functionality. The Tavily MCP server includes multiple tools, robust error handling, and optimized response formatting, all ready to use without writing any code.
这就是标准化的力量。
工具开发者则可以专注于构建可靠、功能丰富的服务器。
代理开发者可以专注于推理和编排，因为他们知道任何兼容MCP的工具都能与他们的系统协同工作。
Source
This is the power of standardization. Tool developers can focus on building reliable, feature-rich servers. Agent developers can focus on reasoning and orchestration, knowing that any MCP-compatible tool will work with their system.
在下一节中，我们将探讨这一架构的另一面：如何构建一个MCP客户端，使其能够在我们的智能体中通过编程方式发现并使用这些工具。
Source
In the next section, we'll look at the other side of this architecture: how to build an MCP client that can discover and use these tools programmatically within our agent.
3.4.3 理解MCP客户端
Source
3.4.3 Understanding the MCP client
在上一节中，我们通过 Inspector 的 Web 界面与 Tavily MCP 服务器进行了交互。
虽然这对测试很有帮助，但我们的智能体需要以编程方式与 MCP 服务器交互。
这正是 MCP 客户端发挥作用的地方。
Source
In the previous section, we interacted with the Tavily MCP server through the Inspector's web interface. While helpful for testing, our agent needs to interact with MCP servers programmatically. This is where the MCP client comes in.
MCP客户端是您的智能体用来发现和调用MCP服务器中工具的核心组件。
它处理协议细节：建立连接、请求工具定义、执行工具和解析结果。
理解客户端的工作原理对于将MCP工具集成到您自己的智能体中至关重要。
Source
The MCP client is what your agent uses to discover and invoke tools from MCP servers. It handles the protocol details: establishing connections, requesting tool definitions, executing tools, and parsing results. Understanding how the client works is essential for integrating MCP tools into your own agents.
安装MCP Python SDK以进行动手实践。
Source
Install the MCP Python SDK for hands-on practice.
代码保持原样
uv add mcp
连接到MCP服务器
Source
Connecting to an MCP server
让我们编写一个简单的客户端，连接到Tavily MCP服务器，列出可用工具，并执行搜索。
Source
Let's write a simple client that connects to the Tavily MCP server, lists available tools, and performs a search.
让我们来逐步分析这段代码的执行过程：
Source
Let's trace through what happens in this code:
StdioServerParameters 指定了如何启动服务器。
该命令使用 npx，它可以在不全局安装的情况下运行 npm 包。
参数包括 -y 用于自动确认提示，以及 tavily-mcp@latest 以使用最新版本。
环境变量用于传递 API 密钥和系统 PATH。
Source
StdioServerParameters specifies how to launch the server. The command is npx, which runs npm packages without installing them globally. The args include -y to automatically confirm prompts and tavily-mcp@latest to use the latest version. Environment variables pass the API key and system PATH.
stdio_client 将服务器作为子进程启动。
async with 确保我们在完成后能正确清理资源。
它返回读写流，供会话用于通信。
Source
stdio_client launches the server as a subprocess. The async with ensures proper cleanup when we're done. It returns read and write streams that the session uses for communication.
ClientSession提供了高级API。
调用initialize()后，我们可以使用标准方法（如list_tools()和call_tool()）与服务器交互。
Source
ClientSession provides the high-level API. After calling initialize(), we can interact with the server using standard methods like list_tools() and call_tool().
session.list_tools() 向服务器请求所有可用的工具。
服务器返回工具定义，包括名称、描述和参数模式。
Source
session.list_tools() requests all available tools from the server. The server returns tool definitions including names, descriptions, and parameter schemas.
session.call_tool()执行特定工具。
我们传递工具名称和参数字典。
服务器运行该工具并返回结果。
Source
session.call_tool() executes a specific tool. We pass the tool name and a dictionary of arguments. The server runs the tool and returns the result.
清单 3.22 连接到 MCP 服务器
Source
Listing 3.22 Connecting to an MCP server
代码保持原样
import asyncio import os from mcp import ClientSession, StdioServerParameters from mcp.client.stdio import stdio_client from dotenv import load_dotenv load_dotenv() server_params = StdioServerParameters( command="npx", args=["-y", "tavily-mcp@latest"], env={ "TAVILY_API_KEY": os.getenv("TAVILY_API_KEY"), } ) async with stdio_client(server_params) as (read_stream, write_stream): async with ClientSession(read_stream, write_stream) as session: await session.initialize() # List available tools tools_result = await session.list_tools() print("Available tools:") for tool in tools_result.tools: print(f" - {tool.name}: {tool.description[:60]}...") result = await session.call_tool( "tavily-search", arguments={"query": "2025 Nobel Physics"} ) print("Search Result:") print(result.content)
运行此代码会产生类似的输出
Source
Running this code produces output similar to
代码保持原样
Available tools: - tavily-search: A powerful web search tool that provides comprehensive, real... - tavily-extract: A powerful web content extraction tool that retrieves and pr... - tavily-crawl: A powerful web crawler that initiates a structured web crawl... - tavily-map: A powerful web mapping tool that creates a structured map of... Search Result: [TextContent(type='text', text='Detailed Results:\n\nTitle: Press release: Nobel Prize in Physics 2025...
将MCP工具转换为供LLM使用
Source
Converting MCP tools for LLM use
list_tools()返回的工具使用的是MCP的架构格式。
要让LLM使用这些工具，我们需要将它们转换为LLM提供商所期望的格式。
Source
The tools returned by list_tools() use MCP's schema format. To use these tools with LLMs, we need to convert them to whatever format the LLM provider expects.
幸运的是，我们已在第3.3.2节中为此奠定了基础。
我们创建的format_tool_definition函数接收名称、描述和参数字典，并返回一个结构正确的OpenAI工具定义。
MCP工具对象通过其名称、描述和inputSchema属性，恰好提供这三部分信息。
这使得转换过程变得直接明了。
Source
Fortunately, we already built the foundation for this in Section 3.3.2. The format_tool_definition function we created takes a name, description, and parameters dictionary, and returns a properly structured OpenAI tool definition. MCP tool objects provide exactly these three pieces of information through their name, description, and inputSchema attributes. This makes the conversion straightforward.
清单3.23 将MCP工具转换为OpenAI格式
Source
Listing 3.23 Converting MCP tools to OpenAI format
代码保持原样
def mcp_tools_to_openai_format(mcp_tools) -> list[dict]: """Convert MCP tool definitions to OpenAI tool format.""" return [ format_tool_definition( name=tool.name, description=tool.description, parameters=tool.inputSchema, ) for tool in mcp_tools.tools ]
通过这个转换函数，我们可以从任何MCP服务器检索工具，并立即在OpenAI的API中使用它们。
以下是它在实践中的运作方式。
Source
With this conversion function, we can retrieve tools from any MCP server and immediately use them with OpenAI's API. Here's how it works in practice.
清单3.24 以OpenAI格式检索工具
Source
Listing 3.24 Retrieving tools in OpenAI format
代码保持原样
async with stdio_client(server_params) as (read_stream, write_stream): async with ClientSession(read_stream, write_stream) as session: await session.initialize() # List available tools tools_result = await session.list_tools() openai_format_tools = mcp_tools_to_openai_format(tools_result) for tool in openai_format_tools: print(tool)
3.4.4 动手实践：实现一个MCP服务器
Source
3.4.4 Hands-on: Implementing an MCP server
到目前为止，我们使用的都是他人构建的外部MCP服务器。
虽然仅使用社区提供的服务器也能构建有效的智能体，但掌握如何创建自己的服务器能让你更有信心地驾驭MCP生态系统。
你将能确切了解底层运作机制，从而更轻松地调试问题、扩展现有服务器，或为特定需求构建自定义工具。
Source
So far, we've used external MCP servers built by others. While you can build effective agents using only community-provided servers, understanding how to create your own server gives you the confidence to navigate the MCP ecosystem. You'll know exactly what's happening under the hood, making it easier to debug issues, extend existing servers, or build custom tools for your specific needs.
好消息是，构建MCP服务器出奇地简单。
使用FastMCP库，只需添加一个装饰器，就能将现有的Python函数转换为MCP兼容的工具。
让我们将3.3节中构建的search_web函数转化为一个功能完整的MCP服务器。
Source
The good news is that building an MCP server is surprisingly simple. Using the FastMCP library, you can convert an existing Python function into an MCP-compatible tool by adding just a decorator. Let's transform the search_web function we built in section 3.3 into a fully functional MCP server.
构建服务器
Source
Building the server
首先，我们来安装所需的库。
Source
Let’s start by installing the required libraries.
代码保持原样
uv add fastmcp
现在，创建一个名为 tavily_mcp_server.py 的新文件。
我们将把现有的 search_web 函数包装到 MCP 基础设施中。
FastMCP 实例创建我们的服务器，并为其指定一个名称，以便客户端识别。
@mcp.tool() 装饰器将我们的函数注册为 MCP 工具。
FastMCP 会自动提取函数名称、参数和类型提示，以生成工具模式。
文档字符串成为工具的描述，帮助 LLM 理解何时以及如何使用该工具。
最后，mcp.run(transport='stdio') 启动服务器，使用标准输入/输出进行通信。
Source
Now, create a new file called tavily_mcp_server.py. We'll take our existing search_web function and wrap it with the MCP infrastructure. The FastMCP instance creates our server with a name that identifies it to clients. The @mcp.tool() decorator registers our function as an MCP tool. FastMCP automatically extracts the function name, parameters, and type hints to generate the tool schema. The docstring becomes the tool's description, which helps LLMs understand when and how to use the tool. Finally, mcp.run(transport='stdio') starts the server using standard input/output for communication.
清单 3.25 自定义 Tavily MCP 服务器实现
Source
Listing 3.25 Custom Tavily MCP server implementation
代码保持原样
import os from tavily import TavilyClient from dotenv import load_dotenv from mcp.server.fastmcp import FastMCP load_dotenv() tavily_client = TavilyClient(os.getenv("TAVILY_API_KEY")) mcp = FastMCP("custom-tavily-search") @mcp.tool() def search_web(query: str, max_results: int = 5) -> str: """ Search the web using Tavily API. Args: query: Search query string max_results: Maximum number of results to return (default: 5) Returns: Search results as formatted string """ try: response = tavily_client.search( query, max_results=max_results, ) results = response.get("results", []) return "\n\n".join( f"Title: {r['title']}\nURL: {r['url']}\nContent: {r['content']}" for r in results ) except Exception as e: return f"Error searching web: {str(e)}" if __name__ == "__main__": mcp.run(transport='stdio')
请注意，我们在原始函数中添加的代码非常少。
核心逻辑保持不变；我们只是用MCP基础设施对其进行了封装。
Source
Notice how little code we added to our original function. The core logic remains unchanged; we simply wrapped it with the MCP infrastructure.
与客户建立联系
Source
Connecting with the client
现在，让我们通过使用3.4.3节中学到的客户端代码连接到服务器，来验证我们的服务器是否正常工作。
唯一需要做的更改是更新StdioServerParameters，使其指向我们的自定义服务器，而非官方的Tavily包。
Source
Now let's verify our server works by connecting to it with the client code we learned in section 3.4.3. The only change we need is updating StdioServerParameters to point to our custom server instead of the official Tavily package.
清单 3.26 连接到自定义 MCP 服务器
Source
Listing 3.26 Connecting to the custom MCP server
代码保持原样
server_params = StdioServerParameters( command="uv", args=["run", "tavily_mcp_server.py"], env={ "TAVILY_API_KEY": os.getenv("TAVILY_API_KEY"), } ) async with stdio_client(server_params) as (read_stream, write_stream): async with ClientSession(read_stream, write_stream) as session: await session.initialize() # List available tools tools_result = await session.list_tools() print("Available tools:") for tool in tools_result.tools: print(f" - {tool.name}: {tool.description}")
运行此代码会产生类似输出
Source
Running this code produces output like
代码保持原样
Available tools: - search_web: Search the web using Tavily API. Args: query: Search query string max_results: Maximum number of results to return (default: 5) Returns: Search results as formatted string
将此与第3.4.2节进行比较，其中官方Tavily服务器公开了四个工具（tavily-search、tavily-extract、tavily-crawl、tavily-map）。
我们的自定义服务器仅公开一个工具：search_web。
然而，客户端代码几乎完全相同。
这就是标准化的力量：无论你是连接到复杂的官方服务器还是简单的自定义服务器，客户端接口都保持不变。
Source
Compare this to Section 3.4.2, where the official Tavily server exposed four tools (tavily-search, tavily-extract, tavily-crawl, tavily-map). Our custom server exposes just one tool: search_web. Yet the client code is nearly identical. This is the power of standardization: whether you're connecting to a sophisticated official server or a simple custom one, the client interface remains the same.
我们取得的成就
Source
What we accomplished
在本节中，我们完成了完整的MCP循环：
Source
In this section, we completed the full MCP cycle:
我们以最小的改动将自定义的search_web函数转换成了一个MCP服务器。
Source
We converted our custom search_web function into an MCP server with minimal changes
我们使用与连接官方Tavily服务器相同的客户端模式连接到我们的服务器。
Source
We connected to our server using the same client patterns we used for the official Tavily server
我们已验证工具发现与执行功能运行正常。
Source
We verified that tool discovery and execution work correctly
这体现了MCP的核心价值主张：工具的实现与使用完全解耦。
服务器开发者专注于构建可靠的工具。
智能体开发者专注于推理与编排。
协议则处理两者之间的一切。
Source
This demonstrates the core value proposition of MCP: tool implementation and tool usage are completely decoupled. Server developers focus on building reliable tools. Agent developers focus on reasoning and orchestration. The protocol handles everything in between.
理解了工具和MCP后，我们就拥有了构建完整智能体所需的所有基础组件。
在第四章中，我们将把这些能力整合成一个稳健的智能体框架，实现恰当的工具抽象、错误处理以及迭代推理循环，从而将具备工具使用能力的LLM转化为真正的智能体。
Source
With tools and MCP understood, we have all the building blocks needed for a complete agent. In chapter 4, we'll combine these capabilities into a robust agent framework, implementing proper tool abstraction, error handling, and the iterative reasoning loop that transforms an LLM with tools into a true agent.
3.5 总结
Source
3.5 Summary
工具扩展了大型语言模型的能力，使其能够访问API、执行计算并检索外部信息。
工具可分为三类：信息增强型、行动执行型和领域专用型。
Source
Tools extend LLM capabilities, enabling them to access APIs, perform calculations, and retrieve external information. Tools fall into three categories: information-augmenting, action-executing, and domain-specialized.
工具调用是LLM生成结构化输出的机制，该输出指定使用哪个工具及其参数。
LLM充当用户请求与可用工具之间的中介，但自身并不执行工具。
Source
Tool calling is the mechanism which LLMs generate structured outputs specifying which tool to use and with what parameters. The LLM acts as a mediator between user requests and available tools, but does not execute tools itself.
工具执行由外部系统处理。
LLM生成规范，由独立系统执行，执行结果反馈给LLM的上下文，供进一步推理使用。
Source
Tool execution is handled externally. The LLM generates specifications that a separate system executes, with results fed back into the LLM's context for further reasoning.
工具定义是结构化模式，用于描述可用工具、其参数及预期输出。
清晰明确的定义对于LLM可靠选择工具至关重要。
Source
Tool definitions are structured schemas that describe available tools, their parameters, and expected outputs. Clear and explicit definitions are essential for reliable tool selection by the LLM.
构建自定义工具涉及实现工具功能、创建工具定义以及构建执行基础设施。
虽然对于简单情况而言较为直接，但随着项目规模扩大，自定义工具会带来维护负担和不一致性问题。
Source
Building custom tools involves implementing the tool function, creating tool definitions, and building execution infrastructure. While straightforward for simple cases, custom tools create a maintenance burden and inconsistency as projects scale.
模型上下文协议（MCP）通过服务器-客户端架构标准化了工具开发。
服务器负责托管和执行工具，而客户端则负责发现和调用它们。
这种分离使得工具能够在不同项目和供应商之间重复使用。
Source
MCP (Model Context Protocol) standardizes tool development through a server-client architecture. Servers host and execute tools, while clients discover and invoke them. This separation enables tool reuse across projects and providers.
