我们已经探讨了大型语言模型的工作原理，并赋予了它们使用工具的能力。
现在，是时候将这些部分组合成更强大的东西：一个能够推理自身需求、采取行动获取所需、并持续运作直至解决问题的智能体。
Source
We’ve explored how LLMs work and given them the ability to use tools. Now it's time to combine these pieces into something more powerful: an agent that can reason about what it needs, take actions to get it, and continue until it solves the problem.
如图4.1所示，我们现在将通过构建一个采用ReAct模式的智能体来完成基础智能体循环的搭建，该模式通过链接多步推理与行动来端到端地解决问题，并加入稳健的错误处理机制。
ReAct（推理+行动）并非一个框架，而是一种设计智能体的方式，它模拟了人类解决问题的过程：评估当前状况、决定需要哪些信息或采取何种行动、执行该行动、观察结果，并不断重复这一循环。
Source
As shown in figure 4.1, we’ll now complete the foundation of the basic agent loop by building an Agent using the ReAct pattern, chaining multi-step reasoning and actions to solve problems end-to-end, and adding robust error handling. ReAct (Reasoning + Acting) is not a framework but a way of designing agents that mirrors how humans solve problems: assess the situation, decide what information or action is needed, execute that action, observe the results, and repeat
图4.1 书籍结构概览——聚焦第4章。
Source
Figure 4.1 Book structure overview - Chapter 4 in focus.
到本章结束时，你将拥有一个可运行的智能体，它能够搜索网络获取实时信息，通过多步推理链解决问题，优雅地处理错误，并以你指定的任何格式返回结构化输出。
我们将在GAIA基准测试上对其进行测试。
这个智能体将作为后续所有内容的基础：记忆系统、规划策略、知识检索以及多智能体协作。
Source
By the end of this chapter, you'll have a working Agent that can search the web for real-time information, chain multiple steps of reasoning to solve problems, handle errors gracefully, and return structured output in any format you specify. We'll test it on the GAIA benchmark. This agent will serve as the foundation for everything that follows: memory systems, planning strategies, knowledge retrieval, and multi-agent collaboration.
4.1 ReAct智能体工作原理
Source
4.1 How ReAct agents work
思考一下你会如何回答这个问题：“如果马拉松选手埃利乌德·基普乔格能够无限期地保持他的世界纪录速度，他需要多长时间才能到达月球？”
Source
Think about how you would answer this question: "If marathon runner Eliud Kipchoge could maintain his world record pace indefinitely, how long would it take him to reach the Moon?"
你不会试图立即回答。
相反，你会这样思考：“我需要基普乔格的马拉松配速和地月距离。”然后你会搜索这些信息，计算结果，并组织你的答案。
这种思考与行动的自然循环正是ReAct智能体的运作方式。
Source
You wouldn't try to answer immediately. Instead, you'd think: "I need Kipchoge's marathon pace and the Earth-Moon distance." Then you'd search for that information, calculate the result, and formulate your answer. This natural cycle of thinking and acting is exactly how ReAct agents operate.
ReAct（即推理加行动）是大多数现代AI智能体背后的基础模式。
其核心理念很简单：智能体不是试图一次性回答所有问题，而是在推理所需信息和采取行动获取信息之间交替进行。
Source
ReAct, which stands for Reasoning plus Acting, is the foundational pattern behind most modern AI agents. The core idea is simple: instead of trying to answer everything at once, an agent alternates between reasoning about what it needs and taking actions to get it.
4.1.1 思考-行动循环
Source
4.1.1 The think-act cycle
让我们看看ReAct智能体将如何解决基普乔格问题：
Source
Let's see how a ReAct agent would tackle the Kipchoge problem:
代码保持原样
Thought: I need to find Kipchoge's marathon world record pace. Action: search_web("Kipchoge marathon world record") Observation: Kipchoge's record is 2:01:09 for 42.195 km (Berlin 2022) Thought: Now I need the Earth-Moon distance at closest approach. Action: search_wikipedia("Moon perigee distance") Observation: The Moon's perigee (closest approach) is 356,500 km Thought: I can now calculate the time needed. Action: calculator("356500 / (42.195 / 2.0186) * 1") Observation: 17,034 hours Thought: I have enough information to answer. Final Answer: Approximately 17,000 hours
注意这个模式。
在每一步中，智能体都会明确陈述其思考内容，采取具体行动，并观察结果。
这个循环会一直重复，直到智能体收集到足够的信息来提供最终答案。
Source
Notice the pattern. At each step, the agent explicitly states what it's thinking, takes a concrete action, and observes the result. This cycle repeats until the agent has gathered enough information to provide a final answer.
这种方法的强大之处在于其适应性。
如果首次搜索返回的结果不理想，智能体可以尝试不同的查询。
如果计算结果似乎有误，它可以通过搜索额外信息来验证。
与遇到意外情况就会中断的固定脚本不同，ReAct智能体会根据发现的信息调整其方法。
Source
What makes this approach powerful is its adaptability. If the first search returned unhelpful results, the agent could try a different query. If the calculation seemed wrong, it could verify by searching for additional information. Unlike a fixed script that breaks when something unexpected happens, a ReAct agent adjusts its approach based on what it discovers.
这反映了人类自然解决问题的过程。
我们不会执行预先确定的步骤序列。
我们思考、行动、观察结果，并决定下一步该做什么。
大语言模型负责推理，而工具则负责执行动作。
两者结合形成一个系统，能够解决任何一方单独都无法解决的问题。
Source
This mirrors how humans naturally solve problems. We don't execute a predetermined sequence of steps. We think, act, observe the results, and decide what to do next. The LLM handles the reasoning, while tools handle the actions. Together, they form a system that can tackle problems neither could solve alone.
4.1.2 从文本解析到工具调用
Source
4.1.2 From text parsing to tool calling
早期的ReAct实现面临一个令人沮丧的问题：它们完全依赖于文本解析。
智能体必须以精确的格式输出响应，例如Action: search["query"]，任何偏差都会导致系统崩溃。
缺失一个括号、多出一个空格或关键词稍有不同，都会导致解析失败。
开发者花费大量精力精心设计提示词，恳求大语言模型遵循精确的格式规则，但错误仍然屡见不鲜。
Source
Early ReAct implementations faced a frustrating problem: they relied entirely on text parsing. The agent had to output responses in an exact format, like Action: search["query"], and any deviation would break the system. A missing bracket, an extra space, or a slightly different keyword would cause parsing failures. Developers spent enormous effort crafting prompts that begged the LLM to follow precise formatting rules, yet errors remained common.
工具调用消除了这种脆弱性。
LLM不再解析自由格式文本，而是生成结构化输出，精确指定调用哪个工具及使用哪些参数。
这种格式由API保证，而非寄希望于LLM完美遵循指令。
Source
Tool Calling eliminates this fragility. Instead of parsing free-form text, the LLM generates structured outputs that specify exactly which tool to call and with what arguments. The format is guaranteed by the API, not by hoping the LLM follows instructions perfectly.
图4.2展示了这一演进过程。
左侧，传统方法需要显式的“思考”和“行动”文本，这些文本必须被解析。
右侧，现代工具调用原生处理这一过程。
Source
Figure 4.2 illustrates this evolution. On the left, the traditional approach requires explicit "Thought" and "Action" text that must be parsed. On the right, modern Tool Calling handles this natively.
图4.2展示了从基于文本的ReAct到工具调用ReAct的演变过程。显式的“思考”步骤已被内化到LLM的工具选择流程中，从而消除了对脆弱文本解析的需求。
Source
Figure 4.2 Evolution from text-based ReAct to tool-calling ReAct. The explicit "Thought" step has been internalized into the LLM's tool selection process, eliminating the need for fragile text parsing.
你可能会疑惑：如果没有了明确的“思考”步骤，这还能算是ReAct吗？
是的。
推理并未消失。
它已移至LLM内部。
正如我们在第3章所见，现代大型语言模型（LLM）接受了大量工具调用示例的训练，学会了识别在何种情况下应使用何种工具。
当LLM选择工具并指定其参数时，它已经在内部完成了推理。
其模式依然相同：思考所需内容，采取行动获取，观察结果，然后重复这一过程。
Source
You might wonder: if there's no explicit "Thought" step anymore, is it still ReAct? Yes. The reasoning hasn't disappeared. It has moved inside the LLM. As we saw in chapter 3, modern LLMs are trained on extensive tool-calling examples, learning to recognize which tool is appropriate for which situation. When the LLM selects a tool and specifies its arguments, it has already performed the reasoning internally. The pattern remains the same: reason about what's needed, act to get it, observe the result, repeat.
这就是为什么基于工具调用的智能体在LangGraph、Google ADK和HuggingFace SmolAgents等主流框架中仍被称为ReAct智能体。
其核心原则保持不变：通过迭代推理与行动实现自适应问题解决，由大型语言模型根据上下文动态选择工具，而非遵循预设脚本。
Source
This is why Tool Calling-based agents are still called ReAct agents across major frameworks like LangGraph, Google ADK, and HuggingFace SmolAgents. The core principles remain intact: adaptive problem-solving through iterative reasoning and action, with the LLM dynamically selecting tools based on context rather than following a predetermined script.
现在我们已经准备好构建自己的智能体了。
我们先来看看将要实现的完整架构，从最终结果开始，然后反向理解需要构建的每个组件。
Source
Now we're ready to build our own agent. Let’s look at the complete architecture of what we're going to implement, starting with the end result and working backward to understand each component we need to build.
4.2 智能体架构概述
Source
4.2 Agent architecture overview
在深入实现细节之前，我们先来看看最终要构建的目标。
先理解整体框架，有助于你领会每个组件存在的意义及其协同工作的方式。
本章代码可在此处找到：https://github.com/shangrilar/ai-agent-from-scratch/tree/main/chapter_04_basic_agent。
Source
Before diving into implementation details, let's see what we're building toward. Understanding the complete picture first will help you appreciate why each component exists and how they work together. The code for this chapter can be found here: https://github.com/shangrilar/ai-agent-from-scratch/tree/main/chapter_04_basic_agent.
4.2.1 已完成的智能体
Source
4.2.1 The completed agent
这是我们完成的智能体在实际运行中的样子。
Source
Here's how our finished agent will look in action.
清单4.1 智能体使用示例
Source
Listing 4.1 Agent usage example
代码保持原样
from scratch_agents import Agent, LlmClient from scratch_agents.tools import calculator, search_web agent = Agent( model=LlmClient(model="gpt-5-mini"), tools=[calculator, search_web], instructions="You are a helpful assistant" ) result = await agent.run("What is 1234 * 5678?")
这个简单的界面背后隐藏着巨大的复杂性。
智能体接收用户问题，决定是否使用工具，如有需要则执行工具，并返回最终答案。
对于上面的乘法问题，它会调用计算器工具并返回“7,006,652”。
Source
This simple interface hides significant complexity. The agent receives a user question, decides whether to use tools, executes them if needed, and returns a final answer. For the multiplication question above, it would call the calculator tool and return "7,006,652."
但在这个简洁的API背后，究竟发生了什么？
要构建一个真正能工作的智能体，我们需要理解其信息流以及实现它的各个组件。
Source
But what happens behind this clean API? To build an agent that actually works, we need to understand the information flow and the components that make it possible.
4.2.2 信息流：核心设计
Source
4.2.2 Information flow: The core design
智能体的工作概念上很简单：接收用户输入，询问大语言模型下一步该做什么，如果请求使用工具则执行，将结果反馈给大语言模型，然后重复这一过程直到完成。
这个循环会持续进行，直到大语言模型认为已获得足够信息来提供最终答案。
Source
An agent's job is straightforward in concept: receive user input, ask the LLM what to do next, execute tools if requested, feed results back to the LLM, and repeat until done. This cycle continues until the LLM decides it has enough information to provide a final answer.
仅凭消息为何不够
Source
Why messages alone aren't enough
你可能会认为，只需维护一个简单的消息列表（即与大型语言模型的对话历史）就足够了。
毕竟，我们在第2章管理对话时就是这样做的。
然而，运行一个智能体需要追踪更多的信息：
Source
You might think that maintaining a simple list of messages (the conversation history with the LLM) would suffice. After all, that's what we did in chapter 2 when managing conversations. However, running an agent requires tracking much more information:
事件：所有交互的历史记录，包括用户消息、LLM响应和工具执行结果
Source
events: The history of all interactions, including user messages, LLM responses, and tool execution results
current_step：一个计数器，用于防止无限循环（如果代理持续调用工具怎么办？）
Source
current_step: A counter to prevent infinite loops (what if the agent keeps calling tools forever?)
execution_id：用于调试和日志记录的唯一标识符（哪个执行产生了此错误？）
Source
execution_id: A unique identifier for debugging and logging (which execution produced this error?)
状态：一个用于执行过程中动态数据的便签板，例如任务进度、中间结果或工具可能需要使用的用户偏好
Source
state: A scratchpad for dynamic data during execution, such as task progress, intermediate results, or user preferences that tools might need
final_result：一个用于判断执行是否完成的标志
Source
final_result: A flag to know when execution is complete
如果我们将这些信息分散到不同的变量中，并分别传递给每个方法，代码就会变得难以管理。
每个方法都需要一个冗长的参数列表，而添加新信息（如第6章中的记忆）则需要修改每个方法的签名。
Source
If we scatter this information across different variables and pass them individually to each method, the code becomes unwieldy. Every method would need a long parameter list, and adding new information (like memory in chapter 6) would require modifying every method signature.
解决方案是将所有内容整合到一个单一容器中。
所有方法都接收这一个容器，当需要新信息时，我们只需修改容器定义。
这个容器就是ExecutionContext，它是所有执行状态的中央存储。
Source
The solution is to consolidate everything into a single container. All methods receive this one container, and when new information is needed, we only modify the container definition. This container is ExecutionContext, the central storage for all execution states.
以ExecutionContext为中心的设计
Source
The ExecutionContext-centered design
图4.3展示了信息如何通过我们的智能体流动，其中ExecutionContext处于核心位置。
Source
Figure 4.3 illustrates how information flows through our agent, with ExecutionContext at the center.
图4.3展示了智能体架构中的信息流。ExecutionContext位于中心，管理所有执行状态。箭头表示：(1) 从Context到LlmRequest再到LlmClient，用于发出LLM调用；(2) LlmResponse返回Context，用于接收响应；(3) Context与Tools之间的双向流，用于工具执行。
Source
Figure 4.3 Information flow in the agent architecture. ExecutionContext sits at the center, managing all execution state. Arrows show: (1) Context to LlmRequest to LlmClient for outgoing LLM calls, (2) LlmResponse back to Context for incoming responses, and (3) bidirectional flow between Context and Tools for tool execution.
ExecutionContext作为中央存储，所有信息都在此汇聚。
当智能体需要调用LLM时，它会从ExecutionContext中提取相关信息，生成LlmRequest。
当LLM响应时，响应会流回ExecutionContext中。
当工具执行时，智能体会将ExecutionContext传递给它们，以便工具访问所需的执行状态，并将执行结果记录回ExecutionContext中。
Source
ExecutionContext serves as the central storage where all information converges. When the agent needs to call the LLM, it extracts relevant information from ExecutionContext into an LlmRequest. When the LLM responds, the response flows back into ExecutionContext. When tools execute, the agent passes ExecutionContext to them so they can access any execution state they need, and their results are recorded back into ExecutionContext.
这种架构具有两大关键优势。
首先，它简化了方法签名，因为每个方法只需接收上下文。
其次，它支持上下文传播，使智能体能够将ExecutionContext传递给需要访问执行状态的工具（例如，在行动前检查用户权限的工具）。
Source
This architecture provides two key benefits. First, it simplifies method signatures since every method just receives the context. Second, it enables context propagation, where the agent can pass ExecutionContext to tools that need access to execution state (for example, a tool that checks user permissions before acting).
请注意LlmRequest与ExecutionContext之间的分离。
虽然ExecutionContext存储所有信息，但LlmRequest是一个经过精心筛选的子集，仅包含大语言模型在特定调用中所需的内容。
这种分离正是上下文工程发挥作用的地方：决定包含哪些信息、省略哪些信息，以及如何格式化这些信息以实现最佳的大语言模型性能。
Source
Notice the separation between LlmRequest and ExecutionContext. While ExecutionContext stores everything, LlmRequest is a curated subset containing only what the LLM needs for a specific call. This separation is where context engineering happens: deciding what information to include, what to omit, and how to format it for optimal LLM performance.
4.2.3 我们需要构建的组件
Source
4.2.3 Components we need to build
在架构清晰之后，以下是我们的实施路线图。
每个组件在管理我们刚刚讨论的信息流中都扮演着特定的角色。
Source
With the architecture clear, here's our implementation roadmap. Each component has a specific role in managing the information flow we just discussed
表4.1 智能体组件与实施路线图
Source
Table 4.1 Agent components and implementation roadmap
我们将从基础开始构建。
ExecutionContext首先出现，因为其他所有内容都依赖于它。
工具抽象随之而来，因为我们需要一种一致的方式来定义和执行工具。
LLM通信层标准化了我们与语言模型的交互方式。
最后，Agent类将所有内容整合到解决问题的思考-行动循环中。
Source
We’ll build from the foundation up. ExecutionContext comes first because everything else depends on it. Tool abstraction follows because we need a consistent way to define and execute tools. The LLM communication layer standardizes how we talk to language models. Finally, the Agent class brings everything together into the think-act loop that solves problems.
4.3 执行上下文：智能体的核心存储
Source
4.3 ExecutionContext: The agent's central storage
我们需要ExecutionContext来避免状态分散在多个变量中，并简化组件间共享信息的方式。
现在，让我们通过检查代理运行时实际发生的情况来确定需要存储什么。
Source
We need ExecutionContext to avoid scattering state across multiple variables and to simplify how components share information. Now, let's determine what we need to store by examining what actually happens when an agent runs.
4.3.1 智能体执行过程中会发生什么？
Source
4.3.1 What happens during agent execution?
回想一下第4.1节中的基普乔格问题。
当智能体解决这个问题时，会展开一系列事件：
Source
Recall the Kipchoge problem from section 4.1. When an agent solves this problem, a series of events unfolds:
用户问道：“基普乔格跑到月球需要多长时间？”
Source
User asks: "How long would it take Kipchoge to run to the Moon?"
LLM决定需要信息 → 请求search_web工具。
Source
LLM decides it needs information → requests search_web tool.
工具执行并返回：“基普乔格的纪录是2小时01分09秒，距离为42.195公里。”
Source
Tool executes and returns: "Kipchoge's record is 2:01:09 for 42.195km."
LLM需要更多信息 → 请求使用search_wikipedia工具。
Source
LLM needs more information → requests search_wikipedia tool.
工具执行并返回：“月球近地点为356,500公里。”
Source
Tool executes and returns: "Moon's perigee is 356,500 k.m."
LLM现在可以计算 → 请求计算器工具。
Source
LLM can now calculate → requests calculator tool.
工具执行并返回：“17034”
Source
Tool executes and returns: "17034"
LLM提供了最终答案：“大约17,000小时。”
Source
LLM provides the final answer: "Approximately 17,000 hours."
观察这个序列，我们可以识别出三种不同类型的事件：
Source
Looking at this sequence, we can identify three distinct types of occurrences:
消息是对话中的文本交换。
用户的初始问题和LLM的最终答案都是消息。
每条消息都有一个角色（用户、助手或系统）和文本内容。
Source
Messages are text exchanges in the conversation. The user's initial question and the LLM's final answer are both messages. Each message has a role (user, assistant, or system) and text content.
当大语言模型决定使用工具时，就会发生工具调用。
大语言模型会指定调用哪个工具以及使用什么参数。
在上述步骤2中，大语言模型请求使用查询“Kipchoge马拉松世界纪录”进行网络搜索。
Source
Tool Calls occur when the LLM decides to use a tool. The LLM specifies which tool to call and with what arguments. In step 2 above, the LLM requests search_web with the query "Kipchoge marathon world record."
工具结果记录了工具执行时发生的情况。
它们包含工具的输出以及执行是否成功或失败。
上述步骤3将是一个包含基普乔格马拉松时间的成功结果。
Source
Tool Results capture what happens when tools execute. They include the tool's output and whether execution succeeded or failed. Step 3 above would be a successful result containing Kipchoge's marathon time.
让我们将这些定义为数据类型。
Source
Let's define these as data types.
清单4.2 智能体通信的内容类型
Source
Listing 4.2 Content types for agent communication
代码保持原样
class Message(BaseModel): """A text message in the conversation.""" type: Literal["message"] = "message" role: Literal["system", "user", "assistant"] content: str class ToolCall(BaseModel): """LLM's request to execute a tool.""" type: Literal["tool_call"] = "tool_call" tool_call_id: str name: str arguments: dict class ToolResult(BaseModel): """Result from tool execution.""" type: Literal["tool_result"] = "tool_result" tool_call_id: str name: str status: Literal["success", "error"] content: list ContentItem = Union[Message, ToolCall, ToolResult]
每个类中的type字段作为鉴别器，便于识别我们正在处理的内容类型。
tool_call_id将ToolResult链接回其原始的ToolCall，这在多个工具并行执行时至关重要。
Source
The type field in each class serves as a discriminator, making it easy to identify what kind of content we're dealing with. The tool_call_id links a ToolResult back to its originating ToolCall, which is essential when multiple tools execute in parallel.
这些内容类型记录了发生的事件，但为了调试和分析，我们还需要知道每段内容是由谁在何时产生的。
我们使用一个Event类来包装内容项及其元数据。
Source
These content types capture what happened, but for debugging and analysis, we also need to know who produced each piece of content and when. We wrap content items with metadata using an Event class.
清单4.3 用于执行跟踪的Event类
Source
Listing 4.3 Event class for execution tracking
代码保持原样
class Event(BaseModel): """A recorded occurrence during agent execution.""" id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4())) execution_id: str timestamp: float = Field(default_factory=lambda: datetime.now().timestamp()) author: str # "user" or agent name content: List[ContentItem] = Field(default_factory=list)
执行ID（execution_id）将单次智能体运行中的所有事件归为一组，使我们能够追踪整个问题解决过程。
作者字段用于区分用户输入与智能体操作。
以下是Kipchoge问题中一个步骤作为事件（Event）的示例。
Source
The execution_id groups all events from a single agent run, enabling us to trace an entire problem-solving session. The author field distinguishes between user input and agent actions. Here's how one step from the Kipchoge problem would look as an Event.
代码保持原样
Event( execution_id="abc-123", author="research_agent", content=[ToolCall( tool_call_id="call-1", name="search_web", arguments={"query": "Kipchoge marathon world record"} )] )
智能体执行过程中的每一步都会成为一个事件，从而创建完整的审计追踪，这在调试时极具价值。
Source
Each step in the agent's execution becomes an Event, creating a complete audit trail that proves invaluable when debugging.
4.3.2 实现执行上下文
Source
4.3.2 Implementing ExecutionContext
既然我们已经知道要存储什么，实现ExecutionContext就变得简单直接了。
Source
Now that we know what to store, implementing ExecutionContext is straightforward.
清单4.4 ExecutionContext实现
Source
Listing 4.4 ExecutionContext implementation
代码保持原样
@dataclass class ExecutionContext: """Central storage for all execution state.""" execution_id: str = field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4())) events: List[Event] = field(default_factory=list) current_step: int = 0 state: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict) final_result: Optional[str | BaseModel] = None def add_event(self, event: Event): """Append an event to the execution history.""" self.events.append(event) def increment_step(self): """Move to the next execution step.""" self.current_step += 1
每个字段都有其特定的用途：
Source
Each field serves a specific purpose:
execution_id：此执行会话的唯一标识符，自动生成
Source
execution_id: Unique identifier for this execution session, automatically generated
事件：执行过程中所有事件按时间顺序排列的列表
Source
events: Chronological list of all Events that occur during execution
current_step：用于防止无限循环的计数器（代理在达到max_steps后停止）
Source
current_step: Counter to prevent infinite loops (agent stops after max_steps)
state：用于存储自定义数据的灵活键值存储，例如API配置或中间结果，供工具可能需要使用。
Source
state: Flexible key-value store for custom data that tools might need, such as API configurations or intermediate results
final_result：在执行完成时保存代理的答案
Source
final_result: Holds the agent's answer when execution completes
ExecutionContext也可以传递给需要访问执行状态的工具。
工具可能会从状态中读取数据，或者检查执行历史中的先前事件。
为了实现这一点，我们需要一种一致的方式来定义可以可选接收上下文的工具。
现在，让我们实现Tool Abstraction，将基于函数的工具统一到一个支持此功能的通用接口下。
Source
ExecutionContext can also be passed to tools that need access to the execution state. A tool might read from state or examine previous events in the execution history. For this to work, we need a consistent way to define tools that can optionally receive context. Now, let’s implement Tool Abstraction to unify the function-based tools under a common interface that supports this capability.
4.4 工具抽象
Source
4.4 Tool abstraction
在第3章中，我们将工具构建为简单的Python函数，并创建了一个实用程序，用于将它们转换为LLM的工具定义。
这种方法在学习工具调用的基础知识方面效果很好。
但随着我们准备构建一个完整的智能体框架，一些实际挑战开始显现，而我们的基于函数的方法无法很好地处理这些挑战。
Source
In chapter 3, we built tools as simple Python functions and created a utility to convert them into tool definitions for the LLM. This approach worked well for learning the basics of tool calling. But as we prepare to build a complete agent framework, several practical challenges emerge that our function-based approach doesn't handle well.
4.4.1 为什么我们需要统一的工具接口
Source
4.4.1 Why we need a unified tool interface
让我们回顾一下第3章构建的内容。
我们创建了calculator()和search_web()等函数，然后使用function_to_tool_definition()来生成LLM所需的模式。
Source
Let's revisit what we built in chapter 3. We created functions like calculator() and search_web(), then used function_to_tool_definition() to generate the schemas that LLMs need.
代码保持原样
def search_web(query: str, max_results: int = 5) -> str: """Search the web for information.""" return tavily_client.search(query, max_results=max_results) search_tool_definition = function_to_tool_definition(search_web) search_web(query="Python tutorials")
这种方法可行，但函数与其元数据是作为独立实体存在的。
在构建智能体时，我们需要将函数定义传递给大语言模型，并将名称映射回实际函数以供执行，同时需要手动保持所有内容同步。
Source
This works, but the function and its metadata exist as separate entities. When building an agent, we need to pass definitions to the LLM and map names back to functions for execution, keeping everything in sync manually.
通过工具抽象，所有内容都保持捆绑在一起。
Source
With tool abstraction, everything stays bundled together.
代码保持原样
@tool def search_web(query: str, max_results: int = 5) -> str: return tavily_client.search(query, max_results=max_results) search_web.tool_definition search_web.execute(query="Python tutorials")
我们将通过两个类来实现这一点：BaseTool定义接口，FunctionTool包装现有函数。
Source
Let's implement this with two classes: BaseTool, defining the interface, and FunctionTool wrapping existing functions.
4.4.2 BaseTool：基础组件
Source
4.4.2 BaseTool: The foundation
我们框架中的每个工具都将继承自BaseTool，这是一个定义工具含义的抽象基类。
让我们来看看这个接口需要提供什么。
Source
Every tool in our framework will inherit from BaseTool, an abstract base class that defines what it means to be a tool. Let's examine what this interface needs to provide.
一个工具必须具备三个基本属性：用于识别的名称、解释其用途的描述，以及告知LLM如何使用它的工具定义模式。
该工具还必须可执行，我们将通过一个异步执行方法来表示，该方法接收ExecutionContext以及任何参数。
Source
A tool must have three essential properties: a name for identification, a description explaining its purpose, and a tool_definition schema that tells the LLM how to use it. The tool must also be executable, which we'll represent with an async execute method that receives ExecutionContext along with any arguments.
初始化过程提供了合理的默认值：如果未指定名称，则使用类名；如果未提供描述，则使用文档字符串。
这减少了创建简单工具时的样板代码。
tool_definition属性返回一个模式，该模式告诉LLM该工具接受哪些参数。
我们将其存储为_tool_definition，以便子类在需要时可以延迟生成。
Source
The initialization provides sensible defaults: if no name is given, it uses the class name; if no description is given, it uses the docstring. This reduces boilerplate when creating simple tools. The tool_definition property returns the schema that tells the LLM what parameters the tool accepts. We store it as _tool_definition to allow subclasses to generate it lazily if needed.
清单4.5 BaseTool抽象类
Source
Listing 4.5 BaseTool abstract class
代码保持原样
class BaseTool(ABC): """Abstract base class for all tools.""" def __init__( self, name: str = None, description: str = None, tool_definition: Dict[str, Any] = None, ): self.name = name or self.__class__.__name__ self.description = description or self.__doc__ or "" self._tool_definition = tool_definition @property def tool_definition(self) -> Dict[str, Any] | None: return self._tool_definition @abstractmethod async def execute(self, context: ExecutionContext, **kwargs) -> Any: pass async def __call__(self, context: ExecutionContext, **kwargs) -> Any: return await self.execute(context, **kwargs)
execute方法是抽象的，因为每个工具都必须实现自己的逻辑。
注意，它总是将上下文作为第一个参数接收。
这是实现上下文传播的关键设计决策：Agent将ExecutionContext传递给每个工具，而工具可以在需要访问执行状态时使用它。
不需要上下文的工具会直接忽略它。
Source
The execute method is abstract because every tool must implement its own logic. Notice that it always receives context as its first parameter. This is the key design decision that enables context propagation: the Agent passes ExecutionContext to every tool, and tools can use it if they need access to execution state. Tools that don't need context simply ignore it.
最终，__call__ 方法提供了语法上的便利。
我们可以将工具的执行方式从 tool.execute(context, query="test") 简化为 tool(context, query="test")。
Source
Finally, __call__ provides syntactic convenience. Instead of writing tool.execute(context, query="test"), we can write tool(context, query="test").
定义好BaseTool后，我们就有了一个所有工具都必须遵循的契约。
在下一节中，我们将实现FunctionTool来封装第3章中创建的简单函数。
Source
With BaseTool defined, we have a contract that all tools must follow. In the next section, we'll implement FunctionTool to wrap the simple functions we created in Chapter 3.
4.4.3 FunctionTool：函数封装
Source
4.4.3 FunctionTool: Wrapping functions
FunctionTool充当适配器，将现有函数包装为BaseTool接口。
核心挑战在于上下文传播：Agent将ExecutionContext传递给每个工具，但大多数函数并不期望接收上下文参数。
它们的函数签名类似于search_web(query: str)，而不是search_web(context: ExecutionContext, query: str)。
Source
FunctionTool acts as an adapter that wraps existing functions with the BaseTool interface. The key challenge is context propagation: the Agent passes ExecutionContext to every tool, but most functions don't expect a context parameter. They have signatures like search_web(query: str), not search_web(context: ExecutionContext, query: str).
解决方案是在初始化时检查每个函数的签名。
如果函数有上下文参数，我们就传递它。
否则，我们就省略它。
简单函数保持不变，而上下文感知函数在需要时可以访问执行状态。
Source
The solution is to inspect each function's signature at initialization. If the function has a context parameter, we pass it. If not, we omit it. Simple functions work unchanged, while context-aware functions can access execution state when needed.
在初始化过程中，我们会检查函数是否接受上下文参数。
execute方法利用这一信息来决定是否转发上下文。
代理将所有工具同等对待，向每个工具传递上下文，而每个工具自行决定是否使用它。
_generate_definition方法复用第3章中的function_to_input_schema，通过函数的类型提示自动创建工具模式。
Source
During initialization, we check whether the function accepts a context parameter. The execute method uses this information to decide whether to forward the context. The Agent treats all tools identically, passing context to every one, and each tool decides whether to use it. The _generate_definition method reuses function_to_input_schema from Chapter 3 to automatically create the tool schema from the function's type hints.
清单4.6 FunctionTool实现
Source
Listing 4.6 FunctionTool implementation
代码保持原样
class FunctionTool(BaseTool): """Wraps a Python function as a BaseTool.""" def __init__( self, func: Callable, name: str = None, description: str = None, tool_definition: Dict[str, Any] = None ): self.func = func self.needs_context = 'context' in inspect.signature(func).parameters name = name or func.__name__ description = description or (func.__doc__ or "").strip() tool_definition = tool_definition or self._generate_definition() super().__init__( name=name, description=description, tool_definition=tool_definition ) async def execute(self, context: ExecutionContext, **kwargs) -> Any: """Execute the wrapped function.""" if self.needs_context: result = self.func(context=context, **kwargs) else: result = self.func(**kwargs) # Handle both sync and async functions if inspect.iscoroutine(result): return await result return result def _generate_definition(self) -> Dict[str, Any]: """Generate tool definition from function signature.""" parameters = function_to_input_schema(self.func) return format_tool_definition(self.name, self.description, parameters)
以下是FunctionTool的实际应用示例。
函数的名称、文档字符串和参数会被自动提取，以创建一个功能完整的工具。
Source
Here's FunctionTool in action. The function's name, docstring, and parameters are automatically extracted to create a fully functional tool.
代码保持原样
def calculator(expression: str) -> float: """Calculate mathematical expressions.""" return eval(expression) calc_tool = FunctionTool(calculator) print(calc_tool.name) # "calculator" print(calc_tool.description) # "Calculate mathematical expressions." await calc_tool(context, expression="1234 * 5678") # 7006652
@tool 装饰器
Source
The @tool decorator
为方便起见，我们提供了一个用于创建FunctionTool实例的装饰器。
以下代码等价于编写calculator = FunctionTool(calculator)，但语法更简洁。
Source
For convenience, we provide a decorator that creates FunctionTool instances. The following code is equivalent to writing calculator = FunctionTool(calculator), but with cleaner syntax
代码保持原样
@tool def calculator(expression: str) -> float: """Calculate mathematical expressions.""" return eval(expression)
该装饰器还接受可选参数来覆盖工具的元数据。
您无需使用函数的名称和文档字符串，而是可以指定自定义值，这些值将出现在发送给LLM的工具定义中。
Source
The decorator also accepts optional parameters to override the tool's metadata. Instead of using the function's name and docstring, you can specify custom values that will appear in the tool definition sent to the LLM.
代码保持原样
@tool(name="web_search", description="Search the internet for information") def search_web(query: str) -> str: """Search the web.""" return tavily_client.search(query)
在本书中，我们将使用@tool，因其语法更简洁。
该实现是FunctionTool的一个轻量级封装。
详情请参阅GitHub仓库。
Source
Throughout this book, we'll use @tool for its cleaner syntax. The implementation is a thin wrapper around FunctionTool. See the GitHub repository for details.
4.4.4 集成MCP工具
Source
4.4.4 Integrating MCP Tools
我们探索了MCP，并连接到MCP服务器以发现和执行工具。
现在我们需要在智能体框架中使用这些工具。
挑战在于，MCP工具运行在外部服务器上，需要通过session.call_tool()来调用，而我们的智能体期望的是具有execute()方法的BaseTool实例。
Source
We explored MCP and connected to the MCP servers to discover and execute tools. Now we need to use those tools in our agent framework. The challenge is that MCP tools live on external servers and are executed via session.call_tool(), while our Agent expects BaseTool instances with an execute() method.
解决方案是为每个MCP工具创建一个包装函数来调用服务器，然后用FunctionTool包装该函数。
这种方法复用我们已经构建的所有内容。
Source
The solution is to create a wrapper function for each MCP tool that calls the server, then wrap that function with FunctionTool. This approach reuses everything we've already built.
load_mcp_tools函数连接到MCP服务器，检索所有可用工具，并将每个工具转换为FunctionTool。
该函数接收连接参数（如启动服务器的命令），并返回一个工具列表，这些工具已准备就绪，可供我们的智能体使用。
Source
The load_mcp_tools function connects to an MCP server, retrieves all available tools, and converts each one into a FunctionTool. It takes connection parameters (like the command to start the server) and returns a list of tools ready for use with our agent.
清单4.7 从MCP服务器加载工具
Source
Listing 4.7 Loading tools from MCP servers
代码保持原样
async def load_mcp_tools(connection: dict) -> list[BaseTool]: """Load tools from an MCP server and convert to FunctionTools.""" tools = [] async with stdio_client(StdioServerParameters(**connection)) as (read, write): async with ClientSession(read, write) as session: await session.initialize() mcp_tools = await session.list_tools() for mcp_tool in mcp_tools.tools: func_tool = _create_mcp_tool(mcp_tool, connection) tools.append(func_tool) return tools
核心逻辑位于_create_mcp_tool函数中。
对于每个MCP工具，它会创建一个名为call_mcp的包装函数，该函数建立与服务器的连接，并使用传入的任何参数执行该工具。
然后，这个包装函数会进一步用FunctionTool进行封装。
注意，我们显式传递tool_definition，而不是让FunctionTool自动生成，因为MCP服务器已经通过mcp_tool.inputSchema提供了完整的模式定义。
Source
The core logic lives in _create_mcp_tool. For each MCP tool, it creates a wrapper function called call_mcp that establishes a connection to the server and executes the tool with whatever arguments are passed. This wrapper function is then wrapped with FunctionTool. Notice that we pass tool_definition explicitly rather than letting FunctionTool generate it, because the MCP server already provides a complete schema via mcp_tool.inputSchema.
清单4.8 从MCP工具创建FunctionTool
Source
Listing 4.8 Creating FunctionTool from the MCP tool
代码保持原样
def _create_mcp_tool(mcp_tool, connection: dict) -> FunctionTool: """Create a FunctionTool that wraps an MCP tool.""" async def call_mcp(**kwargs): async with stdio_client(StdioServerParameters(**connection)) as (read, write): async with ClientSession(read, write) as session: await session.initialize() result = await session.call_tool(mcp_tool.name, kwargs) return _extract_text_content(result) tool_definition = { "type": "function", "function": { "name": mcp_tool.name, "description": mcp_tool.description, "parameters": mcp_tool.inputSchema, } } return FunctionTool( func=call_mcp, name=mcp_tool.name, description=mcp_tool.description, tool_definition=tool_definition )
通过此适配器，MCP工具能够无缝集成到我们的智能体中。
以下示例从Tavily MCP服务器加载工具，并与本地计算器工具结合使用。
智能体并不知晓也不关心某些工具是本地函数，而另一些则调用远程MCP服务器。
它们都实现了相同的BaseTool接口。
Source
With this adapter, MCP tools integrate seamlessly with our agent. The following example loads tools from the Tavily MCP server and combines them with a local calculator tool. The agent doesn't know or care that some tools are local functions and others call remote MCP servers. They all implement the same BaseTool interface.
代码保持原样
connection = { "command": "npx", "args": ["-y", "tavily-mcp@latest"], "env": {"TAVILY_API_KEY": os.getenv("TAVILY_API_KEY")} } mcp_tools = await load_mcp_tools(connection) agent = Agent( model=LlmClient(model="gpt-5"), tools=[calculator, *mcp_tools], instructions="You are a helpful assistant." )
关于连接管理的说明
Source
A Note on Connection Management
此实现为每次工具调用创建新的连接。
虽然这种方法易于理解，但会增加开销。
在频繁使用MCP工具的生产系统中，您可能会维护一个持久会话，以避免重复的连接设置。
Source
This implementation creates a new connection for each tool call. While simple to understand, this approach adds overhead. In production systems with frequent MCP tool usage, you might maintain a persistent session to avoid repeated connection setup.
4.5 LLM 通信层
Source
4.5 LLM Communication layer
有了ExecutionContext存储我们的执行状态，以及工具在BaseTool下统一管理，我们还需要一个关键组件：一种与LLM通信的方式。
这一通信层弥合了我们内部数据结构与LLM API需求之间的鸿沟。
Source
With ExecutionContext storing our execution state and tools unified under BaseTool, we need one more piece: a way to communicate with the LLM. This communication layer bridges the gap between our internal data structures and the LLM's API requirements.
4.5.1 为何需要通信层？
Source
4.5.1 Why a communication layer?
考虑当我们的代理需要调用LLM时会发生什么。
ExecutionContext包含一个事件列表，每个事件持有ContentItems，如消息、工具调用和工具结果。
但LLM API期望特定的消息格式：一个包含角色和内容的字典列表。
需要有人在这些表示之间进行转换。
Source
Consider what happens when our agent needs to call the LLM. ExecutionContext contains a list of Events, each holding ContentItems like Messages, ToolCalls, and ToolResults. But LLM APIs expect a specific message format: a list of dictionaries with roles and content. Someone needs to translate between these representations.
我们还面临着提供商多样性的挑战。
虽然我们使用LiteLLM来抽象掉大部分提供商差异（正如我们在第2章所学），但我们仍需要以一致的方式构建请求，并将响应解析为标准格式。
如果没有这一层，翻译逻辑将分散在Agent类中，使其更难维护和扩展。
Source
We also face the challenge of provider diversity. While we use LiteLLM to abstract away most provider differences (as we learned in chapter 2), we still need to structure our requests consistently and parse responses into a standard format. Without this layer, translation logic would scatter throughout the Agent class, making it harder to maintain and extend.
解决方案是三个组件协同工作：
Source
The solution is three components working together:
LlmRequest 封装了我们想要发送的内容：指令、对话内容以及可用的工具。
它作为一个暂存区，在API调用之前，我们在此选择和整理信息。
Source
LlmRequest packages what we want to send: instructions, conversation contents, and available tools. It serves as a staging area where we select and organize information before the API call.
LlmClient负责实际的API通信。
它将LlmRequest转换为LLM API期望的格式，发起调用，并将响应转换回来。
Source
LlmClient handles the actual API communication. It transforms LlmRequest into the format LLM APIs expect, makes the call, and converts the response back.
LlmResponse 标准化了我们接收到的内容。
无论使用哪个提供商，响应都会以相同的格式返回，以便我们的 Agent 能够处理。
Source
LlmResponse standardizes what we receive. Regardless of which provider we use, responses come back in the same format that our Agent can process.
这种分离让每个组件保持专注。
LlmRequest对API格式一无所知。
LlmClient对ExecutionContext一无所知。
每个部分都专注于做好一件事。
Source
This separation keeps each component focused. LlmRequest knows nothing about API formats. LlmClient knows nothing about ExecutionContext. Each piece does one job well.
4.5.2 LlmRequest：选择发送内容
Source
4.5.2 LlmRequest: Selecting what to send
LlmRequest是我们代理向LLM发送请求的出站网关。
它包含了单次LLM调用所需的所有内容，并组织为四个组成部分。
Source
LlmRequest is the outbound gate from our agent to the LLM. It holds everything needed for a single LLM call, organized into four components.
清单 4.9 LlmRequest 类
Source
Listing 4.9 LlmRequest class
代码保持原样
class LlmRequest(BaseModel): """Request object for LLM calls.""" instructions: List[str] = Field(default_factory=list) contents: List[ContentItem] = Field(default_factory=list) tools: List[BaseTool] = Field(default_factory=list) tool_choice: Optional[str] = None
instructions字段存放系统提示片段。
我们允许使用多个指令字符串进行组合，而非单一的整体提示。
这种灵活性在指令来自不同来源时非常有用：基础智能体指令、任务特定指导或动态生成的上下文。
Source
The instructions field holds system prompt fragments. Rather than a single monolithic prompt, we allow multiple instruction strings that get combined. This flexibility proves useful when instructions come from different sources: base agent instructions, task-specific guidance, or dynamically generated context.
contents字段包含作为ContentItem对象的对话历史：用户和助手的消息、LLM请求的ToolCalls以及执行返回的ToolResults。
这是大型语言模型（LLM）用于理解当前状况的核心上下文。
Source
The contents field contains the conversation history as ContentItem objects: Messages from users and assistants, ToolCalls the LLM requested, and ToolResults from executions. This is the core context the LLM uses to understand the current situation.
tools字段列出了可用的工具，这些工具以BaseTool实例的形式存在。
LlmClient在构建API请求时会提取其定义。
Source
The tools field lists available tools as BaseTool instances. LlmClient will extract its definitions when building the API request.
tool_choice字段控制大语言模型如何选择工具。
将其设为“auto”则让大语言模型自由决定。
将其设为“required”会强制使用工具，这对于第4.6节中的结构化输出非常重要。
Source
The tool_choice field controls how the LLM selects tools. Setting it to "auto" lets the LLM decide freely. Setting it to "required" forces tool usage, which becomes important for structured output in section 4.6.
请注意LlmRequest不包含什么：它没有引用ExecutionContext或Events。
Agent负责从ExecutionContext中提取相关信息，并将其打包到LlmRequest中。
这种分离是刻意为之的。
它让LlmRequest成为一个简单的数据容器，同时将上下文选择逻辑保留在Agent中，这正是其所属之处。
Source
Notice what LlmRequest does not contain: it has no reference to ExecutionContext or Events. The Agent is responsible for extracting relevant information from ExecutionContext and packaging it into LlmRequest. This separation is intentional. It makes LlmRequest a simple data container while keeping context selection logic in the Agent where it belongs.
这就是上下文工程发生的地方。
在4.6节中，我们将在Agent类中实现_prepare_llm_request()方法，该方法决定将ExecutionContext中的哪些信息放入每个LlmRequest中。
目前，我们会将所有事件扁平化为内容。
在第6章中，这将成为内存和上下文管理策略的扩展点。
Source
This is where context engineering happens. In section 4.6, we will implement _prepare_llm_request() in the Agent class, which decides what information from ExecutionContext goes into each LlmRequest. For now, we will flatten all events into contents. In Chapter 6, this becomes the extension point for memory and context management strategies.
4.5.3 LlmResponse：标准化我们接收的内容
Source
4.5.3 LlmResponse: Standardizing what we receive
LlmResponse 是入站网关，用于标准化 LLM 的响应，无论其由哪个提供商生成。
Source
LlmResponse is the inbound gate, standardizing LLM responses regardless of which provider generated them.
清单 4.10 LlmResponse 类
Source
Listing 4.10 LlmResponse class
代码保持原样
class LlmResponse(BaseModel): """Response object from LLM calls.""" content: List[ContentItem] = Field(default_factory=list) error_message: Optional[str] = None usage_metadata: Dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)
内容字段包含LLM生成的内容，以ContentItem对象表示。
响应可能包含带有文本的Message、请求工具执行的一个或多个ToolCalls，或两者兼有。
使用我们在第4.3节中定义的相同ContentItem类型，可以保持整个系统中数据模型的一致性。
Source
The content field contains what the LLM produced, represented as ContentItem objects. A response might include a Message with text, one or more ToolCalls requesting tool execution, or both. Using the same ContentItem types we defined in section 4.3 keeps our data model consistent throughout the system.
error_message字段用于捕获失败信息。
当API调用因网络问题、速率限制或无效请求而失败时，我们会将错误存储在此处，而不是抛出异常。
这使得Agent能够优雅地处理失败，例如通过重试或通知用户。
Source
The error_message field captures failures. When an API call fails due to network issues, rate limits, or invalid requests, we store the error here rather than raising an exception. This allows the Agent to handle failures gracefully, perhaps by retrying or informing the user.
usage_metadata字段用于跟踪令牌消耗。
了解每次调用使用了多少输入和输出令牌，有助于成本管理和调试。
目前，我们只是简单地存储这些信息。
第10章详细介绍了监控和成本跟踪。
Source
The usage_metadata field tracks token consumption. Knowing how many input and output tokens each call uses helps with cost management and debugging. For now, we simply store this information. Chapter 10 covers monitoring and cost tracking in detail.
4.5.4 LlmClient：提供者适配器
Source
4.5.4 LlmClient: The provider adapter
LlmClient通过实际的LLM API桥接LlmRequest和LlmResponse。
得益于我们在第2章介绍的LiteLLM，我们可以通过单一实现支持多个提供商。
Source
LlmClient bridges LlmRequest and LlmResponse with actual LLM APIs. Thanks to LiteLLM, which we introduced in chapter 2, we can support multiple providers through a single implementation.
清单 4.11 LlmClient 类
Source
Listing 4.11 LlmClient class
代码保持原样
class LlmClient: """Client for LLM API calls using LiteLLM.""" def __init__(self, model: str, **config): self.model = model self.config = config async def generate(self, request: LlmRequest) -> LlmResponse: """Generate a response from the LLM.""" try: messages = self._build_messages(request) tools = [t.tool_definition for t in request.tools] if request.tools else None response = await acompletion( model=self.model, messages=messages, tools=tools, **({"tool_choice": request.tool_choice} if request.tool_choice else {}), **self.config ) return self._parse_response(response) except Exception as e: return LlmResponse(error_message=str(e))
构造函数接收一个模型标识符（例如“gpt-5-mini”或“anthropic/claude-sonnet-4-5”）以及可选的配置参数，如温度或最大令牌数。
Source
The constructor takes a model identifier (like "gpt-5-mini" or "anthropic/claude-sonnet-4-5") and optional configuration parameters such as temperature or max_tokens.
generate方法通过三个步骤来协调API调用。
首先，它从请求中构建消息列表。
其次，它通过简单的列表推导式提取工具定义。
最后，它调用LiteLLM的acompletion并解析响应。
如果任何步骤失败，它会返回一个包含捕获错误的LlmResponse，而不是导致程序崩溃。
Source
The generate method orchestrates the API call in three steps. First, it builds the messages list from the request. Second, it extracts tool definitions with a simple list comprehension. Third, it calls LiteLLM's acompletion and parses the response. If anything fails, it returns an LlmResponse with the error captured rather than crashing.
构建消息
Source
Building Messages
_build_messages 方法将 LlmRequest 的内容转换为 LLM API 所期望的消息格式。
这里的主要复杂性在于，OpenAI 的 API 要求助手消息及其工具调用出现在单个消息对象中，而我们将其存储为单独的 ContentItems。
Source
The _build_messages method transforms LlmRequest contents into the message format that LLM APIs expect. The main complexity here is that OpenAI's API requires assistant messages and their tool calls to appear together in a single message object, while we store them as separate ContentItems.
清单 4.12 构建 LLM API 的消息
Source
Listing 4.12 Building messages for LLM API
代码保持原样
def _build_messages(self, request: LlmRequest) -> List[dict]: """Convert LlmRequest to API message format.""" messages = [] for instruction in request.instructions: messages.append({"role": "system", "content": instruction}) for item in request.contents: if isinstance(item, Message): messages.append({"role": item.role, "content": item.content}) elif isinstance(item, ToolCall): tool_call_dict = { "id": item.tool_call_id, "type": "function", "function": { "name": item.name, "arguments": json.dumps(item.arguments) } } # Append to previous assistant message if exists if messages and messages[-1]["role"] == "assistant": messages[-1].setdefault("tool_calls", []).append(tool_call_dict) else: messages.append({ "role": "assistant", "content": None, "tool_calls": [tool_call_dict] }) elif isinstance(item, ToolResult): messages.append({ "role": "tool", "tool_call_id": item.tool_call_id, "content": str(item.content[0]) if item.content else "" }) return messages
逻辑对不同类型的ContentItem进行差异化处理。
消息被转换为标准消息对象。
ToolCalls被追加到前一条助手消息的tool_calls数组中，因为我们的代理将它们从同一个LLM响应中连续存储。
如果ToolCall出现时没有前一条助手消息，我们会创建一个内容为空的助手消息。
ToolResults转换为工具角色消息，并通过tool_call_id链接回其原始调用。
Source
The logic handles each ContentItem type differently. Messages become standard message objects. ToolCalls get appended to the preceding assistant message's tool_calls array, since our agent stores them consecutively from the same LLM response. If a ToolCall appears without a preceding assistant message, we create one with null content. ToolResults become tool-role messages linked back to their originating call via tool_call_id.
解析响应
Source
Parsing responses
_parse_response方法将API响应转换回我们的标准格式。
该方法同时处理文本响应和工具调用。
当LLM返回文本时，我们将其包装在Message中。
当它请求工具时，我们创建ToolCall对象。
两者都可能出现在同一个响应中，而我们的ContentItem列表自然地容纳了这种情况。
Source
The _parse_response method converts API responses back into our standard format. The method handles both text responses and tool calls. When the LLM returns text, we wrap it in a Message. When it requests tools, we create ToolCall objects. Both can appear in the same response, and our ContentItem list accommodates this naturally.
清单 4.13 解析 LLM API 响应
Source
Listing 4.13 Parsing LLM API response
代码保持原样
def _parse_response(self, response) -> LlmResponse: """Convert API response to LlmResponse.""" choice = response.choices[0] content_items = [] if choice.message.content: content_items.append(Message( role="assistant", content=choice.message.content )) if choice.message.tool_calls: for tc in choice.message.tool_calls: content_items.append(ToolCall( tool_call_id=tc.id, name=tc.function.name, arguments=json.loads(tc.function.arguments) )) return LlmResponse( content=content_items, usage_metadata={ "input_tokens": response.usage.prompt_tokens, "output_tokens": response.usage.completion_tokens, } )
4.5.5 整合实现
Source
4.5.5 Putting it together
定义好这三个组件后，以下是它们如何协同工作。
我们创建一个带有模型标识符的LlmClient，构建一个包含指令和对话内容的LlmRequest，然后调用generate()方法来获取LlmResponse。
响应内容列表包含LLM的输出作为ContentItem对象，我们可以遍历这些对象来提取答案。
Source
With all three components defined, here is how they work together. We create an LlmClient with a model identifier, build an LlmRequest containing our instructions and conversation contents, and call generate() to get an LlmResponse. The response's content list contains the LLM's output as ContentItem objects, which we can iterate through to extract the answer.
清单4.14 使用LLM通信层
Source
Listing 4.14 Using the LLM communication layer
代码保持原样
from scratch_agents import LlmClient, LlmRequest, Message # Create client client = LlmClient(model="gpt-5-mini") # Build request request = LlmRequest( instructions=["You are a helpful assistant."], contents=[Message(role="user", content="What is 2 + 2?")], ) # Generate response response = await client.generate(request) # Response contains the answer for item in response.content: if isinstance(item, Message): print(item.content) # "4"
通信层提供了清晰的关注点分离。
LlmRequest 封装了要发送的内容。
LlmClient 处理如何发送。
LlmResponse 标准化了返回的内容。
Source
The communication layer provides clean separation of concerns. LlmRequest packages what to send. LlmClient handles how to send it. LlmResponse standardizes what comes back.
4.6 实现智能体
Source
4.6 Implementing the agent
通过ExecutionContext存储状态、工具统一在BaseTool下、LlmClient处理大语言模型通信，我们已经准备好构建协调一切的Agent类。
智能体将我们构建的所有组件整合在一起，协调大语言模型与工具之间的信息流，逐步解决问题。
Source
With ExecutionContext storing our state, tools unified under BaseTool, and LlmClient handling LLM communication, we're ready to build the Agent class that orchestrates everything. The Agent brings together all the components we've built, coordinating information flow between the LLM and tools to solve problems step by step.
图4.4展示了我们所要实现的完整架构。
Agent通过_setup_tools()初始化，随后run()创建ExecutionContext并反复调用step()直至完成。
每个step()执行一次思考-行动循环：think()调用LLM来决定下一步操作，而act()则执行请求的工具。
Source
Figure 4.4 shows the complete picture of what we're implementing. The Agent initializes with _setup_tools(), then run() creates an ExecutionContext and repeatedly calls step() until completion. Each step() performs one think-act cycle: think() calls the LLM to decide what to do next, and act() executes any requested tools.
图4.4展示了智能体实现路线图，包含五个核心方法及其执行流程。编号序列说明了各组件如何协同工作以解决问题。
Source
Figure 4.4 Agent implementation roadmap showing the five core methods and their execution flow. The numbered sequence illustrates how each component works together to solve problems.
我们将按逻辑顺序实现这五种方法：
Source
We'll implement these five methods in a logical order:
_setup_tools()：注册代理将使用的工具，将列表转换为字典以实现高效查找
Source
_setup_tools(): Registers the tools the agent will use, converting the list into a dictionary for efficient lookup
run()：接收用户请求、管理执行循环并返回最终结果的入口点
Source
run(): The entry point that receives user requests, manages the execution loop, and returns the final result
step()：执行一次完整的思考-行动循环，每次交互都会更新ExecutionContext
Source
step(): Performs one complete think-act cycle, updating ExecutionContext with each interaction
think()：调用大语言模型来分析当前情况并决定下一步行动
Source
think(): Calls the LLM to analyze the situation and decide the next action
act()：执行由大语言模型选择的工具并捕获其结果
Source
act(): Executes the tools selected by the LLM and captures their results
在本节结束时，你将拥有一个能够解决多步骤问题的可运行智能体。
我们还将添加结构化输出能力，当你的应用需要可预测的数据格式时，允许智能体返回类型化的Pydantic模型，而非自由格式文本。
Source
By the end of this section, you'll have a working agent that can solve multi-step problems. We'll also add structured output capabilities, allowing the agent to return typed Pydantic models instead of free-form text when your application requires predictable data formats.
4.6.1 智能体类结构
Source
4.6.1 Agent class structure
让我们从Agent类的构造函数和_setup_tools()方法开始。
构造函数接收我们在前面章节构建的所有组件，并将它们存储起来供执行时使用。
Source
Let's start with the Agent class constructor and the _setup_tools() method. The constructor receives all the components we've built in previous sections and stores them for use during execution.
清单4.15 Agent类构造函数
Source
Listing 4.15 Agent class constructor
代码保持原样
class Agent: def __init__( self, model: LlmClient, tools: List[BaseTool] = None, instructions: str = "", max_steps: int = 10, ): self.model = model self.instructions = instructions self.max_steps = max_steps self.tools = self._setup_tools(tools or [])
这些参数各有其特定用途：
Source
The parameters serve distinct purposes:
model：处理LLM通信的LlmClient实例
Source
model: The LlmClient instance that handles LLM communication
工具：代理可使用的BaseTool实例列表
Source
tools: List of BaseTool instances the agent can use
定义智能体行为的系统提示
Source
instructions: System prompt that defines the agent's behavior
max_steps：安全限制，用于防止智能体在未得出结论的情况下持续调用工具而导致无限循环
Source
max_steps: Safety limit to prevent infinite loops when the agent keeps calling tools without reaching a conclusion
_setup_tools()方法用于准备工具列表以供使用。
目前，它只是原样返回列表，但此方法可作为未来增强功能的扩展点，例如添加默认工具。
Source
The _setup_tools() method prepares the tools list for use. For now, it simply returns the list unchanged, but this method serves as an extension point for future enhancements like adding default tools.
清单 4.16 设置智能体工具
Source
Listing 4.16 Setting up agent tools
代码保持原样
def _setup_tools(self, tools: List[BaseTool]) -> List[BaseTool]: return tools
在基本结构就位后，让我们实现协调整个执行的run()方法。
Source
With the basic structure in place, let's implement the run() method that orchestrates the entire execution.
4.6.2 run() 方法
Source
4.6.2 The run() Method
run()方法是智能体执行的入口点。
它创建执行环境，管理思考-行动循环，并返回结果。
Source
The run() method is the entry point for agent execution. It creates the execution environment, manages the think-act loop, and returns the result.
为了让调用者能够访问完整的执行轨迹，我们定义了AgentResult，它将最终输出与其ExecutionContext捆绑在一起。
这使得可以检查代理采取的每一步，这对于调试和分析来说非常宝贵。
Source
To give callers access to the full execution trace, we define AgentResult that bundles the final output with its ExecutionContext. This allows inspection of every step the agent took, which proves invaluable for debugging and analysis.
清单 4.17 AgentResult 数据类
Source
Listing 4.17 AgentResult dataclass
代码保持原样
@dataclass class AgentResult: """Result of an agent execution.""" output: str | BaseModel context: ExecutionContext
该方法首先检查是否提供了ExecutionContext，如果没有则创建一个。
然后它将用户的输入包装在Event中，并添加到上下文中。
主循环会重复调用step()方法，直到获得最终结果或达到最大步数限制。
每一步之后，我们会检查最后一个事件是否代表最终响应，如果是则提取结果。
Source
The method first checks if an ExecutionContext was provided, creating one if not. It then wraps the user's input in an Event and adds it to the context. The main loop repeatedly calls step() until either a final result is obtained or the maximum step limit is reached. After each step, we check if the last event represents a final response and extract the result if so.
清单4.18 代理运行方法
Source
Listing 4.18 Agent run method
代码保持原样
async def run( self, user_input: str, context: ExecutionContext = None ) -> str: # Create or reuse context if context is None: context = ExecutionContext() # Add user input as the first event user_event = Event( execution_id=context.execution_id, author="user", content=[Message(role="user", content=user_input)] ) context.add_event(user_event) # Execute steps until completion or max steps reached while not context.final_result and context.current_step < self.max_steps: await self.step(context) # Check if the last event is a final response last_event = context.events[-1] if self._is_final_response(last_event): context.final_result = self._extract_final_result(last_event) return AgentResult(output=context.final_result, context=context)
辅助方法负责处理完成检测和结果提取。
_is_final_response()方法通过检查事件内容来判断其是否代表最终答案。
当事件既不包含工具调用也不包含工具结果时，即表示大语言模型提供了直接答案，此时事件即为最终事件。
_extract_final_result()方法会遍历事件内容，以查找助手的消息。
Source
The helper methods handle completion detection and result extraction. The _is_final_response() method checks whether an event represents a final answer by examining its contents. An event is final when it contains neither tool calls nor tool results, meaning the LLM provided a direct answer. The _extract_final_result() method iterates through the event's content to find the assistant's message.
清单4.19 完成检测辅助函数
Source
Listing 4.19 Completion detection helpers
代码保持原样
def _is_final_response(self, event: Event) -> bool: """Check if this event contains a final response.""" has_tool_calls = any(isinstance(c, ToolCall) for c in event.content) has_tool_results = any(isinstance(c, ToolResult) for c in event.content) return not has_tool_calls and not has_tool_results def _extract_final_result(self, event: Event) -> str: for item in event.content: if isinstance(item, Message) and item.role == "assistant": return item.content return None
使用方法很简单。
通过result.output获取答案，需要时可通过result.context查看执行细节。
Source
Usage is straightforward. Access the answer via result.output, and examine execution details through result.context when needed.
代码保持原样
result = await agent.run("What is 1234 * 5678?") print(result.output) # "7006652" print(result.context.current_step)
4.6.3 step()方法
Source
4.6.3 The step() method
step()方法执行一个完整的思考-行动循环。
它准备一个请求给LLM，获取LLM的决策，并执行LLM请求的任何工具。
Source
The step() method performs one complete think-act cycle. It prepares a request for the LLM, gets the LLM's decision, and executes any tools the LLM requests.
该方法首先调用_prepare_llm_request()，将当前上下文打包成适合LLM的格式。
然后调用think()获取LLM的响应，并将该响应包装为Event记录到上下文中。
如果响应包含工具调用，则调用act()执行它们，并将结果作为另一个Event记录下来。
最后递增步骤计数器。
Source
The method starts by calling _prepare_llm_request() to package the current context into a format suitable for the LLM. It then calls think() to get the LLM's response and wraps that response in an Event, recording it in the context. If the response contains tool calls, the method calls act() to execute them and record the results as another Event. Finally, it increments the step counter.
清单4.20 代理步骤方法
Source
Listing 4.20 Agent step method
代码保持原样
async def step(self, context: ExecutionContext): # Prepare what to send to the LLM llm_request = self._prepare_llm_request(context) # Get LLM's decision llm_response = await self.think(llm_request) # Record LLM response as an event response_event = Event( execution_id=context.execution_id, author=self.name, content=llm_response.content, ) context.add_event(response_event) # Execute tools if the LLM requested any tool_calls = [c for c in llm_response.content if isinstance(c, ToolCall)] if tool_calls: tool_results = await self.act(context, tool_calls) tool_event = Event( execution_id=context.execution_id, author=self.name, content=tool_results, ) context.add_event(tool_event) context.increment_step()
_prepare_llm_request()方法从ExecutionContext中提取信息，并将其打包成LlmRequest。
它将所有事件扁平化为内容项列表，与代理指令和可用工具结合，并将工具选择设置为“自动”，以便LLM可以决定是否使用工具。
Source
The _prepare_llm_request() method extracts information from ExecutionContext and packages it into an LlmRequest. It flattens all events into a list of content items, combines them with the agent's instructions and available tools, and sets the tool choice to "auto" so the LLM can decide whether to use tools.
清单4.21 从上下文准备LLM请求
Source
Listing 4.21 Preparing LLM request from context
代码保持原样
def _prepare_llm_request(self, context: ExecutionContext) -> LlmRequest: # Flatten events into content items flat_contents = [] for event in context.events: flat_contents.extend(event.content) return LlmRequest( instructions=[self.instructions] if self.instructions else [], contents=flat_contents, tools=self.tools, tool_choice="auto" if self.tools else None, )
注意ExecutionContext和LlmRequest之间的分离。
ExecutionContext保存完整的执行历史，而LlmRequest仅包含我们选择发送给LLM的内容。
目前我们发送所有内容，但这种分离正是上下文工程发挥作用的地方。
你可以通过修改构建LlmRequest的方式，在不触及原始上下文的情况下，总结旧消息、省略不相关的工具结果或注入额外信息。
Source
Notice the separation between ExecutionContext and LlmRequest. ExecutionContext holds the complete execution history, while LlmRequest contains only what we choose to send to the LLM. Currently, we send everything, but this separation is where context engineering happens. You could summarize old messages, omit irrelevant tool results, or inject additional information, all by modifying how you build the LlmRequest without touching the original context.
4.6.4 think()与act()方法
Source
4.6.4 The think() and act() methods
think()和act()方法分别处理每个步骤中的两个核心操作：获取大语言模型的决策和执行所请求的工具。
Source
The think() and act() methods handle the two core operations in each step: getting the LLM's decision and executing the requested tools.
think()方法被有意设计得简单。
它接收准备好的LlmRequest并将其传递给LlmClient，然后返回任何返回的响应。
构建请求的所有复杂性都发生在_prepare_llm_request()中，而解析响应的所有复杂性都发生在LlmClient中。
这使得think()专注于单一职责。
Source
The think() method is intentionally simple. It takes the prepared LlmRequest and passes it to the LlmClient, returning whatever response comes back. All the complexity of building the request happens in _prepare_llm_request(), and all the complexity of parsing the response happens in LlmClient. This keeps think() focused on a single responsibility.
清单4.22 代理思考方法
Source
Listing 4.22 Agent think method
代码保持原样
async def think(self, llm_request: LlmRequest) -> LlmResponse: return await self.model.generate(llm_request)
act()方法执行LLM请求的工具。
它首先构建一个字典，将工具名称映射到工具实例，以便高效查找。
然后，它遍历每个ToolCall，检索对应的工具，使用提供的参数执行它，并收集结果。
该方法将ExecutionContext传递给每个工具执行，允许工具在需要时访问执行状态。
每次执行都包装在try-except块中，将失败捕获为错误结果，而不是导致整个代理崩溃。
Source
The act() method executes the tools that the LLM requested. It first builds a dictionary mapping tool names to tool instances for efficient lookup. Then it iterates through each ToolCall, retrieves the corresponding tool, executes it with the provided arguments, and collects the results. The method passes ExecutionContext to each tool execution, allowing tools to access execution state if they need it. Each execution is wrapped in a try-except block, capturing failures as error results rather than crashing the entire agent.
清单4.23 代理的act方法
Source
Listing 4.23 Agent act method
代码保持原样
async def act( self, context: ExecutionContext, tool_calls: List[ToolCall] ) -> List[ToolResult]: tools_dict = {tool.name: tool for tool in self.tools} results = [] for tool_call in tool_calls: if tool_call.name not in tools_dict: raise ValueError(f"Tool '{tool_call.name}' not found") tool = tools_dict[tool_call.name] try: output = await tool(context, **tool_call.arguments) results.append(ToolResult( tool_call_id=tool_call.tool_call_id, name=tool_call.name, status="success", content=[output], )) except Exception as e: results.append(ToolResult( tool_call_id=tool_call.tool_call_id, name=tool_call.name, status="error", content=[str(e)], )) return results
当工具执行失败时，错误信息会成为对话历史的一部分。
大型语言模型在下一步骤中会看到此次失败，并调整其方法，可能会尝试不同的工具或重新表述查询。
这种优雅的错误处理是ReAct模式的优势之一：智能体能够从失败中恢复，而非完全停止。
Source
When a tool execution fails, the error message becomes part of the conversation history. The LLM sees this failure in the next step and can adapt its approach, perhaps trying a different tool or rephrasing its query. This graceful error handling is one of the advantages of the ReAct pattern: the agent can recover from failures rather than stopping entirely.
4.7 添加结构化输出
Source
4.7 Adding structured output
在第2章中，我们使用结构化输出来测试LLM在GAIA基准问题上的表现。
我们定义了一个包含is_solvable、unsolvable_reason和final_answer等字段的GaiaOutput Pydantic模型，然后将其作为response_format参数传递，以确保LLM返回的数据具有可预测的结构。
这种方法在独立的LLM调用中效果良好。
Source
In chapter 2, we tested LLMs on GAIA benchmark problems using Structured Output. We defined a GaiaOutput Pydantic model with fields like is_solvable, unsolvable_reason, and final_answer, then passed it as the response_format parameter to ensure the LLM returned data in a predictable structure. This approach worked well for standalone LLM calls.
然而，我们在第4.6节构建的智能体仅返回自由格式的文本。
当大语言模型完成推理并提供最终答案时，_extract_final_result()函数只需从助手消息中提取文本内容。
这对于对话交互来说没有问题，但许多生产场景需要结构化数据，以便下游系统能够可靠地解析。
Source
However, the Agent we built in section 4.6 returns only free-form text. When the LLM finishes reasoning and provides its final answer, _extract_final_result() simply extracts the text content from the assistant message. This works fine for conversational interactions, but many production scenarios require structured data that downstream systems can reliably parse.
考虑一个分析客户反馈的代理。
与其返回“情感为积极，置信度为85%”，你可能需要它返回一个结构化对象，包含情感：“积极”和置信度：0.85。
或者想象一个研究代理，它必须以特定格式返回发现结果，以供报告生成流水线使用。
自由格式的文本需要脆弱的解析逻辑，每当LLM以不同方式表述时，这种逻辑就可能失效。
Source
Consider an agent that analyzes customer feedback. Instead of returning "The sentiment is positive with a confidence of 85%", you might need it to return a structured object with sentiment: "positive" and confidence: 0.85. Or imagine a research agent that must return findings in a specific format for a report generation pipeline. Free-form text would require fragile parsing logic that could break whenever the LLM phrases things differently.
为此，我们将为Agent添加结构化输出能力。
本练习有两个目的：通过修改其核心方法来加深你对Agent架构的理解，并学习一种为Agent添加新功能的模式。
Source
To address this, we'll add structured output capability to our Agent. This exercise serves two purposes: you'll reinforce your understanding of the Agent architecture by modifying its core methods, and you'll learn a pattern for extending agents with new features.
4.7.1 方法：工具作为输出格式化器
Source
4.7.1 The approach: Tools as output formatters
关键洞察在于，我们可以利用现有的工具调用基础设施来强制执行结构化输出。
我们不是让大语言模型生成自由文本，然后再尝试将其解析为某种结构，而是创建一个特殊的工具，该工具接受我们期望的输出模式作为其输入。
当智能体需要提供最终答案时，它会调用这个工具并传入结构正确的数据，从而保证类型安全和格式合规。
Source
The key insight is that we can leverage our existing tool-calling infrastructure to enforce structured outputs. Instead of having the LLM generate free text and then trying to parse it into a structure, we create a special tool that accepts our desired output schema as its input. When the agent needs to provide its final answer, it calls this tool with properly structured data, guaranteeing type safety and format compliance.
这种方法具有多个优势。
首先，它复用了我们现有的工具调用机制，保持了实现的简洁性和一致性。
其次，它利用了大语言模型在工具调用方面的广泛训练，以确保格式正确。
大语言模型已经知道如何生成符合模式的合法JSON；我们只需提供一个与我们期望输出结构相匹配的模式即可。
Source
This approach has several advantages. First, it reuses our existing tool-calling mechanism, keeping the implementation simple and consistent. Second, it leverages the LLM's extensive training on tool calling to ensure proper formatting. The LLM already knows how to generate valid JSON matching a schema; we simply give it a schema that matches our desired output structure.
该实现需要对五个方法进行修改，每个方法在智能体架构中都扮演着特定角色。
Source
The implementation requires modifications to five methods, each playing a specific role in the Agent's architecture.
让我们逐一实现这些修改。
Source
Let's implement each modification.
4.7.2 修改智能体
Source
4.7.2 Modifying the agent
构造函数变更
Source
Constructor changes
首先，我们在构造函数中添加一个output_type参数。
当提供此参数时，它应该是一个Pydantic模型类，用于定义预期的输出结构。
我们还添加了output_tool_name来跟踪我们动态创建的工具的名称。
Source
First, we add an output_type parameter to the constructor. When provided, this should be a Pydantic model class that defines the expected output structure. We also add output_tool_name to track the name of our dynamically created tool.
清单4.24 带有结构化输出的Agent构造函数
Source
Listing 4.24 Agent constructor with structured output
代码保持原样
class Agent: def __init__( self, model: LlmClient, tools: List[BaseTool] = None, instructions: str = "", max_steps: int = 10, output_type: Optional[Type[BaseModel]] = None, # New parameter ): self.model = model self.instructions = instructions self.max_steps = max_steps self.output_type = output_type self.output_tool_name = None # Will be set if output_type provided self.tools = self._setup_tools(tools or [])
在 _setup_tools() 中动态创建工具
Source
Dynamic tool creation in _setup_tools()
关键逻辑发生在_setup_tools()中。
当指定了output_type时，我们会动态创建一个final_answer工具，该工具接受指定的Pydantic模型作为输入。
这个工具只是简单地返回它接收到的任何结构化数据，但通过将其设为工具，我们确保LLM必须按照我们的模式来格式化其响应。
Source
The key logic happens in _setup_tools(). When an output_type is specified, we dynamically create a final_answer tool that accepts the specified Pydantic model as its input. This tool simply returns whatever structured data it receives, but by making it a tool, we ensure the LLM must format its response according to our schema.
请注意，我们在工具定义中使用了Python的闭包来捕获self.output_type。
我们之前实现的@tool装饰器会自动处理Pydantic模型验证，确保任何对final_answer的调用都必须提供符合我们模式的数据。
Source
Notice how we use Python's closure to capture self.output_type in the tool definition. The @tool decorator we implemented earlier automatically handles the Pydantic model validation, ensuring that any call to final_answer must provide data matching our schema.
清单4.25 动态输出工具创建
Source
Listing 4.25 Dynamic output tool creation
代码保持原样
def _setup_tools(self, tools: List[BaseTool]) -> List[BaseTool]: if self.output_type is not None: @tool( name="final_answer", description="Return the final structured answer matching the required schema." ) def final_answer(output: self.output_type) -> self.output_type: return output tools = list(tools) # Create a copy to avoid modifying the original tools.append(final_answer) self.output_tool_name = "final_answer" return tools
在 _prepare_llm_request() 中强制使用工具
Source
Forcing tool usage in _prepare_llm_request()
当需要结构化输出时，我们需要确保智能体实际使用final_answer工具，而不是提供自由文本响应。
OpenAI API和大多数其他提供商都支持tool_choice参数，可以强制模型使用工具。
我们修改_prepare_llm_request()函数来适当地设置这个参数。
Source
When structured output is required, we need to ensure the agent actually uses the final_answer tool instead of providing a free-text response. The OpenAI API and most other providers support a tool_choice parameter that can force the model to use tools. We modify _prepare_llm_request() to set this appropriately.
逻辑很简单：如果我们有一个输出工具（意味着需要结构化输出），我们就设置 tool_choice="required" 来强制 LLM 使用工具。
否则，我们就回退到原始行为。
Source
The logic is straightforward: if we have an output tool (meaning structured output is needed), we set tool_choice="required" to force the LLM to use a tool. Otherwise, we fall back to the original behavior.
清单4.26 强制使用工具以获取结构化输出
Source
Listing 4.26 Forcing tool usage for structured output
代码保持原样
def _prepare_llm_request(self, context: ExecutionContext) -> LlmRequest: flat_contents = [] for event in context.events: flat_contents.extend(event.content) # Determine tool choice strategy if self.output_tool_name: tool_choice = "required" # Force tool usage for structured output elif self.tools: tool_choice = "auto" else: tool_choice = None return LlmRequest( instructions=[self.instructions] if self.instructions else [], contents=flat_contents, tools=self.tools, tool_choice=tool_choice, )
在_is_final_response()中检测完成状态
Source
Detecting completion in _is_final_response()
为了正确检测代理何时生成最终结构化输出，我们修改了_is_final_response()函数。
当需要结构化输出时，我们寻找final_answer工具的成功结果。
只有当这个特定工具成功返回时，我们才认为代理的工作已完成。
对于自由文本响应，我们保持原始行为。
Source
To properly detect when the agent has produced its final structured output, we modify _is_final_response(). When structured output is required, we look for a successful result from our final_answer tool. Only when this specific tool returns successfully do we consider the agent's work complete. For free-text responses, we maintain the original behavior.
清单4.27 检测结构化输出完成情况
Source
Listing 4.27 Detecting structured output completion
代码保持原样
def _is_final_response(self, event: Event) -> bool: if self.output_tool_name: # For structured output: check if final_answer tool succeeded for item in event.content: if (isinstance(item, ToolResult) and item.name == self.output_tool_name and item.status == "success"): return True return False # Original logic for free-text responses has_tool_calls = any(isinstance(c, ToolCall) for c in event.content) has_tool_results = any(isinstance(c, ToolResult) for c in event.content) return not has_tool_calls and not has_tool_results
提取结构化结果
Source
Extracting structured results
最后，我们更新_extract_final_result()方法，以从工具结果中提取结构化数据。
当指定了必需输出工具时，我们查找其成功执行的情况，并返回经过验证的Pydantic模型实例。
这为调用代码提供了一个强类型对象来操作，而不是原始文本。
Source
Finally, we update _extract_final_result() to extract structured data from tool results. When a required output tool was specified, we look for its successful execution and return the validated Pydantic model instance. This gives the calling code a strongly-typed object to work with rather than raw text.
清单4.28 提取结构化结果
Source
Listing 4.28 Extracting structured results
代码保持原样
def _extract_final_result(self, event: Event) -> str | BaseModel: if self.output_tool_name: # Extract structured output from final_answer tool result for item in event.content: if (isinstance(item, ToolResult) and item.name == self.output_tool_name and item.status == "success" and item.content): return item.content[0] # Original logic for free-text responses for item in event.content: if isinstance(item, Message) and item.role == "assistant": return item.content return None
4.7.3 在实践中使用结构化输出
Source
4.7.3 Using structured output in practice
完成这些修改后，使用结构化输出就变得简单直接了。
以下是如何构建一个分析客户反馈并返回结构化情感数据的智能体。
Source
With these modifications in place, using structured output becomes straightforward. Here's how you might build an agent that analyzes customer feedback and returns structured sentiment data.
清单4.29 在实践中使用结构化输出
Source
Listing 4.29 Using structured output in practice
代码保持原样
from pydantic import BaseModel from typing import Literal, List class SentimentAnalysis(BaseModel): sentiment: Literal["positive", "negative", "neutral"] confidence: float key_phrases: List[str] agent = Agent( model=LlmClient(model="gpt-5-mini"), tools=[], instructions="Analyze the sentiment of the provided text.", output_type=SentimentAnalysis ) result = await agent.run("This product exceeded my expectations! Highly recommend.") print(f"Sentiment: {result.sentiment}") # "positive" print(f"Confidence: {result.confidence}") # 0.92 print(f"Key phrases: {result.key_phrases}") # ["exceeded expectations", "highly recommend"]
智能体处理输入信息，分析情感倾向，并在准备就绪时调用final_answer工具，传入一个结构正确的SentimentAnalysis对象。
返回类型是Pydantic模型本身而非字符串，因此您可以直接访问其字段，并享有完整的类型安全保障。
Source
The agent processes the input, reasons about the sentiment, and when ready to respond, calls the final_answer tool with a properly structured SentimentAnalysis object. The return type is the Pydantic model itself, not a string, so you can access fields directly with full type safety.
这一模式可以自然地扩展到更复杂的场景中。
你可以为研究摘要、数据提取结果或应用程序所需的任何结构化格式定义输出模式。
通过将结构化输出集成到我们现有的工具调用机制中，我们在不增加智能体核心逻辑复杂性的前提下，增强了类型安全和格式保证。
Source
This pattern extends naturally to more complex scenarios. You could define output schemas for research summaries, data extraction results, or any structured format your application requires. By integrating structured output through our existing tool-calling mechanism, we've added powerful type safety and format guarantees without complicating the agent's core logic.
4.8 使用GAIA基准进行测试
Source
4.8 Testing with the GAIA benchmark
在第2章中，我们直接在GAIA问题上测试了LLM，并观察到了它们的局限性。
大多数问题需要LLM不具备的信息，导致准确率较低。
现在，让我们看看我们的智能体在配备工具后表现如何。
Source
In chapter 2, we tested LLMs directly on GAIA problems and observed their limitations. Most problems required information that the LLM didn't have, leading to low accuracy. Now let's see how our Agent performs when equipped with tools.
4.8.1 从LLM到智能体
Source
4.8.1 From LLM to agent
评估设置基本与第2章保持一致。
我们复用了GaiaOutput、gaia_prompt、is_correct()以及实验运行器的结构。
关键区别在于解决问题的对象：不再是直接调用LLM，而是使用带有工具的Agent。
Source
The evaluation setup remains largely the same as in chapter 2. We reuse GaiaOutput, gaia_prompt, is_correct(), and the experiment runner structure. The key difference is what solves each problem: instead of a direct LLM call, we now use an Agent with tools.
首先，我们从Tavily MCP服务器加载工具，这已在第3章中探讨过。
Source
First, we load tools from the Tavily MCP server, which we explored in chapter 3.
清单 4.30 为 GAIA 加载 MCP 工具
Source
Listing 4.30 Loading MCP tools for GAIA

from scratch_agents.tools import load_mcp_tools tavily_connection = { "command": "npx", "args": ["-y", "tavily-mcp@latest"], "env": {"TAVILY_API_KEY": os.getenv("TAVILY_API_KEY")} } mcp_tools = await load_mcp_tools(tavily_connection)
接下来，我们创建一个为GAIA评估配置的智能体。
该智能体接收用于网络搜索的MCP工具，并使用GaiaOutput作为其结构化输出类型。
Source
Next, we create an Agent configured for GAIA evaluation. The Agent receives the MCP tools for web search and uses GaiaOutput as its structured output type.
清单 4.31 创建 GAIA 评估智能体
Source
Listing 4.31 Creating GAIA evaluation agent
代码保持原样
def create_gaia_agent(model: str, tools: list) -> Agent: return Agent( model=LlmClient(model=model), tools=tools, instructions=gaia_prompt, output_type=GaiaOutput, max_steps=15, )
核心变化在于solve_problem。
在第2章中直接调用acompletion()，现在我们调用agent.run()。
返回的AgentResult包含输出和完整的执行上下文。
Source
The core change is in solve_problem. Where chapter 2 called acompletion() directly, we now call agent.run(). The returned AgentResult contains both the output and the full execution context.
清单4.32 使用代理解决问题
Source
Listing 4.32 Solving problems with agent
代码保持原样
SEMAPHORE = asyncio.Semaphore(3) async def solve_problem(agent: Agent, question: str) -> AgentResult: async with SEMAPHORE: return await agent.run(question)
现在信号量限制的是并发Agent执行，而非单个LLM调用。
每次Agent执行可能涉及多次内部LLM调用，因为它会进行推理并使用工具，但我们限制并行问题解决以避免压垮API。
Source
The semaphore now limits concurrent Agent executions rather than individual LLM calls. Each Agent execution may involve multiple internal LLM calls as it reasons and uses tools, but we limit parallel problem-solving to avoid overwhelming the APIs.
评估流程的其余部分，包括evaluate_single()和run_experiment()，遵循与第2章相同的结构。
唯一的调整是通过result.output访问答案，而不是直接解析LLM响应。
完整实现请参见GitHub仓库。
Source
The rest of the evaluation pipeline, including evaluate_single() and run_experiment(), follows the same structure as chapter 2. The only adjustment is accessing the answer via result.output instead of parsing the LLM response directly. See the GitHub repository for the complete implementation.
