# Reset workspace to clean state reset_workspace() # Select a problem with zip file attachment zip_problems = [p for p in problems_with_files if p['file_name'].endswith('.zip')] problem = zip_problems[1] file_path = WORK_DIR / problem['file_name'] # Construct prompt including file location prompt = f"""{problem['Question']} The attached file is located at: {file_path} """ print(prompt)
现在让我们运行代理，并观察文件结构探索过程。
Source
Now let's run the agent and observe the file structure exploration process.
清单5.23 在压缩文件问题上运行智能体
Source
Listing 5.23 Running agent on zip file problem
代码保持原样
response = await agent.run(prompt) print(response)
智能体的探索过程遵循系统化的模式。
首先，它使用unzip_file函数提取压缩文件。
接着，它调用list_files函数来检查文件夹结构。
出现了两个文件：Job Listing.pdf和Applicants.xlsx。
仅凭文件名就能清晰地揭示它们之间的关系——一个描述职位要求，另一个列出候选人。
Source
The agent's exploration process follows a systematic pattern. First, it extracts the zip file using unzip_file. Then it calls list_files to examine the folder structure. Two files emerge: Job Listing.pdf and Applicants.xlsx. The filenames alone reveal their relationship clearly —one describes the job requirements, the other lists candidates.
智能体首先使用read_media_file分析PDF文件，提取资格要求。
然后，它通过read_file读取Excel文件，审查所有申请人的数据。
最后，它将资格要求与每位候选人进行交叉比对，以找到答案。
Source
The agent first analyzes the PDF using read_media_file to extract the qualification requirements. Then it reads the Excel file with read_file to review all applicants' data. Finally, it cross-references the requirements against each candidate to find the answer.
关键观察在于，智能体无需复杂搜索算法即可导航文件结构。
文件名和扩展名可作为自然的提示线索。
“职位列表”提供了需要匹配的要求，而“申请人”则指明了待筛选的候选人数据。
智能体利用这些命名惯例和格式线索，高效定位解决问题所需的信息。
Source
The key observation is that the agent navigates file structures without complex search algorithms. Filenames and extensions serve as natural hints. "Job Listing" suggests requirements to match against, while "Applicants" indicates candidate data to filter. The agent uses these naming conventions and format cues to efficiently locate the information needed to solve the problem.
5.4 通过回调扩展智能体
Source
5.4 Extending agents with callbacks
我们在第4章实现的Agent提供了执行工具和接收结果的基本功能。
然而，在实际部署中，会出现需要先获得用户批准才能执行工具，或者压缩搜索结果以高效管理上下文的情况。
我们需要修改Agent的核心逻辑来满足这些需求吗？
Source
The Agent we implemented in chapter 4 provides basic functionality for executing tools and receiving results. However, in real-world deployments, situations arise where you need to obtain user approval before executing a tool, or compress search results to manage context efficiently. Do we need to modify the Agent's core logic to address these requirements?
幸运的是，我们不需要这样做。
使用Callback模式，我们可以在不触及Agent核心代码的情况下扩展其行为。
在本节中，我们将为Agent添加一个Callback机制，并通过两个实际示例学习如何使用它。
Source
Fortunately, we don't. Using the Callback pattern, we can extend the Agent's behavior without touching its core code. In this section, we'll add a Callback mechanism to the Agent and learn how to use it through two practical examples.
5.4.1 智能体扩展的必要性
Source
5.4.1 The need for agent extension
让我们从上下文工程的角度来思考智能体的扩展点。
在智能体调用大语言模型并执行工具的过程中，我们可以在多个环节进行干预。
Source
Let's consider extension points for our agent from a Context Engineering perspective. During the process of the agent calling the LLM and executing tools, there are several points where we can intervene.
在调用大语言模型之前进行干预，允许我们向上下文中注入额外信息、压缩旧消息或检查缓存响应。
大语言模型响应后，我们可以验证或后处理结果。
工具执行前，我们可以请求用户批准危险操作或返回缓存结果。
工具执行后，我们可以压缩结果或屏蔽敏感信息。
最后，在整个执行完成后，我们可以保存对话或生成摘要。
Source
Intervening before an LLM call allows us to inject additional information into the context, compress old messages, or check for cached responses. After the LLM responds, we can validate or post-process the results. Before tool execution, we can request user approval for dangerous operations or return cached results. After tool execution, we can compress results or mask sensitive information. Finally, after the entire execution completes, we can save the conversation or generate summaries.
这一切都是通过回调函数实现的。
回调函数是用户定义的函数，在特定执行点被调用。
它们使我们能够在不修改智能体核心逻辑的情况下添加各种功能。
Source
All of this is possible through Callbacks. Callbacks are user-defined functions that are invoked at specific execution points. They enable us to add various capabilities without modifying the agent's core logic.
我们将使用的回调类型如下，如图5.7所示。
Source
The types of Callbacks we'll use are as follows, as shown in figure 5.7.
before_llm_callback和after_llm_callback分别在LLM调用之前和之后执行。
它们用于操作上下文或拦截响应。
Source
before_llm_callback and after_llm_callback execute before and after LLM calls. They're used for manipulating context or intercepting responses.
before_tool_callback 和 after_tool_callback 分别在工具执行前和执行后运行。
这些就是本节我们将重点关注的回调函数。
它们用于批准工具执行或压缩结果。
Source
before_tool_callback and after_tool_callback execute before and after tool execution. These are the callbacks we'll focus on in this section. They're used for approving tool execution or compressing results.
after_run_callback 在智能体运行完全结束后执行。
它可用于将会话内容保存到内存中，我们将在第6章介绍内存时使用它。
Source
after_run_callback executes after the entire agent run completes. It can be used to save conversation content to memory, and we'll use it when we cover Memory in chapter 6.
在本节中，我们将实现并利用与本章节主题直接相关的工具回调。
其余的回调遵循相同的模式，完整代码可在GitHub仓库中获取。
Source
In this section, we'll implement and utilize tool callbacks that are directly related to this chapter’s topic. The remaining callbacks follow the same pattern, and the complete code is available in the GitHub repository.
图5.7展示了在智能体执行流程中插入回调函数的各个节点。LLM回调函数在think()方法执行前后被调用，而工具回调函数则在act()方法内每次工具执行前后被调用。
Source
Figure 5.7 Points where Callbacks are inserted in the agent execution flow. LLM callbacks are called before and after think(), and tool callbacks are called before and after each tool execution within act().
5.4.2 实现工具回调
Source
5.4.2 Implementing tool callbacks
现在，让我们为Agent类添加工具回调支持。
首先，我们定义回调的行为方式。
Source
Now let's add tool callback support to the Agent class. First, we define how callbacks behave.
before_tool_callback(context, tool_call)在工具执行前被调用。
如果此回调返回一个值，则跳过实际工具执行，并使用该值作为结果。
如果它返回None，则实际工具会执行。
Source
before_tool_callback(context, tool_call) is called before a tool executes. If this callback returns a value, the actual tool execution is skipped and that value is used as the result. If it returns None, the actual tool executes.
after_tool_callback(context, tool_result) 在工具执行后被调用。
如果此回调返回一个值，它将替换原始结果。
如果返回 None，则保留原始结果。
Source
after_tool_callback(context, tool_result) is called after a tool executes. If this callback returns a value, it replaces the original result. If it returns None, the original result is preserved.
当注册了多个回调函数时，执行会在第一个返回非None值的回调处停止。
这被称为提前退出模式。
Source
When multiple callbacks are registered, execution stops at the first callback that returns a non-None value. This is called the Early Exit pattern.
我们修改 Agent 构造函数以添加回调参数。
它接受两个列表：before_tool_callbacks 和 after_tool_callbacks。
如果未提供回调，它们会被初始化为空列表，以便后续代码可以无需进行 None 检查即可遍历它们。
Source
We modify the Agent constructor to add callback parameters. It accepts two lists: before_tool_callbacks and after_tool_callbacks. If callbacks aren't provided, they're initialized as empty lists so that subsequent code can iterate over them without None checks.
清单5.24 向Agent添加回调参数
Source
Listing 5.24 Adding callback parameters to Agent
代码保持原样
class Agent: def __init__( self, model: LlmClient, tools: List[BaseTool] = None, instructions: str = "", max_steps: int = 10, output_type: Optional[Type[BaseModel]] = None, before_tool_callbacks: List[Callable] = None, after_tool_callbacks: List[Callable] = None, ): self.model = model self.instructions = instructions self.max_steps = max_steps self.tools = self._setup_tools(tools or []) self.output_type = output_type # Initialize callback lists self.before_tool_callbacks = before_tool_callbacks or [] self.after_tool_callbacks = after_tool_callbacks or []
接下来，我们重构act()方法。
原始代码直接为每个工具调用执行工具，但现在它被分为三个阶段。
Source
Next, we refactor the act() method. The original code executed tools directly for each tool_call, but now it's divided into three stages.
在第一阶段，我们遍历before_tool_callbacks并执行每个回调。
如果回调返回非None值，我们会将该值存储在tool_response中并跳出循环。
我们使用inspect.isawaitable()来支持异步回调。
Source
In the first stage, we iterate through before_tool_callbacks and execute each callback. If a callback returns a non-None value, we store that value in tool_response and break out of the loop. We use inspect.isawaitable() to support asynchronous callbacks as well.
在第二阶段，仅当tool_response仍为None时，我们才执行实际工具。
如果回调已提供结果，则跳过此阶段。
Source
In the second stage, we execute the actual tool only if tool_response is still None. If a callback has already provided a result, this stage is skipped.
在第三阶段，我们遍历after_tool_callbacks。
如果回调函数返回一个新的ToolResult，它会替换原始结果。
Source
In the third stage, we iterate through after_tool_callbacks. If a callback returns a new ToolResult, it replaces the original result.
清单5.25 使用回调重构act()方法
Source
Listing 5.25 Refactoring act() method with callbacks
代码保持原样
import inspect async def act( self, context: ExecutionContext, tool_calls: List[ToolCall] ) -> List[ToolResult]: tools_dict = {tool.name: tool for tool in self.tools} results = [] for tool_call in tool_calls: if tool_call.name not in tools_dict: raise ValueError(f"Tool '{tool_call.name}' not found") tool = tools_dict[tool_call.name] tool_response = None status = "success" # Stage 1: Execute before_tool_callbacks for callback in self.before_tool_callbacks: result = callback(context, tool_call) if inspect.isawaitable(result): result = await result if result is not None: tool_response = result break # Stage 2: Execute actual tool only if callback didn't provide a result if tool_response is None: try: tool_response = await tool(context, **tool_call.arguments) except Exception as e: tool_response = str(e) status = "error" tool_result = ToolResult( tool_call_id=tool_call.tool_call_id, name=tool_call.name, status=status, content=[tool_response], ) # Stage 3: Execute after_tool_callbacks for callback in self.after_tool_callbacks: result = callback(context, tool_result) if inspect.isawaitable(result): result = await result if result is not None: tool_result = result break results.append(tool_result) return results
5.4.3 人在回路：工具执行审批
Source
5.4.3 Human in the loop: Tool execution approval
虽然代理自动执行任务效率很高，但有时可能存在风险。
对于文件删除、邮件发送或数据库修改等敏感操作，应在执行前要求用户确认。
如图5.8所示，人机协同模式正是为这类场景设计的。
Source
While it's efficient for agents to perform tasks automatically, this can sometimes be risky. Sensitive operations like file deletion, email sending, or database modifications should require user confirmation before execution. The Human in the Loop pattern is designed for exactly these situations, as shown in figure 5.8.
图5.8展示了人机协同模式中的工具执行审批流程。当用户请求“清理项目文件夹”时，代理在尝试调用delete_file工具时会暂停操作，并向用户请求审批。
Source
Figure 5.8 Tool execution approval flow in the Human in the Loop pattern. When a user requests "Clean up the project folder," the agent pauses when it tries to call the delete_file tool and requests approval from the user.
让我们以文件删除工具为例，这是一个需要批准的危险工具。
这是一个虚拟实现，仅返回消息而不实际删除文件。
Source
Let's create a file deletion tool as an example of a dangerous tool that requires approval. This is a dummy implementation that only returns a message without actually deleting files.
清单 5.26 实现 delete_file 工具
Source
Listing 5.26 Implementing delete_file tool
代码保持原样
@tool def delete_file(file_path: str) -> str: """Deletes a file. This action cannot be undone.""" # Only returns message instead of actual deletion (for demo) return f"File {file_path} has been deleted."
现在，让我们实现一个回调函数，仅在调用危险工具（如delete_file）时请求批准。
回调函数首先检查工具名称是否在需要批准的工具列表中。
如果不是，则返回None以允许立即执行。
如果是，回调函数会显示工具信息并等待用户输入。
输入'y'会返回None以允许实际执行工具，而任何其他输入都会返回拒绝消息以跳过工具执行。
Source
Now let's implement a callback that requests approval only when dangerous tools like delete_file are called. The callback first checks if the tool name is in the list of tools requiring approval. If not, it returns None to allow immediate execution. If it is, the callback displays the tool information and waits for user input. Entering 'y' returns None to allow actual tool execution, while any other input returns a rejection message to skip the tool execution.
清单5.27 实现批准回调
Source
Listing 5.27 Implementing approval callback
代码保持原样
# List of dangerous tools requiring approval DANGEROUS_TOOLS = ["delete_file", "send_email", "execute_sql"] def approval_callback(context: ExecutionContext, tool_call: ToolCall): """Requests user approval before executing dangerous tools.""" # Execute immediately if not a dangerous tool if tool_call.name not in DANGEROUS_TOOLS: return None print(f"\n⚠️ Dangerous tool execution requested") print(f"Tool: {tool_call.name}") print(f"Arguments: {tool_call.arguments}") response = input("Do you want to execute? (y/n): ").lower().strip() if response == 'y': print("✅ Approved. Executing...\n") return None # Proceed with actual tool execution else: print("❌ Denied. Skipping execution.\n") return f"User denied execution of {tool_call.name}"
回调函数的返回值是关键。
返回None会导致act()方法执行实际工具。
返回字符串则将该字符串作为工具结果，实际工具不会执行。
LLM可以在下一步看到这个拒绝消息，并尝试不同的方法。
Source
The callback's return value is key. Returning None causes the act() method to execute the actual tool. Returning a string uses that as the tool result, and the actual tool doesn't execute. The LLM can see this rejection message in the next step and try a different approach.
让我们将这个回调应用于一个智能体。
像list_files或read_file这样的安全工具无需批准即可执行，而只有在调用delete_file时才会请求批准。
Source
Let's apply this callback to an agent. Safe tools like list_files or read_file execute without approval, while approval is requested only when delete_file is called.
清单 5.28 创建带有批准回调的智能体
Source
Listing 5.28 Creating agent with approval callback
代码保持原样
agent = Agent( model=LlmClient(model="gpt-5"), tools=[list_files, read_file, delete_file], instructions="You are a helpful assistant that can explore and manage files.", max_steps=20, before_tool_callbacks=[approval_callback], )
执行时，你会看到以下流程。list_files 无需批准即可执行，因为它不在危险工具列表中。
当调用 delete_file 时，批准提示会出现。
Source
When executed, you'll see the following flow. list_files executes without approval since it's not in the dangerous tools list. When delete_file is called, the approval prompt appears.
5.4.4 压缩搜索结果
Source
5.4.4 Compressing search results
在5.3.4节的练习中，我们确认了网络搜索结果可能消耗超过37,000个token，而通过向量搜索仅提取相关部分可以节省超过99%，将其减少至304个token。
然而，每次手动执行此过程都相当繁琐。
让我们在智能体层面使用after_tool_callback来自动化这一过程。
Source
In the exercise in section 5.3.4, we confirmed that web search results can consume over 37,000 tokens, and extracting only relevant portions through vector search can save over 99%, reducing it to 304 tokens. However, performing this process manually every time is cumbersome. Let's automate this at the agent level using after_tool_callback.
这个想法很简单。
网络搜索工具执行后，如果结果过长，我们会使用向量搜索来提取仅与查询相关的部分。
此回调仅适用于搜索工具，并原封不动地传递其他工具的结果。
Source
The idea is simple. After the web search tool executes, if the result is too long, we use vector search to extract only the portions relevant to the query. This callback applies only to the search tool and passes through results from other tools unchanged.
回调流程如下。
首先，我们检查工具名称，如果不是search_web，则返回None。
如果是搜索工具，我们会检查结果长度，若其字符数少于2000，则直接返回原结果。
对于较长的搜索结果，我们会查找对应的查询，并执行我们在5.3节中实现的文本分块和向量搜索。
最后，我们返回一个仅包含前3个分块的新ToolResult。
Source
The callback flow is as follows. First, we check the tool name and return None if it's not search_web. If it is the search tool, we check the result length and return it unchanged if it's under 2,000 characters. For long results, we find the query for that search and perform the chunking and vector search we implemented in section 5.3. Finally, we return a new ToolResult containing only the top 3 chunks.
清单5.29 实现搜索压缩器回调
Source
Listing 5.29 Implementing search compressor callback
代码保持原样
def search_compressor(context: ExecutionContext, tool_result: ToolResult): """Callback that compresses web search results.""" # Pass through unchanged if not a search tool if tool_result.name != "search_web": return None original_content = tool_result.content[0] # No compression needed if result is short enough if len(original_content) < 2000: return None # Extract search query matching the tool_call_id query = _extract_search_query(context, tool_result.tool_call_id) if not query: return None # Use functions implemented in section 5.3 chunks = fixed_length_chunking(original_content, chunk_size=500, overlap=50) embeddings = get_embeddings(chunks) results = vector_search(query, chunks, embeddings, top_k=3) # Create compressed result compressed = "\n\n".join([r['chunk'] for r in results]) return ToolResult( tool_call_id=tool_result.tool_call_id, name=tool_result.name, status="success", content=[compressed] )
_extract_search_query辅助函数从ExecutionContext中查找特定搜索调用的查询。
由于大语言模型可以并行请求多次搜索，因此通过tool_call_id精确匹配比仅查找最近一次搜索更为安全。
我们遍历事件，寻找类型为ToolCall、名称为search_web且ID匹配的项，然后返回查询参数。
Source
The _extract_search_query helper function finds the query for a specific search call from the ExecutionContext. Since the LLM can request multiple searches in parallel, it's safer to match exactly by tool_call_id rather than simply finding the most recent search. We iterate through events looking for items that are ToolCall type, have the name search_web, and match the ID, then return the query argument.
清单 5.30 从上下文中提取搜索查询
Source
Listing 5.30 Extracting search query from context
代码保持原样
def _extract_search_query(context: ExecutionContext, tool_call_id: str) -> str: """Extracts the search query for a specific tool_call_id from context.""" for event in context.events: for item in event.content: if (isinstance(item, ToolCall) and item.name == "search_web" and item.tool_call_id == tool_call_id): return item.arguments.get("query", "") return ""
现在，让我们创建一个同时应用这两个回调的智能体。
我们在before_tool_callbacks中注册批准回调，并在after_tool_callbacks中注册压缩回调。
Source
Now let's create an agent that applies both callbacks together. We register the approval callback in before_tool_callbacks and the compression callback in after_tool_callbacks.
清单 5.31 创建具有多个回调的智能体
Source
Listing 5.31 Creating agent with multiple callbacks
代码保持原样
agent = Agent( model=LlmClient(model="gpt-5"), tools=[search_web, list_files, read_file, delete_file], instructions="You are a helpful assistant that can search the web and " "explore files to answer questions.", max_steps=20, before_tool_callbacks=[approval_callback], after_tool_callbacks=[search_compressor], )
当执行网络搜索时，搜索结果会自动被压缩。
我们在5.3.4节中手动完成的工作，现在会在智能体执行过程中自动应用。
我们无需修改智能体的核心逻辑，就能实现相同的令牌节省和噪声减少效果。
Source
When web search executes, results are automatically compressed. The work we performed manually in section 5.3.4 is now applied automatically during agent execution. We achieve the same token savings and noise reduction benefits without modifying the agent's core logic at all.
关键见解
Source
Key insights
在本节中，我们了解到可以通过回调模式扩展智能体行为，而无需修改其核心逻辑。
Source
In this section, we learned that we can extend agent behavior without modifying its core logic through the Callback pattern.
before_tool_callback 在工具执行前进行干预。
如果它返回一个值，则跳过实际执行，并使用该值作为结果。
它可以用于人工介入审批、缓存检查、输入验证等多种场景。
Source
before_tool_callback intervenes before tool execution. If it returns a value, actual execution is skipped and that value is used as the result. It can be used for Human in the Loop approval, cache checking, input validation, and more.
after_tool_callback 在工具执行后进行干预。
如果它返回一个值，就会替换原始结果。
它可用于搜索结果压缩、敏感信息屏蔽、结果格式转换等多种用途。
Source
after_tool_callback intervenes after tool execution. If it returns a value, it replaces the original result. It can be used for search result compression, sensitive information masking, result format conversion, and more.
通过组合多个回调函数，我们可以清晰地处理复杂需求。
每个回调函数都有单一职责，可以根据需要添加或移除。
Source
By combining multiple callbacks, we can handle complex requirements cleanly. Each callback has a single responsibility and can be added or removed as needed.
本节中实现的人工介入（Human in the Loop）是同步的。
整个程序会在input()函数等待用户输入时阻塞。
这在本地环境测试时没问题，但在Web服务或API服务器中不能使用这种方法。
在第6章中，我们将实现异步的人工介入，此时智能体不会中途暂停，而是通过向用户发送响应来请求批准，并在收到用户响应后恢复执行。
Source
The Human in the Loop implementation in this section operates synchronously. The entire program blocks while the input() function waits for user input. This is fine for testing in a local environment, but you can't use this approach in web services or API servers. In chapter 6, we'll implement asynchronous Human in the Loop where the agent doesn't pause in the middle but instead requests approval through a response to the user and resumes execution when the user's response arrives.
在第六章中，我们还将使用after_run_callback。
我们将使用这个回调在对话结束后将对话内容保存到记忆库中。
你将继续看到回调模式如何作为扩展智能体功能的核心机制被运用。
Source
We'll also use after_run_callback in chapter 6. We'll use this callback to save conversation content to Memory after a conversation ends. You'll continue to see how the callback pattern is utilized as a core mechanism for extending agent functionality.
5.5 总结
Source
5.5 Summary
内部数据需要与网络搜索不同的处理方式。
单个文件可以直接读入上下文，但多个文件需要探索，而大规模数据则需要搜索机制来提取仅相关的部分。
Source
Internal data requires different approaches than web search. Single files can be read directly into context, but multiple files need exploration, and large-scale data requires search mechanisms to extract only relevant portions.
四种搜索方法满足不同需求：关键词搜索用于精确匹配，向量搜索用于语义相似性，图搜索用于关系遍历，以及基于结构的搜索用于导航组织化的文件系统。
生产系统通常结合多种方法。
Source
Four search methods serve different needs: keyword search for exact matching, vector search for semantic similarity, graph search for relationship traversal, and structure-based search for navigating organized file systems. Production systems often combine multiple methods.
向量搜索将文本转换为数值向量，使语义相似性表现为几何距离。
该流程涉及将长文档分块、生成嵌入向量，并通过计算余弦相似度来寻找最相关的内容。
Source
Vector search converts text to numerical vectors where semantic similarity becomes geometric distance. The pipeline involves chunking long documents, generating embeddings, and calculating cosine similarity to find the most relevant content.
基于结构的搜索利用文件系统组织本身作为信息来源。
文件夹名称、文件名称和目录层级提供了有意义的元数据，代理可以通过list_files和read_file等简单工具进行导航。
Source
Structure-based search leverages file system organization as information itself. Folder names, file names, and directory hierarchies provide meaningful metadata that agents can navigate using simple tools like list_files and read_file.
回调模式可在不修改核心逻辑的情况下扩展代理行为。before_tool_callback 支持对危险操作进行人工干预审批，而 after_tool_callback 则支持自动压缩搜索结果。
Source
The Callback pattern extends agent behavior without modifying core logic. before_tool_callback enables Human in the Loop approval for dangerous operations, while after_tool_callback enables automatic compression of search results.
通过搜索进行上下文工程，显著减少了标记使用量。
在我们的练习中，仅提取相关片段就将超过37,000个标记减少至仅304个标记，实现了99%的节省率，同时保留了回答查询所需的信息。
Source
Context engineering through search dramatically reduces token usage. In our exercise, extracting only relevant chunks reduced over 37,000 tokens to just 304 tokens, achieving a 99% savings rate while preserving the information needed to answer the query.

6 Adding memory to your agent
6 为你的智能体添加记忆
