6 Adding memory to your agent
本章涵盖
Source
This chapter covers
记忆在LLM智能体中的作用
Source
The role of memory in LLM agents
通过滑动窗口、压缩和摘要管理上下文增长
Source
Managing context growth with sliding window, compaction, and summarization
为多轮对话实现会话管理
Source
Implementing sessions for multi-turn conversations
构建异步人机协同工作流程
Source
Building asynchronous human-in-the-loop workflows
为跨会话知识保留创建长期记忆
Source
Creating long-term memory for cross-session knowledge retention
记忆正是区分无状态工具与智能助手的关键所在。
如果没有记忆，智能体就无法在同一任务中回忆先前的事件，无法从早期会话继续对话，也无法从过去的经验中学习。
每次交互都需从头开始，迫使用户重复提供上下文，并阻碍智能体随时间推移而改进。
Source
Memory is what separates a stateless tool from an intelligent assistant. Without memory, an agent cannot recall previous events within the same task, continue conversations from earlier sessions, or learn from past experiences. Each interaction starts from scratch, forcing users to repeat context and preventing the agent from improving over time.
本章从三个使用模式探讨记忆功能。
首先，我们实施上下文优化策略，以防止在复杂问题解决过程中出现上下文爆炸。
其次，我们构建Session和SessionManager以维持跨多次交互的对话连续性，并将此架构扩展至支持异步人机协作工作流。
最后，我们创建一个长期记忆系统，该系统通过向量搜索跨会话边界提取、存储和检索知识。
Source
This chapter addresses memory in three usage patterns. First, we implement context optimization strategies to prevent context explosion during complex problem-solving. Second, we build Session and SessionManager to maintain conversation continuity across multiple interactions, extending this architecture to support asynchronous human-in-the-loop workflows. Finally, we create a long-term memory system that extracts, stores, and retrieves knowledge across session boundaries using vector search.
图6.1 书籍结构概览：聚焦第6章。
Source
Figure 6.1 Book structure overview: Chapter 6 in focus.
6.1 智能体记忆的构成
Source
6.1 The anatomy of agent memory
记忆将智能体从一个简单的工具转变为能够学习和适应的智能助手。
没有记忆，即使是最复杂的智能体每次都要从头开始，无法参考之前的对话或从过往经验中学习。
Source
Memory transforms an agent from a simple tool into an intelligent assistant that learns and adapts. Without memory, even the most sophisticated agent starts from scratch every time, unable to reference previous conversations or learn from past experiences.
在本节中，我们审视当前智能体的局限性，区分短期记忆与长期记忆，并进一步根据智能体的使用模式将短期记忆划分为两种类型。
接着，我们阐明第1章中的上下文工程框架如何与记忆相关联。
Source
In this section, we examine the limitations of our current agent, distinguish between short-term and long-term memory, and further divide short-term memory into two patterns based on agent usage. We then clarify how the Context Engineering framework from chapter 1 connects to memory.
6.1.1 当前记忆架构的局限性
Source
6.1.1 Limitations of the current memory architecture
到目前为止开发的代理依赖于原始的ExecutionContext。
它的运作方式很简单：在执行过程中附加所有内容，然后在执行后丢弃所有内容。
虽然这对于简单任务有效，但它缺乏有效管理信息的机制。
Source
The agent developed so far relies on a raw ExecutionContext. It operates simply: append everything during execution, then discard everything after. While this works for simple tasks, it lacks a mechanism to manage information effectively.
考虑两种场景。
首先是空间问题：在解决复杂的GAIA问题时，工具调用结果会迅速累积。
上下文可能超出大语言模型的窗口限制，导致智能体在完成任务前崩溃。
其次是时间问题：作为跨多个对话的个人助手，智能体会忘记会话之间的所有内容。
昨天说过“我是詹姆斯，我是一名营销人员”的用户，今天必须重复这些信息。
Source
Consider two scenarios. First, a problem of space: when solving a complex GAIA problem, tool call results accumulate rapidly. The context can exceed the LLM's window limit, crashing the agent before it finishes. Second, a problem of time: as a personal assistant across multiple conversations, the agent forgets everything between sessions. A user who said "I'm James, I work as a marketer" yesterday must repeat this information today.
这些限制源于缺乏有效的记忆管理机制。
让我们将这些挑战归纳为三个具体问题，并概述相应的解决方案。
Source
These limitations stem from the absence of memory management. Let’s categorize these problems into three distinct challenges and outline our solutions.
当前记忆架构面临的三大挑战
Source
Three challenges of the current memory architecture
在深入探讨挑战之前，让我们先确立三个概念，它们将构成本章所有构建内容的基础。
Source
Before diving into the challenges, let's establish three concepts that form the foundation for everything we'll build in this chapter.
会话是用户与代理之间一次连续、不间断的对话。
可以将其想象为打开一个新的聊天窗口——在该窗口内讨论的所有内容都属于同一个会话。
关闭窗口并在稍后开始新的对话会创建一个新的会话。
Source
A session is a single, continuous conversation between a user and an agent. Think of it as opening a new chat window—everything discussed within that window belongs to the same session. Closing the window and starting a new conversation later creates a new session.
短期记忆存储了迄今为止完成的工作：对话历史、工具调用结果以及中间推理——所有存储在ExecutionContext.events中的内容。
Source
Short-term memory stores the work done so far: conversation history, tool call results, and intermediate reasoning—everything stored in ExecutionContext.events.
长期记忆是指会话结束后仍持续存在的信息。
当用户今天提到“我是营销人员”时，长期记忆能确保代理在下周、即使是在全新的会话中，仍能记住这一信息。
Source
Long-term memory is information that persists after sessions end. When a user mentions "I'm a marketer" today, long-term memory ensures the agent remembers this next week, even in a completely new session.
挑战一：上下文爆炸
Source
Challenge 1: Context explosion
许多智能体仅用于一次性执行。
当我们运行GAIA基准测试时，我们执行一次run()后就终止了。
对于这类情况，我们当前的实现已经足够。
然而，在复杂问题中，多次工具调用可能导致上下文迅速膨胀。
核心挑战在于：“如何在当前执行过程中压缩上下文？”
Source
Many agents are used for one-off execution. When we ran the GAIA benchmark, we executed run() once and terminated. For such cases, our current implementation is sufficient. However, in complex problems, multiple tool calls can cause context to grow rapidly. The core challenge: "How do we compress context during the current execution?"
挑战二：缺乏对话连续性
Source
Challenge 2: Lack of conversation continuity
当智能体收到用户的多个请求（如对话式聊天机器人），或因某些工具执行需要用户批准而暂停时，会发生什么？
我们如何在多次调用run()时保持状态？
Source
What happens when an agent receives multiple requests from users, like a conversational chatbot, or needs to pause because certain tool executions require user approval? How do we maintain state across multiple run() calls?
如果没有适当的会话管理，每次run()调用都是独立运行的。
对话会中断。
图6.2对此进行了说明：在左侧，没有会话的情况下，询问完Project Alpha后，后续请求会让智能体不清楚指的是哪个项目。
在右侧，有了会话后，上下文得以保留，智能体能正确理解所指内容。
Source
Without proper session management, each run() call operates independently. The conversation breaks. Figure 6.2 illustrates this: on the left, without a session, a follow-up request after asking about Project Alpha, leaves the agent unaware of which project is meant. On the right, with a session, context is preserved and the agent correctly understands the reference.
图6.2 无会话（左侧）中，每次run()都会创建一个新的ExecutionContext，并在完成后丢弃。而有会话（右侧）时，多次run()调用共享同一个Session，从而维持对话的连续性。
Source
Figure 6.2 Without Session (left), each run() creates a new ExecutionContext that's discarded after completion. With Session (right), multiple run() calls share the same Session, maintaining conversation continuity.
在Web服务中，服务器以无状态方式运行。
每个HTTP请求都是独立处理的，服务器内存在请求结束时被释放。
当用户在10分钟后发送另一条消息时，这便是一个新的请求。
Source
In web services, servers operate statelessly. Each HTTP request is processed independently, and server memory is released when the request ends. When a user sends another message 10 minutes later, it's a new request.
维持对话上下文需要明确的工作：为每个对话分配唯一的session_id，在run()结束时将会话状态保存到外部存储，并在下一次run()开始时加载之前的状态。
Source
Maintaining conversation context requires explicit work: assign a unique session_id to each conversation, save session state to external storage when run() ends, and load the previous state when the next run() starts.
挑战3：缺乏持久性知识
Source
Challenge 3: Lack of persistent knowledge
考虑一个个性化的AI助手。
像“我是一名营销人员”这样的信息，今天分享后，下周甚至在新对话中也应该被记住。
会话结束后，哪些信息应该保留，以及如何保留？
Source
Consider a personalized AI assistant. Information like "I'm a marketer" shared today should be remembered next week—even in a new conversation. What should survive after a session ends, and how?
这与挑战2有根本性的不同。
对话连续性在相同的session_id内保持上下文；你可以关闭并重新打开聊天窗口，只要session相同，上下文就会持续存在。
持久性知识在不同session_id之间共享信息——即使开启全新的对话，智能体也能记住用户。
Source
This differs fundamentally from challenge 2. Conversation continuity maintains context within the same session_id; you can close and reopen the chat window, and context persists as long as it's the same session. Persistent knowledge shares information across different session_ids—the agent remembers the user when starting a brand new conversation.
图6.3展示了这一过程的工作原理。
当会话1结束时，系统会检查是否有值得保留的信息。
如果有，这些知识就会被存储在长期记忆中。
当新会话开始时，智能体会根据需要搜索并检索相关信息。
Source
Figure 6.3 shows how this works. When session 1 ends, the system examines whether any information is worth preserving. If so, that knowledge is stored in long-term memory. When a new session begins, the agent searches and retrieves relevant information as needed.
虽然图中将会话级别的存储过程进行了简化展示，但在实际系统中，存储和检索操作是在每次run()执行时进行的——通过增量式存储和检索来实现更精细的控制。
Source
Although the figure simplifies the process by showing storage at the session level, in practice the system operates at each run() execution—storing and retrieving incrementally for finer control.
图6.3展示了长期记忆如何实现跨会话的信息共享。每次执行run()都会创建一个ExecutionContext，多次执行构成一个Session，而会话中的重要信息会被提取并存储以供未来使用。
Source
Figure 6.3 Long-term memory enables information sharing across sessions. Each run() creates an ExecutionContext, multiple runs form a Session, and important information from sessions is extracted and stored for future use.
6.1.2 上下文工程与记忆
Source
6.1.2 Context engineering and memory
在第1章中，我们将上下文工程定义为“在正确的时间提供正确信息的艺术”，并介绍了五种策略。
第6章（记忆）是其中三种策略汇聚的中心。
Source
In chapter 1, we defined Context Engineering as "the art of providing the right information at the right time" and introduced five strategies. Chapter 6 (Memory) is a hub where three of these strategies converge.
表6.1 上下文工程策略及相关章节
Source
Table 6.1 Context engineering strategies and related chapters
上述模式与上下文工程策略的对应关系如下。
模式1和模式2对应的是缩减和写入。
为管理不断扩展的上下文，我们采用滑动窗口、压缩、摘要等方法进行缩减，或将其分离并存储到外部。
模式3将重要信息保存到外部存储（写入），并在需要时检索使用（检索）。
Source
The patterns above map to context engineering strategies as follows. Patterns 1 and 2 relate to Reduce and Write. To manage expanding context, we shrink it using methods like sliding window, compaction, and summarization, or separate and store it externally. Pattern 3 saves important information to external storage (Write) and retrieves it for use (Retrieval).
表6.2 将每种模式映射到相应策略
Source
Table 6.2 Mapping each pattern to strategies
我们将模式1和模式2归为一组，因为两者都针对同一个问题：“如何管理当前发送给LLM的上下文？”
Source
We group Patterns 1 and 2 together because both address the same problem: "How do we manage the context being sent to the LLM right now?"
模式1：当上下文在单次run()调用中增长时
Source
Pattern 1: When context grows within a single run()
模式二：当对话历史在多次run()调用中积累时
Source
Pattern 2: When conversation history accumulates across multiple run() calls
这些解决方案同样采用了相同的Reduce策略。
滑动窗口仅保留最近的N条消息。
压缩会删除工具调用及其结果，或将它们保存到文件中。
摘要功能会浓缩旧的对话内容。
Source
The solutions also use the same Reduce strategy. Sliding window keeps only the most recent N messages. Compaction deletes tool calls and their results, or saves them to a file. Summarization condenses old conversations.
两者的区别在于数据存储的位置。
在模式1中，我们在ExecutionContext内处理事件。
在模式2中，SessionManager加载存储在Session中的事件，然后以相同方式处理它们。
Source
The difference is where the data resides. In Pattern 1, we work with events within ExecutionContext. In Pattern 2, SessionManager loads events stored in a Session, then processes them the same way.
6.2 执行过程中的上下文管理
Source
6.2 Managing context during execution
模式1的核心挑战在于，解决复杂问题时，随着工具调用和结果的不断积累，上下文会迅速膨胀。
让我们来实现具体的策略以解决这个问题。
Source
The core challenge of Pattern 1 is that context grows rapidly as tool calls and results accumulate while solving complex problems. Let’s implement concrete strategies to address this problem.
6.2.1 存储与展示分离
Source
6.2.1 Separating storage from presentation
上下文管理的第一条原则是将存储与呈现分离。
ExecutionContext.events中记录的所有事件都保持不可变；只有发送给LLM的LlmRequest.contents会被处理。
Source
The first principle of context management is separating storage from presentation. All events recorded in ExecutionContext.events remain immutable; only the LlmRequest.contents sent to the LLM are processed.
为何这种分离很重要
Source
Why this separation matters
将 ExecutionContext 视为您的基准事实：一份完整、结构化的记录，包含了所有发生的事件。
LlmRequest 只是一个可计算投影，您可以根据每次具体的模型调用进行细化和优化。
Source
Think of ExecutionContext as your ground truth: a complete, structured record of everything that happened. LlmRequest is simply a computed projection that you can refine and optimize for each specific model call.
这种分离带来了若干好处。
如果没有原始历史记录，追踪智能体失败的原因就会变得困难。
要回答“为什么它会从这些搜索结果中得出错误结论？”这个问题，你需要当时的原始搜索结果。
此外，某些工具可以引用先前执行操作的结果。
如果删除原始数据，这些工具可能无法正常运行。
Source
This separation provides several benefits. Without the original history, tracing the cause of agent failures becomes difficul. To answer, "Why did it draw the wrong conclusion from these search results?" you need the original search results from that moment. Additionally, some tools can reference results from previously performed operations. If you delete originals, these tools may not function properly.
以在社交媒体上发布照片为例：您保留原始照片，仅在发布时应用滤镜。
由于原始数据得以保留，您随时可以对其进行不同的处理。
我们的上下文管理方式保持不变。
ExecutionContext是维护完整执行历史的存储库，而LlmRequest则处理该历史记录以便传递给LLM。
您可以改变LLM查看上下文的方式，而无需迁移或修改存储的数据。
Source
Consider posting photos to social media: you keep the original photo and only apply filters when posting. With the original preserved, you can always process it differently later. Our context management works the same way. ExecutionContext is the repository that maintains the complete execution history, while LlmRequest processes that history for delivery to the LLM. You can change how the LLM sees the context without migrating or modifying your stored data.
通过回调实现
Source
Implementation via callbacks
在第4章中，我们介绍了before_llm_callback。
该回调在LLM调用之前执行，提供了处理LlmRequest的机会。
Source
In chapter 4, we introduced before_llm_callback. This callback executes just before the LLM call, providing an opportunity to process the LlmRequest.
回调接收ExecutionContext和LlmRequest两者。
它从ExecutionContext中读取当前状态，并修改LlmRequest的内容。
如果回调返回None，则LLM调用继续使用修改后的请求；如果返回LlmResponse，则跳过LLM调用，直接使用该响应。
关键在于，ExecutionContext.events是只读的；修改仅发生在LlmRequest.contents中。
Source
The callback receives both ExecutionContext and LlmRequest. It reads the current state from ExecutionContext and modifies the contents of LlmRequest. If the callback returns None, the LLM call proceeds with the modified request; if it returns an LlmResponse, the LLM call is skipped and that response is used instead. The key point is that ExecutionContext.events is read-only; modifications occur only in LlmRequest.contents.
代码保持原样
before_llm_callback(context: ExecutionContext, request: LlmRequest) -> Optional[LlmResponse]
要灵活应用上下文优化策略，您需要调整令牌阈值等配置值。
以下函数使用闭包模式解决此问题。create_optimizer_callback 接受优化函数和阈值作为参数，生成一个回调函数。
生成的回调函数仅在令牌数量超过阈值时调用优化函数。
Source
To flexibly apply context optimization strategies, you need to adjust configuration values like token thresholds. The following function addresses this using the closure pattern. create_optimizer_callback takes an optimization function and a threshold as arguments to generate a callback function. The generated callback only invokes the optimization function when the token count exceeds the threshold.
清单6.1 创建带阈值的优化器回调
Source
Listing 6.1 Creating an optimizer callback with threshold
代码保持原样
def create_optimizer_callback(apply_optimization, threshold: int = 50000): """Factory function that creates a callback applying optimization strategy""" async def callback( context: ExecutionContext, request: LlmRequest ) -> Optional[LlmResponse]: token_count = count_tokens(request) if token_count < threshold: return None # Support both sync and async functions result = apply_optimization(context, request) if inspect.isawaitable(result): await result return None return callback
优化函数遵循 (context, request) -> None 的签名。
接收上下文的原因在于，执行状态（例如压缩进度）需要记录在 context.state 中。
现在，让我们看看具体的优化策略。
Source
Optimization functions follow the (context, request) -> None signature. The reason for receiving context is that execution state (e.g., how far compression has progressed) needs to be recorded in context.state. Now, let's look at specific optimization strategies.
6.2.2 滑动窗口策略
Source
6.2.2 Sliding window strategy
最简单的方法是仅保留最近的N条消息。
通过丢弃较早的消息并仅保留最新的消息，你可以限制上下文的大小。
Source
The simplest approach is to keep only the most recent N messages. By discarding older messages and keeping only the newest, you limit the context size.
基本实现
Source
Basic implementation
以下函数实现了滑动窗口策略，包含三个步骤：（1）遍历内容以找到用户的原始问题；（2）无条件保留用户消息之前的所有内容，确保智能体保留问题上下文；（3）仅保留后续项目（助手消息、工具调用、工具结果）中最新的window_size项。
Source
The following function implements a sliding window strategy with three steps: (1) iterate through contents to find the user's original question; (2) unconditionally preserve everything up to the user message, ensuring the agent retains the problem context; (3) keep only the most recent window_size items from subsequent items (assistant messages, tool calls, tool results).
清单6.2 滑动窗口策略实现
Source
Listing 6.2 Sliding window strategy implementation
代码保持原样
def apply_sliding_window( context: ExecutionContext, request: LlmRequest, window_size: int = 20 ) -> None: """Sliding window that keeps only the most recent N messages""" contents = request.contents # Find user message position user_message_idx = None for i, item in enumerate(contents): if isinstance(item, Message) and item.role == "user": user_message_idx = i break if user_message_idx is None: return # Preserve up to user message preserved = contents[:user_message_idx + 1] # Keep only the most recent N from remaining items remaining = contents[user_message_idx + 1:] if len(remaining) > window_size: remaining = remaining[-window_size:] request.contents = preserved + remaining
要使用滑动窗口，请将其传递给create_optimizer_callback。
Source
To use the sliding window, pass it to create_optimizer_callback.
清单6.3 使用滑动窗口与优化器回调
Source
Listing 6.3 Using sliding window with optimizer callback
代码保持原样
optimizer = create_optimizer_callback( apply_optimization=apply_sliding_window, threshold=30000 ) agent = Agent( model=LlmClient(model="gpt-5"), before_llm_callback=optimizer )
局限性
Source
Limitations
滑动窗口实现简单且可预测，但存在若干局限性。
如果N值较小，可能会丢失重要上下文；如果N值较大，则无法解决上下文爆炸问题。
更根本地说，消息数量并不是衡量上下文大小的良好指标。
文件读取结果虽然只是一条消息，但可能占用数万个令牌。
因此，更精确的管理需要直接测量令牌数量。
Source
The sliding window is simple to implement and predictable, but has several limitations. If N is small, you may lose important context; if N is large, it doesn't solve the context explosion problem. More fundamentally, message count isn't a good indicator of context size. A file read result is one message but can occupy tens of thousands of tokens. Therefore, more precise management requires directly measuring token counts.
6.2.3 令牌计数
Source
6.2.3 Token counting
LLM的实际限制由令牌数量决定，而非消息数量。
单个文件读取结果可能占用10,000个令牌，而20段简短对话加起来可能只有500个令牌。
精确的上下文管理需要直接测量令牌数量。
Source
The LLM's actual limit is determined by token count, not message count. A single file read result might take up 10,000 tokens, while 20 short conversations combined might only be 500 tokens. Accurate context management requires directly measuring token counts.
介绍tiktoken
Source
Introducing tiktoken
tiktoken是OpenAI提供的分词器库。
由于它与GPT模型实际使用的分词器完全相同，因此可以精确计算token数量。
即使使用其他模型（如Claude、Gemini等），它也可作为粗略估算工具。
Source
tiktoken is a tokenizer library provided by OpenAI. Since it's identical to the tokenizer actually used by GPT models, you can calculate exact token counts. Even when using other models (Claude, Gemini, etc.), it can be used as a rough estimate.
以下函数用于计算一个 LlmRequest 的总令牌数。
关键在于使用 build_messages 将其转换为实际发送给 API 的格式，然后再计算令牌数。
这能为您提供准确的令牌计数，其中包含了指令、内容以及工具定义。
Source
The following function calculates the total token count of an LlmRequest. The key is to use build_messages to convert to the actual format sent to the API, then calculate tokens. This gives you an accurate token count that includes instructions, contents, and tool definitions.
清单6.4 使用tiktoken进行令牌计数
Source
Listing 6.4 Token counting with tiktoken
代码保持原样
def count_tokens(request: LlmRequest) -> int: """Calculate total token count of LlmRequest""" import tiktoken from .llm import build_messages # Select encoding for model, use default on failure try: encoding = tiktoken.encoding_for_model(request.model_id or "gpt-5") except KeyError: encoding = tiktoken.get_encoding("o200k_base") # Convert to API message format then count tokens messages = build_messages(request) total_tokens = 0 for message in messages: # Per-message overhead (role, separators, etc.) total_tokens += 4 # Content tokens if message.get("content"): total_tokens += len(encoding.encode(message["content"])) # tool_calls tokens if message.get("tool_calls"): for tool_call in message["tool_calls"]: func = tool_call.get("function", {}) if func.get("name"): total_tokens += len(encoding.encode(func["name"])) if func.get("arguments"): total_tokens += len(encoding.encode(func["arguments"])) # Tool definition tokens if request.tools: for tool in request.tools: tool_def = tool.tool_definition total_tokens += len(encoding.encode(json.dumps(tool_def))) return total_tokens
为何即使在限制以下，优化仍然重要
Source
Why optimization matters even below the limit
大多数现代模型支持12.8万到超过100万个标记的上下文窗口。
你可能会认为，只有在接近这些限制时，优化才是必要的。
然而，上下文膨胀在达到最大值之前就会造成问题。
Source
Most modern models support context windows of 128K to over 1M tokens. You might think optimization is only necessary when approaching these limits. However, context bloat creates problems well before reaching the maximum.
上下文优化不仅仅是为了避免错误。
即便在限制范围内，臃肿的上下文也会带来三个问题。
首先，成本和延迟会随着令牌数量的增加而增长。
模型定价是按令牌计费的，而且首令牌生成时间会随着上下文大小的增加而延长。
其次，无关信息会分散模型对当前任务的注意力。
研究表明，模型难以在冗长的上下文中找到相关信息，这种现象被称为“迷失在中间”。第三，你需要为模型的响应预留空间。
Source
Context optimization isn't just about avoiding errors. Even within the limit, bloated context creates three problems. First, cost and latency grow with token count. Model pricing is per-token, and time-to-first-token increases with context size. Second, irrelevant information distracts the model from the immediate task. Research shows that models struggle to find relevant information buried in long contexts, a phenomenon known as "lost in the middle." Third, you need to reserve space for the model's response.
最近的研究和生产经验表明，性能下降在远低于宣传的上下文限制时就已经开始。
Chroma的“上下文衰减”研究（2025年）发现，随着输入长度的增加，即使是简单任务，模型性能也变得越来越不可靠。
Manus的工程团队指出：“即使上下文窗口在技术上支持更长的内容，模型性能在超过一定上下文长度后往往会下降。”
Source
Recent research and production experience show that performance degradation begins well below the advertised context limit. Chroma's "Context Rot" study (2025) found that model performance becomes increasingly unreliable as input length grows, even on simple tasks. Manus's engineering team notes that "model performance tends to degrade beyond a certain context length, even if the window technically supports it."
具体阈值因模型、任务复杂度和用例而异，但共识很明确：最佳工作上下文远小于最大窗口大小。
作为一般原则，应将上下文最小化到任务实际所需的范围。
Source
The exact threshold varies by model, task complexity, and use case, but the consensus is clear: the optimal working context is much smaller than the maximum window size. As a general rule, minimize context to what's actually needed for the task.
在本书的示例中，我们使用一个较小的阈值（约20K个标记）来清晰地观察压缩和上下文管理行为。
Source
In this book's examples, we use a small threshold value (around 20K tokens) to clearly observe compaction and context management behaviors.
6.2.4 压缩策略
Source
6.2.4 Compaction strategy
压缩的核心思想是用轻量级引用替换已处理的数据。
如果你已经读取了文件并完成了分析，就没有必要将整个文件内容保留在上下文中。
相反，你会留下一个提示，说明“此文件已读取，需要时可重新读取”。
Source
The core idea of compaction is to replace already-processed data with lightweight references. If you've read a file and completed analysis, there's no need to keep the entire file contents in context. Instead, you leave a hint saying "this file was read and can be re-read if needed."
这种方法遵循“默认范围”原则：为智能体提供所需的最小上下文，并让它必要时明确请求更多信息。
智能体看到类似“搜索结果已处理”的引用。
“如有需要，重新搜索。”如果智能体确实需要再次使用该数据，它会调用相应工具。
Source
This approach follows a "scope by default" principle: give the agent the minimum context needed, and let it explicitly request more when necessary. The agent sees a reference like "Search results processed. Re-search if needed." If it actually needs that data again, it calls the tool.
压缩根据压缩目标分为两种类型：
Source
Compaction divides into two types based on the compression target:
工具调用压缩：写入操作
Source
ToolCall compression: Write operations
像create_file这样将数据存储在外部工具，会在工具调用的参数中包含大量数据。
例如，将一个10,000字符的报告保存到文件，会产生类似这样的工具调用：
Source
Tools like create_file, which store data externally, include large data in the ToolCall's arguments. For example, saving a 10,000-character report to a file results in a ToolCall like this:
代码保持原样
ToolCall( name="create_file", arguments={"path": "report.md", "content": "... 10000 characters of report content ..."} )
对于已经保存到文件中的内容，无需再在上下文中持续维护。
从ToolCall的参数中移除该内容，并替换为一条引用消息。
Source
There's no need to keep maintaining content already saved to a file in the context. Remove the content from the ToolCall's arguments and replace it with a reference message.
工具结果压缩：读取操作
Source
ToolResult compression: Read operations
像read_file或search_web这样的工具，它们从外部来源获取数据，会将大量数据包含在ToolResult的content中。
文件内容或搜索结果可能占用数万个令牌。
Source
Tools like read_file or search_web, which fetch data from external sources, include large data in the ToolResult's content. File contents or search results can occupy tens of thousands of tokens.
如果智能体已经处理过该信息，则仅保留“检索到了什么信息”而非原始数据。
如果智能体需要再次引用该内容，它可以再次调用该工具。
Source
If the agent has already processed the information, leave only "what information was retrieved" instead of the original data. If the agent needs to reference that content again, it can call the tool again.
实现
Source
Implementation
以下代码实现了压缩功能。
关键在于通过单个for循环遍历内容时，同时处理ToolCalls和ToolResults。
由于ToolCalls总是出现在对应的ToolResults之前，当遇到ToolCall时，可以保存其参数，以便在后续压缩ToolResult时使用。
Source
The following code implements compaction. The key is processing both ToolCalls and ToolResults while iterating through contents with a single for loop. Since ToolCalls always appear before their corresponding ToolResults, when you encounter a ToolCall, you can save its arguments for use when compressing the ToolResult later.
TOOLCALL_COMPACTION_RULES 定义了其 ToolCall 参数应被压缩的工具，而 TOOLRESULT_COMPACTION_RULES 定义了其 ToolResult 内容应被压缩的工具。
Source
TOOLCALL_COMPACTION_RULES defines tools whose ToolCall arguments should be compressed, and TOOLRESULT_COMPACTION_RULES defines tools whose ToolResult content should be compressed.
清单6.5 压缩策略实现
Source
Listing 6.5 Compaction strategy implementation
代码保持原样
# Tools to compress ToolCall arguments TOOLCALL_COMPACTION_RULES = { "create_file": "[Content saved to file]", } # Tools to compress ToolResult content TOOLRESULT_COMPACTION_RULES = { "read_file": "File content from {file_path}. Re-read if needed.", "search_web": "Search results processed. Query: {query}. Re-search if needed.", "tavily_search": "Search results processed. Query: {query}. Re-search if needed.", } def apply_compaction(context: ExecutionContext, request: LlmRequest) -> None: """Compress tool calls and results into reference messages""" tool_call_args: Dict[str, Dict] = {} compacted = [] for item in request.contents: if isinstance(item, ToolCall): # Save arguments (for use when compressing ToolResult later) tool_call_args[item.tool_call_id] = item.arguments # If the ToolCall itself is a compression target (create_file, etc.) if item.name in TOOLCALL_COMPACTION_RULES: compressed_args = { k: TOOLCALL_COMPACTION_RULES[item.name] if k == "content" else v for k, v in item.arguments.items() } compacted.append(ToolCall( tool_call_id=item.tool_call_id, name=item.name, arguments=compressed_args )) else: compacted.append(item) elif isinstance(item, ToolResult): # If ToolResult is a compression target (read_file, search_web, etc.) if item.name in TOOLRESULT_COMPACTION_RULES: args = tool_call_args.get(item.tool_call_id, {}) template = TOOLRESULT_COMPACTION_RULES[item.name] compressed_content = template.format( file_path=args.get("file_path", args.get("path", "unknown")), query=args.get("query", "unknown") ) compacted.append(ToolResult( tool_call_id=item.tool_call_id, name=item.name, status=item.status, content=[compressed_content] )) else: compacted.append(item) else: compacted.append(item) request.contents = compacted
这便将“每个提示中10万令牌的噪音”转化为一种精准、按需可用的资源。
数据量可能非常庞大，但上下文窗口依然保持精简。
Source
This turns "100K tokens of noise in every prompt" into a precise, on-demand resource. The data can be huge, but the context window remains lean.
提示缓存的权衡
Source
Trade-offs with prompt caching
在应用压缩时，有一个重要因素需要考虑：提示缓存。
Source
There's an important factor to consider when applying compaction: prompt caching.
提示缓存是LLM API提供的一项成本优化功能。
当连续请求中提示的初始部分相同时，API会复用先前计算的结果。
这可以将成本降低高达90%，并加快响应速度。
OpenAI、Anthropic和Google都支持此功能，且无需特殊配置即可自动应用。
Source
Prompt caching is a cost-optimization feature provided by LLM APIs. When the initial portion of prompts is identical across consecutive requests, the API reuses previously computed results. This can reduce costs by up to 90% and speed up response times. OpenAI, Anthropic, and Google all support this feature, and it's applied automatically without special configuration.
问题在于压缩会修改过去的消息。
这很重要，因为提示缓存是通过重用相同前缀的计算来工作的。
考虑在两个连续步骤中会发生什么：
Source
The problem is that compaction modifies past messages. This matters because rompt caching works by reusing computation for identical prefixes. Consider what happens across two consecutive steps:
代码保持原样
Step 5: [system][user][msg1][msg2][msg3][msg4][msg5] Step 6: [system][user][msg1][msg2][msg3][msg4][msg5][msg6] ↑ only this needs new computation
当你在上下文中间修改消息（例如压缩旧的工具结果）时，之后的所有内容都会变得不同。
Source
When you modify messages in the middle of context (like compressing old tool results), everything after that point becomes different.
代码保持原样
Step 6 (Compacted): [system][user][msg1][compressed msg2][msg3]...[msg6] ↑ changed → everything after is cache miss
解决方案是基于阈值的优化。
在特定阈值以下，保持上下文稳定以保留缓存优势。
只有当上下文溢出的成本超过缓存未命中的成本时，才进行修改。
我们已实现的create_optimizer_callback函数负责处理这一角色。
Source
The solution is threshold-based optimization. Below a certain threshold, keep the context stable to preserve caching benefits. Only modify when the cost of context overflow exceeds the cost of cache misses. The create_optimizer_callback we already implemented handles this role.
代码保持原样
# Below 50000 tokens, don't apply Compaction (maintain caching benefits) # At 50000 tokens or above, apply Compaction (prevent degradation) optimizer = create_optimizer_callback( apply_optimization=apply_compaction, threshold=50000 )
6.2.5 摘要策略
Source
6.2.5 Summarization strategy
压缩仅针对特定的工具调用和结果。
如果一般对话或智能体的推理过程变得冗长，仅靠压缩无法解决。
在这些情况下，摘要被用作最后的手段。
Source
Compaction only targets specific tool calls and results. If the general conversation or the agent's reasoning becomes lengthy, compaction alone can't solve it. In these cases, summarization is used as a last resort.
选择摘要目标
Source
Selecting summarization targets
摘要生成会优先选择最早的消息作为摘要目标。
然而，用户的原始问题必须被保留。
智能体绝不能忘记它当前试图解决的问题。
Source
Summarization selects the oldest messages first as summarization targets. However, the user's original question must be preserved. The agent must not forget what it's currently trying to solve.
摘要仅针对中间过程：调用了哪些工具、发现了什么信息以及取得了哪些进展。
这些信息被总结并添加到系统提示中。
Source
Summarization targets only the intermediate process: which tools were called, what information was discovered, and the progress made. This information is summarized and added to the system prompt.
设计摘要提示
Source
Designing the summary prompt
以下是一个用于总结智能体中间过程的提示。
请求结构化输出可确保摘要保持一致。
Source
The following is a prompt for summarizing the agent's intermediate process. Requesting structured output ensures summaries are consistent.
代码保持原样
SUMMARIZATION_PROMPT = """You are summarizing an AI agent's work progress. Given the following execution history, extract: 1. Key findings: Important information discovered 2. Tools used: List of tools that were called 3. Current status: What has been accomplished and what remains Be concise. Focus on information that will help the agent continue its work. Execution History: {history} Provide a structured summary."""
实现
Source
Implementation
以下函数实现了总结功能。
核心逻辑包含四个步骤：
Source
The following function implements summarization. The core logic consists of four steps:
找到用户消息位置，以标记保护范围的起始点。
Source
Find the user message position to mark the starting point of the preservation range.
保留最近 keep_recent 条消息的原始形式。
Source
Keep the most recent keep_recent messages in their original form.
使用LLM总结它们之间的中间过程。
Source
Summarize the intermediate process between them using the LLM.
将结果重构为“用户问题 + 摘要消息 + 最近消息”。
Source
Reconstruct the result as "user question + summary message + recent messages."
在context.state中记录上次摘要的位置，可以防止在后续的摘要调用中重复摘要已经摘要过的部分。
Source
Recording the last summarization position in context.state prevents re-summarizing portions that have already been summarized in subsuquent summarization calls.
清单6.6 摘要策略实现
Source
Listing 6.6 Summarization strategy implementation
代码保持原样
async def apply_summarization( context: ExecutionContext, request: LlmRequest, llm_client: LlmClient, keep_recent: int = 5 ) -> None: """Replace old messages with a summary""" contents = request.contents # Find user message position user_idx = None for i, item in enumerate(contents): if isinstance(item, Message) and item.role == "user": user_idx = i break if user_idx is None: return # Check previous summary position (skip already-summarized portions) last_summary_idx = context.state.get("last_summary_idx", user_idx) # Calculate summarization target range summary_start = last_summary_idx + 1 summary_end = len(contents) - keep_recent # Overlap prevention: exit if nothing to summarize or range is invalid if summary_end <= summary_start: return # Determine portions to preserve (no overlap) preserved_start = contents[:last_summary_idx + 1] preserved_end = contents[summary_end:] to_summarize = contents[summary_start:summary_end] # Generate summary history_text = format_history_for_summary(to_summarize) summary = await generate_summary(llm_client, history_text) # Add summary to instructions request.append_instructions(f"[Previous work summary]\n{summary}") # Keep only preserved portions in contents request.contents = preserved_start + preserved_end # Record summary position context.state["last_summary_idx"] = len(preserved_start) - 1 def format_history_for_summary(items: List[ContentItem]) -> str: """Convert ContentItem list to text for summarization""" lines = [] for item in items: if isinstance(item, Message): lines.append(f"[{item.role}]: {item.content[:500]}...") elif isinstance(item, ToolCall): lines.append(f"[Tool Call]: {item.name}({item.arguments})") elif isinstance(item, ToolResult): content_preview = str(item.content[0])[:200] if item.content else "" lines.append(f"[Tool Result]: {item.name} -> {content_preview}...") return "\n".join(lines) async def generate_summary(llm_client: LlmClient, history: str) -> str: """Generate history summary using LLM""" request = LlmRequest( instructions=[SUMMARIZATION_PROMPT.format(history=history)], contents=[Message(role="user", content="Please summarize.")] ) response = await llm_client.generate(request) for item in response.content: if isinstance(item, Message): return item.content return ""
压缩与摘要化
Source
Compaction vs. summarization
这两种策略在根本上有所不同。
压缩是确定性的：你可以根据工具名称精确预测哪些内容会被压缩。
总结是语义性的：由大型语言模型决定什么是重要的。
确定性操作成本更低、速度更快且更可预测，因此我们首先应用它们。
Source
These two strategies differ fundamentally. Compaction is deterministic: you can predict exactly what will be compressed based on tool names. Summarization is semantic: an LLM decides what's important. Deterministic operations are cheaper, faster, and more predictable, so we apply them first.
另一个重要区别在于可逆性。
通过压缩，智能体可以通过再次调用工具来恢复原始数据。
通过摘要化，原始推理过程会永久丢失。
因此，应优先尝试压缩，仅在压缩效果不足时才应用摘要化。
Source
There's another important difference: reversibility. With compaction, the agent can restore original data by calling the tool again. With summarization, the original reasoning is permanently lost. Therefore, try compaction first and only apply summarization when that's insufficient.
6.2.6 分层上下文管理
Source
6.2.6 Hierarchical context management
我们应该以何种顺序应用这些策略？
考虑到成本与效果，图6.4所示的层次化方法是合理的。
Source
In what order should we apply these strategies? Considering cost and effectiveness, the hierarchical approach illustrated in figure 6.4 is reasonable.
图6.4 上下文管理策略决策流程。
Source
Figure 6.4 Context management strategy decision flow.
首先，测量令牌数量。
如果低于阈值，则不执行任何操作。
这保持了提示缓存的优势，并避免了不必要的处理。
Source
First, measure the token count. If it is below the threshold, do nothing. This maintains prompt caching benefits and avoids unnecessary processing.
如果超过阈值，则应用压缩。
压缩是免费且快速的。
在大多数情况下，文件读取或搜索结果通常是上下文增长的主要原因，因此仅进行压缩通常就足够了。
Source
If the threshold is exceeded, apply Compaction. Compaction is free and fast. In most cases, file reads or search results are the main culprits of context growth, so Compaction alone is often sufficient.
如果压缩后阈值仍然超出，则应用摘要化处理。
这是最后的办法。
这会增加额外的LLM调用成本，但总比因上下文错误导致失败要好。
Source
If the threshold is still exceeded after compaction, apply summarization. This is the last resort. It incurs additional LLM call costs, but it's better than failure due to context errors.
集成实现
Source
Integrated implementation
要按顺序应用多个策略，将它们实现为一个类会更清晰。
以下类整合了所有策略。
__call__方法被注册为before_llm_callback，并按顺序执行这三个阶段。
在每个阶段之后，会重新测量令牌数量，如果低于阈值，则立即返回。
Source
To apply multiple strategies sequentially, implementing them as a class is cleaner. The following class integrates all strategies. The __call__ method is registered as before_llm_callback and executes the three stages sequentially. After each stage, tokens are re-measured and if below the threshold, it returns immediately.
清单6.7 Hierarchical ContextOptimizer类
Source
Listing 6.7 Hierarchical ContextOptimizer class
代码保持原样
class ContextOptimizer: """Hierarchical context optimization strategy""" def __init__( self, llm_client: LlmClient, token_threshold: int = 50000, enable_compaction: bool = True, enable_summarization: bool = True, keep_recent: int = 5 ): self.llm_client = llm_client self.token_threshold = token_threshold self.enable_compaction = enable_compaction self.enable_summarization = enable_summarization self.keep_recent = keep_recent async def __call__( self, context: ExecutionContext, request: LlmRequest ) -> Optional[LlmResponse]: """Register as before_llm_callback""" # Step 1: Measure tokens if count_tokens(request) < self.token_threshold: return None # Step 2: Apply Compaction if self.enable_compaction: apply_compaction(context, request) if count_tokens(request) < self.token_threshold: return None # Step 3: Apply Summarization if self.enable_summarization: await apply_summarization( context, request, self.llm_client, self.keep_recent ) return None
向智能体注册
Source
Registering with the agent
以下代码演示了如何将ContextOptimizer注册为智能体的before_llm_callback。
优化LLM使用成本较低的模型（gpt-5-mini）来降低成本，而智能体的主模型则使用功能更强大的模型（gpt-5）。
Source
The following code demonstrates how to register ContextOptimizer as the agent's before_llm_callback. The optimization LLM uses a less expensive model (gpt-5-mini) to reduce costs, while the agent's main model uses a more powerful model (gpt-5).
代码保持原样
optimizer = ContextOptimizer( llm_client=LlmClient(model="gpt-5-mini"), token_threshold=50000, enable_compaction=True, enable_summarization=True ) agent = Agent( model=LlmClient(model="gpt-5"), tools=[search_web, read_file, create_file], instructions="You are a helpful research assistant.", max_steps=30, before_llm_callback=optimizer )
6.3 持续执行：会话与状态管理
Source
6.3 Continuous execution: Session and state management
我们已经探讨了模式2（持续执行）的核心挑战：如何在多个run()调用之间保持对话上下文。
目前，我们的智能体在每次调用run()时都会创建一个新的ExecutionContext，导致所有信息在执行结束时丢失。
它既不记得昨天的对话，也不记得片刻之前的对话。
Source
We’ve examined the core challenge of Pattern 2: Continuous Execution: maintaining conversation context across multiple run() calls. Currently, our agent creates a new ExecutionContext with each run() call, causing all information to be lost when execution ends. It remembers neither yesterday's conversation nor the one from moments ago.
我们将在本节中实现的Session和SessionManager正是为了解决这个问题。
通过将对话历史存储在Session中，并使用相同的session_id再次访问，我们可以无缝地继续之前的对话。
以下示例展示了这一能力：
Source
The Session and SessionManager we'll implement in this section address this problem. By storing conversation history in a Session and accessing it again with the same session_id, we can seamlessly continue previous conversations. The following example demonstrates this capability:
代码保持原样
# Maintaining conversation continuity with the same session_id result1 = await agent.run("My name is Alice", session_id="session_1") # → "Nice to meet you, Alice!" result2 = await agent.run("What's my name?", session_id="session_1") # → "Your name is Alice."
然而，会话的作用远不止简单的聊天历史存储。
会话不仅能存储对话历史，还能存储中间执行状态。
利用这一能力，我们可以克服第5章中同步人机交互实现的基本限制。
Source
However, the Session's role extends beyond simple chat history storage. Sessions can store not only conversation history but also intermediate execution state. By leveraging this capability, we can overcome the fundamental limitations of the synchronous human-in-the-loop implementation from chapter 5.
在第5章中，我们使用input()函数实现了用户批准功能。
在执行危险工具之前，代理会提示"您是否批准？"
在终端中显示"(Y/N)"并等待用户响应。
虽然这种方法在本地开发中效果良好，但在生产服务中无法使用。
Source
In chapter 5, we implemented user approval using the input() function. Before executing a dangerous tool, the agent would prompt "Do you approve? (Y/N)" in the terminal and wait for the user's response. While this approach works fine during local development, it's unusable in production services.
解决方案是在遇到需要批准的工具时暂停代理的执行，保存状态，稍后再恢复。
当代理遇到需要批准的工具调用时，它会将当前执行状态保存到会话中并立即返回。
用户随后可以点击网页上的按钮、响应移动应用的通知，甚至几天后通过电子邮件批准。
一旦获得批准，保存的状态将被恢复，执行继续。
Source
The solution is to pause the agent's execution when a tool requiring approval is encountered, save the state, and resume later. When the agent encounters a tool call requiring approval, it saves the current execution state to the Session and returns immediately. The user can then click a button on a web page, respond to a notification on a mobile app, or even approve via email days later. Once approval arrives, the saved state is restored and execution continues.
在本节中，我们将实现两个目标：
Source
In this section, we'll achieve two goals:
第一部分：会话基础。
我们将探索Session类和SessionManager的结构，然后将其与我们的智能体集成，以支持多轮对话。
Source
Part 1: Session Fundamentals. We'll explore the structure of the Session class and SessionManager, then integrate them with our agent to support multi-turn conversations.
第二部分：人在回路。
我们将利用Session的状态持久化能力来实现一个异步工具审批工作流。
通过这种方式，我们将亲眼看到Session提供的价值远超简单的聊天历史存储。
Source
Part 2: Human-in-the-Loop. We'll leverage Session's state persistence capabilities to implement an asynchronous tool approval workflow. Through this, we'll see firsthand that Session offers value far beyond simple chat history storage.
6.3.1 会话类
Source
6.3.1 The session class
会话（Session）是一个容器，用于保存必须在多次run()调用之间持久化的所有信息。
它主要服务于两个核心目的。
首先，它存储对话历史，以便能够继续之前的对话。
其次，它存储任意的执行状态，以便能够恢复被中断的任务。
Source
A Session is a container that holds all information that must persist across multiple run() calls. It serves two core purposes. First, it stores conversation history so that previous conversations can be continued. Second, it stores arbitrary execution state so that interrupted tasks can be resumed.
在设计Session的结构之前，我们需要明确其与第4章实现的ExecutionContext之间的关系。
ExecutionContext保存着单次run()执行期间发生的所有事件和状态。
一旦执行结束，该ExecutionContext就不再使用。
相比之下，Session会跨越多次run()执行而持续存在。
因此，Session的生命周期比ExecutionContext更长。
其工作模式如下：每次run()执行完成后，必要信息会保存到Session中；当下一次run()执行开始时，信息会从Session中恢复。
图6.5展示了这种关系。
Source
Before designing the Session's structure, we need to clarify its relationship with the ExecutionContext we implemented in chapter 4. An ExecutionContext holds all events and states that occur during a single run() execution. Once execution ends, that ExecutionContext is no longer used. A Session, by contrast, persists across multiple run() executions. Therefore, a Session has a longer lifecycle than an ExecutionContext. The pattern works as follows: when each run() execution completes, necessary information is saved to the Session; when the next run() execution begins, information is restored from the Session. This relationship is expressed in figure 6.5.
图6.5 会话与执行上下文之间的关系。
Source
Figure 6.5 Relationship between Session and ExecutionContext.
现在让我们来实现Session类。
session_id唯一标识会话，而user_id则可选地标识用户。
事件列表存储了跨多次run()调用累积的所有事件，而状态字典则存储任意的执行状态。
时间戳记录了会话的创建时间和最后更新时间。
Source
Now let's implement the Session class. The session_id uniquely identifies the session, while user_id optionally identifies the user. The events list stores all events accumulated across multiple run() calls, and the state dictionary stores arbitrary execution state. The timestamps track when the session was created and last updated.
清单6.8 Session类设计
Source
Listing 6.8 Session class design
代码保持原样
class Session(BaseModel): """Container for persistent conversation state across multiple run() calls.""" session_id: str user_id: str | None = None events: list[Event] = Field(default_factory=list) state: dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict) created_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.now) updated_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.now)
Session类设计的一个显著特点是其state字段的多功能性。
凭借其dict[str, Any]类型，它可以存储任何类型的数据。
它可能存储着在人工介入场景中等待批准的待处理工具调用，也可能存储着长时间运行任务的进度。
我们采用这种通用设计，是为了在不修改Session类本身的情况下，支持多样化的执行模式。
Source
A notable aspect of the Session class design is the versatility of the state field. With its dict[str, Any] type, it can store any kind of data. It might hold a pending tool call awaiting approval in a human-in-the-loop scenario, or it might store the progress of a long-running task. We adopted this generic design so that diverse execution patterns can be supported without modifying the Session class itself.
6.3.2 使用SessionManager管理会话
Source
6.3.2 Managing sessions with SessionManager
Session类只是一个数据容器；它不知道如何创建或持久化自身。
我们需要一个独立的管理器，负责创建、检索和保存会话。
这一职责属于SessionManager。
Source
The Session class is merely a data container; it doesn't know how to create or persist itself. We need a separate manager responsible for creating, retrieving, and saving sessions. This role belongs to SessionManager.
SessionManager的核心职责包括：
Source
The core responsibilities of SessionManager are:
创建：新建一个会话并存储它。
Source
Create: Make a new session and store it.
获取：通过session_id查找并返回现有的会话。
Source
Get: Find and return an existing session by session_id.
获取或创建：如果找到现有会话则返回，否则创建新会话。
Source
Get or Create: Return an existing session if found, otherwise create a new one.
保存：将会话中的更改持久化到存储中。
Source
Save: Persist changes to a session back to storage.
我们首先将这些职责定义为一个抽象类，然后根据存储类型提供具体的实现。
例如，InMemorySessionManager将会话存储在Python字典中，而生产环境可能会将其替换为基于数据库的实现。
Source
We first define these responsibilities as an abstract class, then provide concrete implementations depending on the storage type. For example, InMemorySessionManager stores sessions in a Python dictionary, while production environments might swap this for a database-backed implementation.
定义抽象类
Source
Defining the abstract class
首先，我们定义所有SessionManager实现必须遵循的接口。
create方法用于生成新会话，get方法用于检索现有会话，而save方法则将更改持久化到存储中。
由于get_or_create只是get和create的组合，我们将其实现为常规方法而非抽象方法。
子类只需实现get和create方法，get_or_create方法会自动生效。
Source
First, we define the interface that all SessionManager implementations must follow. The create method generates a new session, get retrieves an existing one, and save persists changes to storage. Since get_or_create is simply a combination of get and create, we implement it as a regular method rather than an abstract one. Subclasses only need to implement get and create, and get_or_create works automatically.
注意，所有方法都声明为异步。
对于像InMemorySessionManager这样的简单实现，异步操作并非必需。
然而，使用数据库或外部API的实现需要这些异步操作。
通过在抽象类中定义异步接口，我们可以在不修改调用代码的情况下替换实现。
Source
Notice that all methods are declared as async. For simple implementations like InMemorySessionManager, asynchronous operations aren't necessary. However, implementations that use databases or external APIs require them. By defining an asynchronous interface in the abstract class, we can swap implementations without modifying calling code.
清单6.9 BaseSessionManager抽象类
Source
Listing 6.9 BaseSessionManager abstract class
代码保持原样
from abc import ABC, abstractmethod class BaseSessionManager(ABC): """Abstract base class for session management.""" @abstractmethod async def create( self, session_id: str, user_id: str | None = None ) -> Session: """Create a new session.""" pass @abstractmethod async def get(self, session_id: str) -> Session | None: """Retrieve a session by ID. Returns None if not found.""" pass @abstractmethod async def save(self, session: Session) -> None: """Persist session changes to storage.""" pass async def get_or_create( self, session_id: str, user_id: str | None = None ) -> Session: """Get existing session or create new one.""" session = await self.get(session_id) if session is None: session = await self.create(session_id, user_id) return session
内存中实现
Source
In-memory implementation
现在，我们为开发和测试环境实现InMemorySessionManager。
它使用Python字典作为存储，这意味着当程序终止时，所有会话都会丢失。
在生产环境中，您需要将其替换为基于数据库的实现。
Source
Now we implement InMemorySessionManager for development and testing environments. It uses a Python dictionary as storage, meaning all sessions are lost when the program terminates. In production, you would replace this with a database-backed implementation.
create方法实例化一个新的Session对象并将其存储在字典中。
如果已存在相同session_id的session，它会引发ValueError以防止意外覆盖。
get方法在字典中查找session，如果未找到则返回None。
save方法将session存储在字典中。
Source
The create method instantiates a new Session object and stores it in the dictionary. If a session with the same session_id already exists, it raises a ValueError to prevent accidental overwrites. The get method looks up a session in the dictionary and returns None if not found. The save method stores the session in the dictionary.
清单6.10 InMemorySessionManager实现
Source
Listing 6.10 InMemorySessionManager implementation
代码保持原样
class InMemorySessionManager(BaseSessionManager): """In-memory session storage for development and testing.""" def __init__(self): self._sessions: dict[str, Session] = {} async def create( self, session_id: str, user_id: str | None = None ) -> Session: """Create a new session.""" if session_id in self._sessions: raise ValueError(f"Session {session_id} already exists") session = Session( session_id=session_id, user_id=user_id ) self._sessions[session_id] = session return session async def get(self, session_id: str) -> Session | None: """Retrieve a session by ID.""" return self._sessions.get(session_id) async def save(self, session: Session) -> None: """Save session to storage.""" self._sessions[session.session_id] = session
在Session和SessionManager就位后，让我们将它们集成到智能体中，以实现多轮对话。
Source
With Session and SessionManager in place, letsintegrates them into the agent to enable multi-turn conversations.
6.3.3 将会话集成到智能体中
Source
6.3.3 Integrating sessions into the agent
现在我们需要将这些组件集成到现有的智能体架构中。
集成过程涉及两个部分：扩展ExecutionContext以引用会话，以及修改智能体的run()方法来加载和保存会话。
Source
We now need to integrate these components into our existing agent architecture. The integration involves two parts: extending ExecutionContext to reference a session and modifying the agent's run() method to load and save sessions.
扩展ExecutionContext
Source
Extending ExecutionContext
我们在第4章中实现的执行上下文，充当了单次执行中所有状态的容器。
它将执行历史存储在事件列表中，并将任意运行时状态存储在状态字典中。
随着会话的引入，这些职责发生了转移。
事件和状态现在存在于会话内部，而执行上下文持有对当前会话的引用。
Source
The ExecutionContext we implemented in chapter 4 served as a container for all state within a single execution. It stored execution history in the events list and arbitrary runtime state in the state dictionary. With sessions introduced, these responsibilities shift. Events and state now live inside the Session, while ExecutionContext holds a reference to the current session.
这里的关键设计原则是向后兼容。
现有代码广泛使用了context.events和context.state。
我们使用属性来提供透明访问，使这段代码无需修改即可工作。
Source
The key design principle here is backward compatibility. Existing code extensively uses context.events and context.state. We use properties to provide transparent access, allowing this code to work without modification.
以下代码展示了扩展后的ExecutionContext。
新增的字段是session和session_manager。
session字段引用当前执行所属的会话，而session_manager则处理会话的持久化和检索。
events和state属性在内部分别返回session.events和session.state，因此现有代码无需修改即可继续工作。
Source
The following code shows the extended ExecutionContext. The new fields are session and session_manager. The session field references the session that the current execution belongs to, while session_manager handles session persistence and retrieval. The events and state properties internally return session.events and session.state, so existing code continues to work unchanged.
清单6.11 支持会话的ExecutionContext
Source
Listing 6.11 ExecutionContext with session support
代码保持原样
@dataclass class ExecutionContext: # Existing attributes... # Session support session: Session | None = None session_manager: BaseSessionManager | None = None @property def events(self) -> list[Event]: if self.session: return self.session.events @property def state(self) -> dict[str, Any]: if self.session: return self.session.state def add_event(self, event: Event): """Append an event to the execution history.""" self.events.append(event) # Update session timestamp if available if self.session: self.session.updated_at = datetime.now()
修改智能体初始化
Source
Modifying agent initialization
接下来，我们修改 Agent 类的构造函数以接受 SessionManager。
当提供时，代理会存储它；未提供时，则默认使用 InMemorySessionManager。
Source
Next, we modify the Agent class constructor to accept a SessionManager. When provided, the agent stores it; when not provided, it defaults to InMemorySessionManager.
清单6.12 使用SessionManager初始化代理
Source
Listing 6.12 Agent initialization with SessionManager
代码保持原样
class ToolCallingAgent: """Tool-calling agent with session support.""" def __init__( self, model: LlmClient, tools: list[BaseTool] | None = None, instructions: str = "", max_steps: int = 10, session_manager: BaseSessionManager | None = None, ): self.model = model self.instructions = instructions self.max_steps = max_steps self.tools = self._setup_tools(tools or []) # Use provided session manager or create default self.session_manager = session_manager or InMemorySessionManager()
修改run()方法
Source
Modifying the run() Method
最重要的改动发生在run()方法中。
会话支持需要三个新增部分。
首先，我们接受一个session_id参数来指定在哪个会话中执行。
其次，我们在执行开始时加载或创建会话。
第三，我们在执行完成时保存会话。
Source
The most important changes occur in the run() method. Session support requires three additions. First, we accept a session_id parameter to specify which session to execute within. Second, we load or create the session at the start of execution. Third, we save the session when execution completes.
在以下代码中，请注意关键变化。
当提供session_id时，get_or_create()方法会检索对应的session。
如果session已存在，之前的对话历史会包含在session.events中。
创建ExecutionContext时，我们同时注入session和session_manager。
执行完成后，save()方法会持久化保存session。
Source
In the following code, notice the key changes. When session_id is provided, get_or_create() retrieves the session. If the session already exists, previous conversation history is contained in session.events. When creating ExecutionContext, we inject both the session and session_manager. After execution completes, save() persists the session.
清单6.13 支持会话的run()方法
Source
Listing 6.13 run() method with session support
代码保持原样
async def run( self, user_input: str, session_id: str | None = None, context: ExecutionContext | None = None, ) -> AgentResult: """Execute the agent with optional session support.""" # Load or create session if session_id is provided session = None if session_id: session = await self.session_manager.get_or_create(session_id) # Create context with session support if context is None: context = ExecutionContext( session=session, session_manager=self.session_manager, ) # Existing run() logic... # Save session if available if session: await self.session_manager.save(session) return AgentResult(output=context.final_result, context=context)
6.3.4 基础示例：多轮对话
Source
6.3.4 Basic example: Multi-turn conversation
现在我们已经将Session和SessionManager集成到智能体中，让我们在实践中验证其功能。
我们创建了一个使用InMemorySessionManager的智能体，该管理器将会话存储在内存字典中。
此实现适用于测试和单进程应用。
Source
Now that we've integrated Session and SessionManager into the agent, let's verify it works in practice. We create an agent with InMemorySessionManager, which stores sessions in a dictionary in memory. This implementation is suitable for testing and single-process applications.
清单 6.14 创建支持会话的智能体
Source
Listing 6.14 Creating an agent with session support
代码保持原样
agent = Agent( model=model, instructions="You are a helpful assistant.", session_manager=InMemorySessionManager() )
无会话ID
Source
Without session_id
当我们不指定session_id或每次调用使用不同值时会发生什么？
每次调用run()都被视为一次独立的对话，没有先前交互的记忆。
Source
What happens when we don't specify a session_id or use different values for each call? Each run() invocation is treated as an independent conversation, with no memory of previous interactions.
代码保持原样
result1 = await agent.run("Hi! My name is Alice and I'm a software engineer.") print(f"Response 1: {result1.output}") result2 = await agent.run("What's my name and what do I do?") print(f"Response 2: {result2.output}")
输出将类似于以下内容：
Source
The output will be similar to the following:
代码保持原样
Response 1: Hello Alice! Nice to meet you. It's great to hear that you're a software engineer. How can I help you today? Response 2: I don't have any previous context about you. Could you please tell me your name and what you do?
在第二次调用中，智能体对第一次对话没有任何记忆。
Source
The agent has no memory of the first conversation in the second call.
使用相同的session_id
Source
With the same session_id
现在，让我们为两次调用使用相同的session_id。
两次run()调用共享同一个Session，从而保留了对话上下文。
Source
Now let's use the same session_id for both calls. The two run() invocations share the same Session, preserving conversational context.
代码保持原样
result1 = await agent.run( "Hi! My name is Alice and I'm a software engineer.", session_id="alice_session" ) result2 = await agent.run( "What's my name and what do I do?", session_id="alice_session" )
输出将类似于以下内容：
Source
The output will be similar to the following:
代码保持原样
Response 1: Hello Alice! Nice to meet you. It's great to hear that you're a software engineer. How can I help you today? Response 2: Your name is Alice, and you're a software engineer.
这一次，智能体正确地回忆起了之前交互中的信息。
Source
This time, the agent correctly recalls information from the previous interaction.
理解内部流程
Source
Understanding the internal flow
让我们深入内部机制，来理解这两种场景之间的差异。
Source
Let's examine what happens internally to understand the difference between these two scenarios.
当使用相同的session_id时：
Source
When using the same session_id:
首次运行：get_or_create("alice_session") 创建了一个新的会话。
Source
First run(): get_or_create("alice_session") creates a new Session.
对话存储在session.events中，save()方法会将其持久化保存。
Source
The conversation is stored in session.events, and save() persists it.
第二次运行：get_or_create("alice_session") 返回现有会话。
Source
Second run(): get_or_create("alice_session") returns the existing Session.
ExecutionContext引用了这个Session，因此context.events包含了之前的对话。
Source
ExecutionContext references this Session, so context.events includes the previous conversation.
LLM在生成响应时，能够完全访问先前的上下文。
Source
The LLM generates its response with full access to the prior context.
当未指定session_id或session_id不同时：
Source
When session_id is not specified or differs:
每次调用run()都会创建一个新的Session。
Source
Each run() call creates a new Session.
新会话的事件列表为空，因此LLM在没有先前上下文的情况下进行响应。
Source
The new Session's events list is empty, so the LLM responds without prior context.
在实践中，构建需要用户跨多条消息进行交互的对话式应用时，你会使用会话。
如果没有会话，每次run()调用都是完全独立的，这适用于一次性任务，例如GAIA基准问题。
Source
In practice, you'll use sessions when building conversational applications where users interact across multiple messages. Without sessions, each run() call is completely independent, which is appropriate for one-off tasks like GAIA benchmark problems.
6.3.5 用于工具确认的数据结构
Source
6.3.5 Data structures for tool confirmation
现在，让我们实现一个异步的人机协同工作流。
这将证明Session提供的价值远超简单的聊天历史存储：它支持在任意节点暂停和恢复执行，这对于需要人工审批的工作流至关重要。
Source
Now let’s implement an asynchronous human-in-the-loop workflow. This will demonstrate that Session provides value far beyond simple chat history storage: it enables pausing and resuming execution at arbitrary points, which is essential for workflows requiring human approval.
要实现这个工作流程，我们首先需要定义数据结构。
我们需要一些类型来表示哪些工具调用正在等待批准，以及用户做出了哪些决策。
Source
To implement the workflow, we first need to define data structures. We need types that represent which tool calls are awaiting approval and what decisions the user has made.
待处理工具调用
Source
Pending tool call
PendingToolCall表示一个等待执行的工具调用。
这类似于我们在第4章中定义的ToolCall，但包含了审批请求所需的额外信息。
tool_call字段按原样保留原始的ToolCall对象，而confirmation_message字段包含要向用户显示的消息。
例如：“此操作将删除database.db。
您要继续吗？”
Source
PendingToolCall represents a tool call waiting to be executed. It's similar to the ToolCall we defined in chapter 4, but includes additional information needed for approval requests. The tool_call field preserves the original ToolCall object as-is, and the confirmation_message field contains the message to display to the user. For example: "This action will delete database.db. Do you want to continue?"
清单 6.15 PendingToolCall 类
Source
Listing 6.15 PendingToolCall class
代码保持原样
class PendingToolCall(BaseModel): """A tool call awaiting user confirmation.""" tool_call: ToolCall confirmation_message: str
工具确认
Source
Tool confirmation
ToolConfirmation表示用户的批准决策。
tool_call_id标识此响应对应哪个工具调用，approved字段指示是否获得批准。modified_arguments是一个可选字段，如果用户修改了参数，则包含修改后的值。
例如，用户可能会请求：“我批准删除文件，但将目标文件改为temp.txt。”
Source
ToolConfirmation represents the user's approval decision. The tool_call_id identifies which tool call this response corresponds to, and the approved field indicates whether it was approved. modified_arguments is an optional field containing modified values if the user changed the arguments. For example, a user might request: "I approve the file deletion, but change the target file to temp.txt."
清单 6.16 ToolConfirmation 类
Source
Listing 6.16 ToolConfirmation class
代码保持原样
class ToolConfirmation(BaseModel): """User's decision on a pending tool call.""" tool_call_id: str approved: bool modified_arguments: dict | None = None
扩展AgentResult
Source
Extending AgentResult
我们在第4章实现的AgentResult是一个用于存放智能体执行结果的容器。
output字段存储最终结果，context字段存储ExecutionContext。
为了支持人机协同，我们需要区分执行是已完成还是暂停等待审批。
Source
The AgentResult we implemented in chapter 4 was a container for agent execution results. The output field stored the final result, and the context field stored the ExecutionContext. To support human-in-the-loop, we need to distinguish whether execution has completed or is paused waiting for approval.
添加一个状态字段来表示这一点。“complete”表示正常完成，“pending”表示等待批准，“error”表示发生错误。
当状态为“pending”时，pending_tool_calls字段包含等待批准的工具调用列表。
Source
Add a status field to express this. "complete" means normal completion, "pending" means waiting for approval, and "error" means an error occurred. When the status is "pending", the pending_tool_calls field contains the list of tool calls awaiting approval.
清单 6.17 支持待处理功能的 AgentResult
Source
Listing 6.17 AgentResult with pending support
代码保持原样
from typing import Literal class AgentResult(BaseModel): """Result of agent execution.""" output: str | BaseModel | None = None context: ExecutionContext status: Literal["complete", "pending", "error"] = "complete" pending_tool_calls: list[PendingToolCall] = Field(default_factory=list)
使用Pydantic序列化状态
Source
Serializing state with Pydantic
Session的state字段类型为dict[str, Any]，可以存储任意数据。
然而，Python字典无法直接存储Pydantic模型对象。
当将会话保存到数据库或序列化为JSON时，问题就会出现。
Source
The Session's state field is of type dict[str, Any], which can store arbitrary data. However, Python dictionaries cannot directly store Pydantic model objects. Problems arise when saving the session to a database or serializing it to JSON.
Pydantic的model_dump()和model_validate()方法解决了这个问题。model_dump()将Pydantic对象转换为字典，而model_validate()则将字典恢复为Pydantic对象。
使用这种模式，你可以安全地在Session状态中存储和恢复复杂对象。
Source
Pydantic's model_dump() and model_validate() methods solve this problem. model_dump() converts a Pydantic object to a dictionary, and model_validate() restores a dictionary back to a Pydantic object. Using this pattern, you can safely store and restore complex objects in Session's state.
以下代码展示了存储和恢复待处理工具调用的模式。
当act()方法发现需要批准的工具时，它会使用model_dump()进行序列化并保存到状态中。
在下一次调用run()时，它会通过model_validate()恢复并继续执行。
Source
The following code shows the pattern for storing and restoring pending tool calls. When the act() method discovers a tool requiring approval, it serializes with model_dump() and saves to state. On the next run() call, it restores with model_validate() and resumes execution.
代码保持原样
# Saving: when pending occurs in act() pending_calls = [PendingToolCall(tool_call=tc, confirmation_message=msg)] context.state["pending_tool_calls"] = [p.model_dump() for p in pending_calls] # Restoring: when resuming run() raw_pending = context.state.get("pending_tool_calls", []) pending_calls = [PendingToolCall.model_validate(d) for d in raw_pending]
这种序列化模式允许您在不修改Session类的情况下存储各种执行状态。
除了人机交互场景外，您还可以以同样的方式存储长时间运行任务的进度、检查点数据、智能体收集的中间结果等。
Source
This serialization pattern allows you to store various execution states without modifying the Session class. Beyond human-in-the-loop scenarios, you can store progress of long-running tasks, checkpoint data, intermediate results collected by the agent, and more in the same way.
现在数据结构已准备就绪。
让我们为工具本身添加审批要求功能，并实现智能体的暂停与恢复逻辑。
Source
Now the data structures are ready. Let’s add the approval requirement feature to tools themselves and implement the agent's pause and resume logic.
6.3.6 扩展工具以进行确认
Source
6.3.6 Extending tools for confirmation
我们如何确定一个工具是否需要批准？
最直观的方法是将这些信息包含在工具本身中。
通过扩展我们在第4章中实现的BaseTool类，添加与确认相关的属性，智能体可以在执行工具前检查这些属性，并在必要时暂停执行。
Source
How can we determine whether a tool requires approval? The most intuitive approach is to include this information in the tool itself. By extending the BaseTool class we implemented in chapter 4 to add confirmation-related attributes, the agent can check these attributes before executing a tool and pause execution when necessary.
扩展BaseTool
Source
Extending BaseTool
让我们为BaseTool类添加两个属性：requires_confirmation，一个布尔值，表示工具在执行前是否需要用户确认；以及confirmation_message_template，一个用于向用户显示的确认请求消息模板。
该模板使用{name}和{arguments}占位符，这些占位符会动态填入实际的工具调用信息。
Source
Let’s add two attributes to the BaseTool class: requires_confirmation, a boolean indicating whether the tool requires user approval before execution, and confirmation_message_template, a template for the approval request message shown to the user. The template uses {name} and {arguments} placeholders, which are dynamically filled with actual tool call information.
清单6.18 支持确认功能的BaseTool
Source
Listing 6.18 BaseTool with confirmation support
代码保持原样
class BaseTool(ABC): # Existing attributes: name, description, parameters, execute()... # Confirmation support requires_confirmation: bool = False confirmation_message_template: str = ( "The agent wants to execute '{name}' with arguments: {arguments}. " "Do you approve?" ) def get_confirmation_message(self, arguments: dict[str, Any]) -> str: """Generate a confirmation message for this tool call.""" return self.confirmation_message_template.format( name=self.name, arguments=arguments )
get_confirmation_message()方法使用实际参数填充模板，生成最终消息。
当代理暂停工具执行时，它会在PendingToolCall中包含此消息以呈现给用户。
Source
The get_confirmation_message() method fills the template with actual arguments to generate the final message. When the agent pauses tool execution, it includes this message in the PendingToolCall to present to the user.
定义需要确认的工具
Source
Defining tools that tequire confirmation
我们还修改了第4章实现的@tool装饰器，使其接受requires_confirmation和confirmation_message参数。
完整的修改代码可在GitHub仓库中找到。
以下是使用更新后的装饰器定义需要确认的工具的示例。
Source
We also modify the @tool decorator implemented in chapter 4 to accept requires_confirmation and confirmation_message parameters. The complete modified code is available in the GitHub repository. Here is an example of defining tools that require confirmation using the updated decorator.
delete_file 配置了 requires_confirmation=True，在执行前需要用户批准。
相比之下，get_weather 是一个只读操作，无需批准即可立即执行。
在自定义消息中使用 {arguments[key]} 格式可以包含特定的参数值，让用户在决定是否批准前，能够确切了解将要执行的操作。
Source
delete_file is configured with requires_confirmation=True, requiring user approval before execution. In contrast, get_weather is a read-only operation and executes immediately without approval. Using the {arguments[key]} format in custom messages allows including specific argument values in the message, enabling users to understand exactly what action will be performed before deciding whether to approve.
