@tool( name="delete_file", description="Delete a file from the filesystem", requires_confirmation=True, confirmation_message="⚠️ The agent wants to delete '{arguments[filename]}'. " "This action cannot be undone. Do you approve?" ) def delete_file(filename: str) -> str: """Delete the specified file.""" import os os.remove(filename) return f"Successfully deleted {filename}" @tool( name="get_weather", description="Get current weather for a location" ) def get_weather(location: str) -> str: """Get weather information. No confirmation needed.""" return f"Weather in {location}: Sunny, 22°C"
6.3.7 在智能体中实现暂停与恢复功能
Source
6.3.7 Implementing pause and resume in the agent
既然我们已经为工具添加了确认要求属性，现在就该实现代理检查此属性并暂停或恢复执行的逻辑了。
我们将修改act()和run()方法，以完善人机协同工作流程。
Source
Now that we've added the confirmation requirement attribute to tools, it's time to implement the logic for the agent to check this attribute and pause or resume execution. We'll modify the act() and run() methods to complete the human-in-the-loop workflow.
内部特性与外部扩展
Source
Internal features vs external extensions
在深入实现之前，我们先讨论一个重要的设计决策。
我们已经探讨了如何使用回调函数来自定义智能体行为，包括通过before_llm_callback修改提示词，以及通过after_tool_callback对工具结果进行后处理。
这些回调函数是由用户注入的外部扩展点。
Source
Before diving into implementation, let's address an important design decision. We’ve explored how to customize agent behavior using callbacks, modifying prompts with before_llm_callback and post-processed tool results with after_tool_callback. These callbacks are external extension points injected by users.
然而，工具确认功能则有所不同。
这不是用户可选添加的功能，而是框架本身提供的核心功能。
当遇到需要批准的工具时停止执行，并在收到批准后恢复执行的逻辑，是智能体内部行为的一部分。
Source
However, Tool Confirmation is different. This isn't a feature that users optionally add; it's a core feature that the framework itself provides. The logic of stopping execution when encountering a tool requiring approval and resuming upon receiving approval is part of the agent's internal behavior.
因此，工具确认处理是在_prepare_llm_request()方法内部实现的，而不是作为回调函数。
该方法负责构建发送给LLM请求的内部逻辑，并将审批结果转换为ToolResults，以便自然地将其纳入对话流程，如图6.6所示。
Source
For this reason, Tool Confirmation handling is implemented inside the _prepare_llm_request() method rather than as a callback. This method is responsible for the internal logic of constructing requests to send to the LLM, and it converts approval results into ToolResults to naturally include them in the conversation flow, as shown in figure 6.6.
图6.6 智能体架构中的内部特性与外部扩展对比。
Source
Figure 6.6 Internal features vs external extensions in agent architecture.
在这种结构中，_prepare_llm_request() 负责处理框架的核心逻辑，而回调函数则处理用户的定制需求。
通过将这两个层级明确分离，每一层都可以专注于自身的职责。
Source
In this structure, _prepare_llm_request() handles the framework's essential logic, while callbacks handle user customization. With the two layers clearly separated, each can focus on its own responsibilities.
设计原则
Source
Design principles
在开始实施之前，我们先确立两个核心设计原则。
Source
Before implementation, let's establish two core design principles.
预执行阻止：需要批准的工具必须在执行前获得用户批准。
先执行工具、展示结果，然后再问"我执行了这个操作"是毫无意义的。
这样可以吗？"像文件删除或支付处理这样的操作是无法撤销的。
Source
Pre-execution Blocking: Tools requiring approval must receive user approval before execution. It's meaningless to execute a tool first, show the results, and then ask, "I performed this action. Is that okay?" Actions like file deletion or payment processing cannot be undone.
白名单批准：用户可以仅批准部分待处理的工具调用。
当代理请求三个工具调用时，用户应能够批准其中两个并拒绝一个。
只有包含在批准列表中的工具才会被执行，不在列表中的工具会被自动拒绝。
Source
Whitelist Approval: Users can approve only some of the pending tool calls. When the agent requests three tool calls, the user should be able to approve two and reject one. Only tools included in the approval list are executed, and tools not in the list are automatically rejected.
修改 act() 方法
Source
Modifying the act() method
我们在第4章实现的act()方法会立即执行LLM返回的所有工具调用。
现在，我们修改它以检查requires_confirmation属性，并将需要确认的工具存储在context.state中，而不是立即执行它们。
Source
The act() method we implemented in chapter 4 immediately executed all tool calls returned by the LLM. Now we modify it to check the requires_confirmation attribute and store tools requiring approval in context.state instead of executing them.
清单 6.20 带有确认检查的修改后的 act() 方法
Source
Listing 6.20 Modified act() method with confirmation check
代码保持原样
async def act( self, context: ExecutionContext, tool_calls: List[ToolCall] ) -> List[ToolResult]: tools_dict = {tool.name: tool for tool in self.tools} pending_calls = [] for tool_call in tool_calls: tool = tools_dict.get(tool_call.name) # Check if confirmation is required if tool.requires_confirmation: pending = PendingToolCall( tool_call=tool_call, confirmation_message=tool.get_confirmation_message( tool_call.arguments ) ) pending_calls.append(pending) continue # Do not execute, do not create ToolResult # Execute tools that don't require confirmation # ... existing tool execution logic ... # Store pending calls in session state if pending_calls: context.state["pending_tool_calls"] = [ p.model_dump() for p in pending_calls ] return results
让我们来看看关键的变化。
在遍历工具调用时，我们会检查每个工具的requires_confirmation属性。
对于需要确认的工具，我们会创建一个PendingToolCall对象，将其添加到pending_calls列表中，然后继续处理下一个工具，而不创建ToolResult。
只有那些不需要确认的工具会立即执行并返回结果。
Source
Let's examine the key changes. As we iterate through tool calls, we check each tool's requires_confirmation attribute. For tools that require approval, we create a PendingToolCall object, add it to the pending_calls list, and move on to the next tool without creating a ToolResult. Only tools that don't require approval are executed immediately and return results.
act() 的返回类型保持不变，仍然是 List[ToolResult]。
由于待处理工具调用信息存储在 context.state 中，调用方可以检查 context.state 来确定待处理状态。
这种方法在保持与现有接口兼容性的同时，增加了新的功能。
Source
The return type of act() remains the same List[ToolResult]. Since pending tool call information is stored in context.state, callers can check context.state to determine pending status. This approach adds new functionality while maintaining compatibility with the existing interface.
修改run()方法
Source
Modifying the run() Method
run()方法必须处理两种场景。
首先，当在新执行过程中遇到需要批准的工具时，它会暂停执行并返回待定状态。
其次，当恢复先前暂停的执行时，它会在context.state中记录用户的批准决策，并继续执行。
Source
The run() method must handle two scenarios. First, when a tool requiring approval is encountered during a new execution, it pauses execution and returns with a pending status. Second, when resuming a previously paused execution, it registers the user's approval decisions in context.state and continues execution.
清单6.21 带暂停和恢复功能的修改版run()方法
Source
Listing 6.21 Modified run() method with pause and resume
代码保持原样
async def run( self, user_input: str | None = None, session_id: str | None = None, tool_confirmations: List[ToolConfirmation] | None = None, context: ExecutionContext | None = None, ) -> AgentResult: # Register confirmations for processing in _prepare_llm_request if tool_confirmations: context.state["tool_confirmations"] = [ c.model_dump() for c in tool_confirmations ] # Main agent loop while not context.final_result and context.current_step < self.max_steps: await self.step(context) # Check for pending confirmations after each step if context.state.get("pending_tool_calls"): pending_calls = [ PendingToolCall.model_validate(p) for p in context.state["pending_tool_calls"] ] return AgentResult( status="pending_confirmation", context=context, pending_tool_calls=pending_calls, )
让我们回顾一下关键变化：
Source
Let's review the key changes:
tool_confirmations 参数：接受用户批准决策的列表。
当从先前挂起的状态恢复时，该列表会注册到 context.state 中。
实际处理在下一步 step() 调用期间的 _prepare_llm_request() 中执行。
Source
tool_confirmations parameter: Accepts a list of user approval decisions. When resuming from a previously pending state, this list is registered in context.state. The actual processing is performed in _prepare_llm_request() during the next step() call.
待处理检查：在代理循环中执行step()后，检查context.state中是否有待处理的工具调用。
如果存在，立即返回pending_confirmation状态以暂停执行。
Source
Pending check: After executing step()in the agent loop, check for pending tool calls in context.state. If present, immediately return with pending_confirmation status to pause execution.
可选参数user_input：在恢复暂停的执行时，仅需提供tool_confirmations；user_input现在为可选参数。
Source
Optional user_input parameter: When resuming a paused execution, only tool_confirmations is required; user_input is now optional.
修改 _prepare_llm_request() 函数
Source
Modifying _prepare_llm_request()
_prepare_llm_request() 方法处理在 context.state 中注册的批准决策。
它执行已批准的工具并将结果记录为事件，同时为被拒绝的工具记录拒绝消息。
由于执行已批准工具时需要 await，该方法现在是异步的。
Source
The _prepare_llm_request() method processes approval decisions registered in context.state. It executes approved tools and records results as events, while logging rejection messages for rejected tools. This method is now async because await is required when executing approved tools.
清单 6.22 用于确认处理的修改版 _prepare_llm_request()
Source
Listing 6.22 Modified _prepare_llm_request() for confirmation processing
代码保持原样
async def _prepare_llm_request( self, context: ExecutionContext ) -> LlmRequest: """Package context into an LlmRequest, processing confirmations first.""" # Process pending confirmations if both are present if ("pending_tool_calls" in context.state and "tool_confirmations" in context.state): confirmation_results = await self._process_confirmations(context) # Add results as an event so they appear in contents if confirmation_results: confirmation_event = Event( execution_id=context.execution_id, author=self.name, content=confirmation_results, ) context.add_event(confirmation_event) # Clear processed state del context.state["pending_tool_calls"] del context.state["tool_confirmations"] # Flatten events into content items flat_contents = [] for event in context.events: flat_contents.extend(event.content) # ... existing LlmRequest construction logic ...
处理顺序至关重要。
首先，处理批准决策以生成ToolResults并将其记录为事件；然后构建包含这些事件的内容。
这能确保LLM在下一步中看到批准/拒绝的结果。
Source
The processing order is important. First, process approval decisions to generate ToolResults and record them as events; then construct contents including those events. This ensures the LLM can see the approval/rejection results in the next step.
这种顺序是有保证的，因为_prepare_llm_request()是一个内部方法。
如果我们在before_llm_callback中实现这个逻辑，就会出现时序问题：新添加的事件不会被包含在内容中，因为回调函数接收的是一个已经构建好的LlmRequest。
这也是为什么框架内部功能应该在内部方法中处理，而不是在回调函数中的另一个原因。
Source
This ordering is guaranteed because _prepare_llm_request() is an internal method. If we implemented this logic before_llm_callback, a timing issue would occur: newly added events wouldn't be included in contents because callbacks receive an already-constructed LlmRequest. This is another reason why framework internal features should be handled in internal methods rather than callbacks.
实现确认处理逻辑
Source
Implementing confirmation processing logic
_process_confirmations() 方法执行实际的批准处理。
对于每个待处理的工具调用，它会检查批准状态，执行已批准的工具，并为未批准的情况（无论是明确拒绝还是未出现在批准列表中）记录拒绝消息。
Source
The _process_confirmations() method performs the actual approval processing. For each pending tool call, it checks approval status, executes approved tools, and records rejection messages for unapproved cases (either explicit rejection or absence from the approval list).
清单 6.23 _process_confirmations() 实现
Source
Listing 6.23 _process_confirmations() implementation
代码保持原样
async def _process_confirmations( self, context: ExecutionContext ) -> List[ToolResult]: tools_dict = {tool.name: tool for tool in self.tools} results = [] # Restore pending tool calls from state pending_map = { p["tool_call"]["tool_call_id"]: PendingToolCall.model_validate(p) for p in context.state["pending_tool_calls"] } # Build confirmation lookup by tool_call_id confirmation_map = { c["tool_call_id"]: ToolConfirmation.model_validate(c) for c in context.state["tool_confirmations"] } # Process ALL pending tool calls for tool_call_id, pending in pending_map.items(): tool = tools_dict.get(pending.tool_call.name) confirmation = confirmation_map.get(tool_call_id) if confirmation and confirmation.approved: # Merge original arguments with modifications arguments = { **pending.tool_call.arguments, **(confirmation.modified_arguments or {}) } # Execute the approved tool try: output = await tool(context, **arguments) results.append(ToolResult( tool_call_id=tool_call_id, name=pending.tool_call.name, status="success", content=[output], )) except Exception as e: results.append(ToolResult( tool_call_id=tool_call_id, name=pending.tool_call.name, status="error", content=[str(e)], )) else: # Rejected: either explicitly or not in confirmation list if confirmation: reason = confirmation.reason or "Tool execution was rejected by user." else: reason = "Tool execution was not approved." results.append(ToolResult( tool_call_id=tool_call_id, name=pending.tool_call.name, status="error", content=[reason], )) return results
在此实现中有三个关键点：
Source
There are three key points in this implementation:
白名单批准：我们遍历所有待处理工具调用，仅执行那些在批准列表中且approved=True的调用。
任何不在批准列表中或approved=False的请求均被视为拒绝。
Source
Whitelist approval: We iterate through all pending tool calls and execute only those that are in the approval list with approved=True. Any not in the approval list or with approved=False are treated as rejections.
参数合并：当提供modified_arguments时，我们使用{**original, **modified}将其与原始参数合并。
修改后的参数会覆盖原始参数，允许用户有选择地修改特定参数，例如仅更新文件路径。
Source
Argument merging: When modified_arguments is provided, we merge it with the original arguments using {**original, **modified}. Modified arguments overwrite the originals, allowing users to selectively modify specific arguments, such as only updating the file path.
清晰的反馈：被拒绝的工具也会作为ToolResults记录下来。
由于LLM期望工具调用返回结果，我们必须明确告知它工具被拒绝的情况，以便它能做出适当响应。
例如，如果文件删除请求被拒绝，LLM可以建议替代方法或向用户请求澄清。
Source
Clear feedback: Rejected tools are also recorded as ToolResults. Since the LLM expects results for tool calls, we must explicitly inform it when a tool is rejected so it can respond appropriately. For example, if a file deletion is rejected, the LLM can suggest alternative approaches or ask the user for clarification.
完整流程概览
Source
Complete flow summary
我们来总结一下我们已实现的暂停与恢复机制的整体流程。
Source
Let's summarize the complete flow of the pause-and-resume mechanism we've implemented.
图6.7 暂停与恢复机制的整体流程。

Figure 6.7 Overall flow of the pause and resume mechanism.
6.3.8 完整示例：人机协同工作流程
Source
6.3.8 Complete example: Human-in-the-loop workflow
现在，让我们结合所有已实现的组件，展示一个完整的人机协同工作流程。
我们将创建一个简单的场景，其中智能体尝试删除一个文件，暂停以等待用户批准，然后根据用户决定恢复执行。
Source
Now let's combine all the components we've implemented to demonstrate a complete human-in-the-loop workflow. We'll create a simple scenario where the agent attempts to delete a file, pauses for user approval, and then resumes execution based on the user's decision.
设置示例
Source
Setting up the example
首先，我们定义一个需要确认的工具，并创建一个支持会话的智能体。
delete_file工具被配置为requires_confirmation=True，因此智能体在执行前会暂停并等待用户批准。
Source
First, we define a tool that requires confirmation and create an agent with session support. The delete_file tool is configured with requires_confirmation=True, so the agent will pause and wait for user approval before executing.
清单6.24 设置人机回环的工具和智能体
Source
Listing 6.24 Setting up tools and agent for human-in-the-loop
代码保持原样
from agent import Agent, InMemorySessionManager, ToolConfirmation from tools import tool @tool( name="delete_file", description="Delete a file from the filesystem", requires_confirmation=True, confirmation_message="⚠️ Delete '{arguments[filename]}'? This cannot be undone." ) def delete_file(filename: str) -> str: import os os.remove(filename) return f"Deleted {filename}" @tool(name="list_files", description="List files in a directory") def list_files(directory: str = ".") -> str: import os return "\n".join(os.listdir(directory)) agent = Agent( model=model, tools=[delete_file, list_files], instructions="You are a helpful file management assistant.", session_manager=InMemorySessionManager() )
步骤1：初始请求
Source
Step 1: Initial request
用户要求智能体删除一个临时文件。
当智能体尝试调用delete_file工具时，执行会暂停，因为需要确认。
Source
The user asks the agent to delete a temporary file. When the agent attempts to call the delete_file tool, execution pauses because confirmation is required.
清单6.25 触发待确认的初始请求

Listing 6.25 Initial request triggering pending confirmation
代码保持原样
result = await agent.run( "Please delete the file named temp.txt", session_id="file_session" ) print(f"Status: {result.status}") # Status: pending_confirmation print(f"Pending tools: {len(result.pending_tool_calls)}") # Pending tools: 1 for pending in result.pending_tool_calls: print(f"Tool: {pending.tool_call.name}") print(f"Arguments: {pending.tool_call.arguments}") print(f"Message: {pending.confirmation_message}") # Tool: delete_file # Arguments: {'filename': 'temp.txt'} # Message: ⚠️ Delete 'temp.txt'? This cannot be undone.
代理立即返回，状态为“pending_confirmation”。
pending_tool_calls列表包含了等待批准的工具的详细信息，例如向用户显示的确认消息。
Source
The agent returns immediately with status="pending_confirmation". The pending_tool_calls list includes details about the tool awaiting approval, such as the confirmation message shown to the user.
步骤2：用户批准

Step 2: User approval
在实际应用中，用户可能会点击网页上的按钮或响应移动通知。
这里，我们通过创建ToolConfirmation对象并恢复执行来模拟批准过程。
Source
In a real application, the user might click a button on a web page or respond to a mobile notification. Here, we simulate approval by creating a ToolConfirmation object and resuming execution.
清单6.26 经用户批准后恢复执行
Source
Listing 6.26 Resuming execution with user approval
代码保持原样
# User approves the deletion confirmation = ToolConfirmation( tool_call_id=result.pending_tool_calls[0].tool_call.tool_call_id, approved=True ) result = await agent.run( session_id="file_session", tool_confirmations=[confirmation] ) print(f"Status: {result.status}") # Status: complete print(f"Output: {result.output}") # Output: I've deleted the file temp.txt as requested.
当我们再次使用相同的session_id和批准决定调用run()时，代理会恢复执行。
它会执行已批准的工具，接收结果，并生成最终响应。
Source
When we call run() again with the same session_id and the approval decision, the agent resumes execution. It executes the approved tool, receives the result, and generates a final response.
6.4 长期记忆：跨会话积累知识
Source
6.4 Long-term memory: Accumulating knowledge across sessions
Session和SessionManager使我们能够在同一session_id内继续对话。
然而，一旦会话完全结束，其信息就会丢失。
在本节中，我们实现长期记忆，以积累和利用跨越会话边界的知识。
Source
The Session and SessionManager allowed us to continue conversations within the same session_id. However, once a session completely ends, its information is lost. In this section, we implement long-term memory to accumulate and utilize knowledge beyond session boundaries.
长期记忆是结合上下文工程的写入（存储）和检索（搜索）策略的一个典型例子。
会话结束后，重要信息会保存到外部存储（写入），而在新会话中，这些信息会被检索并添加到上下文中（检索）。
Source
Long-term memory is a prime example of combining Context Engineering's Write (storage) and Retrieval (search) strategies. After a session ends, important information is saved to external storage (Write), and in new sessions, this information is retrieved and added to the context (Retrieval).
6.4.1 长期记忆的结构
Source
6.4.1 The structure of long-term memory
我们实现的SessionManager和这里介绍的MemoryManager解决的是不同的问题。
Source
The SessionManager we implemented and the MemoryManager introduced here address different problems.
SessionManager负责维护会话内的对话连续性。
当你使用相同的session_id多次调用run()时，之前的对话内容会被保留。
然而，使用不同的session_id开始新对话会阻止访问先前会话的内容。
Source
SessionManager maintains conversation continuity within a session. When you call run() multiple times with the same session_id, the previous conversation content is preserved. However, starting a new conversation with a different session_id prevents access to the previous session content.
MemoryManager存储重要信息，即使在会话结束后也能保留，允许在未来的会话中检索和使用。
例如，“用户提到他们是营销人员”或“之前解决这个问题时采用了什么方法”。
Source
MemoryManager stores important information even after a session ends, allowing retrieval and use in future sessions. Examples include "the user mentioned they're a marketer" or "what approach was used when solving this problem before."
图6.8 MemoryManager的作用。
Source
Figure 6.8 The role of MemoryManager.
SessionManager负责会话内的横向连续性（对话流程），而MemoryManager则负责跨会话的纵向连续性（知识积累）。
Source
SessionManager handles horizontal continuity within sessions (conversation flow), while MemoryManager handles vertical continuity across sessions (knowledge accumulation).
两大支柱：存储与检索
Source
The two pillars: Storage and retrieval
长期记忆系统有两个核心操作：存储（写入）和检索。
最简单的方法是将文本直接转换为向量嵌入进行存储，然后在检索时找到并返回与查询文本相似的向量。
然而，存储整个对话会引入噪声，重要信息可能被埋没。
Source
Long-term memory systems have two core operations: storage (Write) and retrieval. The simplest approach is to convert text directly into vector embeddings for storage, then find and return vectors similar to the query text during retrieval. However, storing entire conversations introduces noise, and important information can get buried.
最近的记忆库（如mem0和graphiti）通过使用LLM仅提取值得保留的信息，对此进行了改进。
当存储新信息时，它们会执行四种操作之一来处理与现有记忆的冲突。
Source
Recent memory libraries like mem0 and graphiti improve on this by using LLMs to extract only information worth preserving. When storing newinformation, they perform one of four operations to manage conflicts with existing memories.
ADD会存储尚不存在的新信息。
Source
ADD stores new information that doesn't already exist.
UPDATE 用于修改现有记忆。
Source
UPDATE modifies existing memories.
DELETE 会移除矛盾的记忆。
Source
DELETE removes contradictory memories.
SKIP会忽略已存储的信息。
Source
SKIP ignores information that's already stored.
在本章中，我们仅实现添加和跳过功能。
用户档案信息（如姓名、职业、偏好等）会随时间变化，需要更新和删除，但问题解决记录则不同。
即使是同一问题，不同的方法或结果也值得作为独立记录保存（添加），而完全相同的尝试则可以忽略（跳过）。
无需修改或删除过去的失败记录；保留它们有助于避免重复同样的错误。
这种记忆的不可变性简化了我们的实现。
Source
In this chapter, we implement only ADD and SKIP. User profile information (name, occupation, preferences, etc.) can change over time and requires UPDATE and DELETE, but problem-solving records are different. Even forthe same problem, different approaches or results are worth storing as separate records (ADD), while completely identical attempts can be ignored (SKIP). There's no need to modify or delete past failure records; keeping them helps avoid repeating the same mistakes. This immutability of memories simplifies our implementation.
6.4.2 信息提取：结构化输出
Source
6.4.2 Information extraction: Structured output
如果要从记忆中提取的信息是简单事实，文本格式就足够了。
适合单句存储的信息，例如“用户是营销人员”或“偏好Python”，可以直接存储和搜索。
Source
If the information to extract from memory is simple facts, text format is sufficient. Information that fits in a single sentence, like "the user is a marketer" or "prefers Python" can be stored and searched as-is.
有时需要存储的信息更为复杂。
以GAIA问题解决记录为例：我们不仅要存储“解决了这个问题”，还需要记录问题是什么、使用了什么方法以及结果如何。
这些信息必须结构化，以便智能体在遇到类似问题时，能够参考过去成功的做法或避免失败的方法。
Source
Sometimes the information to store is more complex. Consider GAIA problem-solving records: instead of just "solved this problem," we need to store what the problem was, what approach was used, and the result. This information must be structured so the agent can reference past successful approaches or avoid failed ones when encountering similar problems.
扩展LlmClient
Source
Extending LlmClient
我们在LlmClient中添加了两个方法，分别用于信息提取和向量嵌入。
第4章中的generate()方法以LlmRequest作为输入，专门用于智能体执行。
对于基础的文本生成任务，需要更简单的接口。
Source
We add two methods to LlmClient for information extraction and vector embeddings. The generate() method from chapter 4 takes LlmRequest as input and is specialized for agent execution. Simpler interfaces are needed for basic text generation.
ask()方法接收一个提示并返回文本或JSON。
当提供response_format参数时，它会以请求的格式返回输出。
Source
The ask() method takes a prompt and returns text or JSON. When a response_format parameter is provided, it returns output in the requested format.
代码保持原样
# Simple text generation answer = await llm_client.ask("What is 2 + 2?") # JSON structured output data = await llm_client.ask(prompt, response_format=GaiaOutput)
定义记忆模式
Source
Defining the memory schema
我们使用Pydantic来定义GAIA问题解决记录的模式。
该模式捕获了问题解决尝试的基本要素：task_summary描述问题要求，approach记录用于解决的方法和工具，final_answer存储代理提交的答案，is_correct指示答案是否正确，error_analysis则在尝试失败时捕获失败原因。
Source
We use Pydantic to define a schema for GAIA problem-solving records. The schema captures the essential elements of a problem-solving attempt: task_summary describes what the problem asked, approach records the methods and tools used to solve it, final_answer stores the agent's submitted answer, is_correct indicates whether the answer was right, and error_analysis captures why the attempt failed when it did.
清单6.27 TaskMemory模式定义
Source
Listing 6.27 TaskMemory schema definition
代码保持原样
class TaskMemory(BaseModel): """Structured memory for GAIA problem-solving records""" task_summary: str = Field(description="What the problem asked") approach: str = Field(description="Methods and tools used to solve it") final_answer: str = Field(description="The agent's submitted answer") is_correct: bool = Field(description="Whether the answer was correct") error_analysis: str | None = Field( default=None, description="Why the attempt failed, if it did" ) def to_embedding_text(self) -> str: """Generate text for vector search""" return f"Task: {self.task_summary}"
to_embedding_text() 方法生成用于向量搜索的文本。
这里，它仅包含问题摘要，以便在检索过程中能够找到类似的问题。
解决方法和答案作为元数据存储，并在检索后使用。
Source
The to_embedding_text() method generates text for vector search. Here, it includes only the problem summary so that similar problems can be found during retrieval. The approach and answer are stored as metadata and used after retrieval.
提取提示设计
Source
Extraction prompt design
我们设计一个提示，从智能体的执行历史中提取结构化的记忆。
该提示指示大语言模型分析完整的执行轨迹，并识别关键要素：正在解决的问题、采取的方法以及是否成功。
Source
We design a prompt that extracts structured memories from the agent's execution history. The prompt instructs the LLM to analyze the complete execution trace and identify the key elements: what problem was being solved, what approach was taken, and whether it succeeded.
代码保持原样
TASK_MEMORY_EXTRACTION_PROMPT = """You are analyzing an agent's problem-solving record to extract a learning record. Analyze the following execution history: <execution_history> {execution_history} </execution_history> """
执行历史包含智能体的推理过程、工具调用、中间结果以及用户添加的反馈，这些反馈表明答案是否正确。
LLM将所有信息整合成结构化的记忆。
Source
The execution history contains the agent's reasoning process, tool calls, intermediate results, and feedback added by the user indicating whether the answer was correct. The LLM synthesizes all of this into a structured memory.
重复检查提示
Source
Duplicate check prompt
在存储新记忆之前，我们会检查是否已存在类似信息。
这可以防止记忆存储区被关于同一问题的冗余条目填满。
Source
Before storing a new memory, we check whether similar information already exists. This prevents the memory store from filling with redundant entries about the same problem.
清单 6.28 DuplicateCheckResult 模式与提示
Source
Listing 6.28 DuplicateCheckResult schema and prompt
代码保持原样
class DuplicateCheckResult(BaseModel): """Result of duplicate check""" decision: str = Field(description="ADD (new information) or SKIP (duplicate)") reason: str = Field(description="Explanation for the decision") DUPLICATE_CHECK_PROMPT = """Compare the new memory against existing memories to determine if it's a duplicate. Existing memories: {existing_memories} New memory: {new_memory} Respond with one of: - ADD: This is new information that should be stored - SKIP: Similar information already exists, no need to store Judgment criteria: - Same problem with different approach or different result counts as new information - Same problem with same approach and same result is a duplicate """
提示词提供现有记忆作为上下文，并要求大语言模型做出二元决策。
DuplicateCheckResult 模式同时捕获了决策及其背后的推理过程。
Source
The prompt provides existing memories as context and asks the LLM to make a binary decision. The DuplicateCheckResult schema captures both the decision and the reasoning behind it.
6.4.3 使用ChromaDB构建向量存储
Source
6.4.3 Building a vector store with ChromaDB
在第5章中，我们通过动手实践学习了向量搜索的原理。
我们介绍了计算余弦相似度并返回前几位结果的过程。
现在，我们将使用向量数据库来实现存储和检索功能。
在我们的实践中，我们使用ChromaDB，它轻量级且配置简单。
Source
In chapter 5, we learned the principles of vector search through hands-on implementation. We coveredthe process of calculating cosine similarity and returning top results. Now we’ll implement storage and retrieval using a vector database. For our practice, we use ChromaDB, which is lightweight and simple to configure.
安装ChromaDB及其核心概念
Source
Installing ChromaDB and core concepts
ChromaDB是一个轻量级向量数据库，可在本地运行。
您可以通过安装Python包立即使用它，无需单独设置服务器，这使其非常适合原型设计和学习。
Source
ChromaDB is a lightweight vector database that runs locally. You can use it immediately by installing the Python package, with no separate server setup required, making it ideal for prototyping and learning.
代码保持原样
uv add chromadb
ChromaDB的核心概念是集合。
集合（Collection）将相关文档分组，类似于关系数据库中的表。
每个集合将文档文本、嵌入向量和元数据存储在一起。
Source
The core concept in ChromaDB is the Collection. A Collection groups related documents, similar to a table in relational databases. Each Collection stores document text, embedding vectors, and metadata together.
基本用法
Source
Basic usage
以下代码展示了ChromaDB的基本存储和检索流程。
我们使用chromadb.Client()创建一个内存客户端，并使用get_or_create_collection()创建一个集合。
当你在embedding_function参数中指定嵌入函数时，它会在存储和检索过程中自动将文本转换为向量。
Source
The following code demonstrates ChromaDB's basic storage and retrieval flow. We create an in-memory client with chromadb.Client() and a collection with get_or_create_collection(). When you specify an embedding function in the embedding_function parameter, it automatically converts text to vectors during both storage and retrieval.
清单6.29 ChromaDB基本用法
Source
Listing 6.29 ChromaDB basic usage
代码保持原样
import chromadb from chromadb.utils.embedding_functions import OpenAIEmbeddingFunction # Create client (in-memory) client = chromadb.Client() # Set up embedding function embedding_fn = OpenAIEmbeddingFunction( model_name="text-embedding-3-small" ) # Create collection collection = client.get_or_create_collection( name="my_memories", embedding_function=embedding_fn ) # Store documents - just pass text, embeddings are generated automatically collection.add( ids=["mem_001", "mem_002"], documents=["The cat is sleeping on the sofa", "The dog is playing in the park"], metadatas=[{"category": "cat"}, {"category": "dog"}] ) # Search - just pass query text, embeddings are generated automatically results = collection.query( query_texts=["Where is the cat resting"], n_results=1 ) print(results["documents"]) # [['The cat is sleeping on the sofa']] print(results["metadatas"]) # [[{'category': 'cat'}]]
当你指定 embedding_function 时，调用 add() 方法时会自动对文档文本进行嵌入，调用 query() 方法执行相似性搜索时也会自动对 query_texts 进行嵌入。
嵌入向量的生成和余弦相似度计算均在内部自动处理。
Source
When you specify an embedding_function, the document text is automatically embedded when calling add(), and query_texts are also automatically embedded when calling query() to perform similarity search. The embedding generation and cosine similarity calculation are all handled internally.
使用元数据
Source
Using metadata
metadatas参数存储每个文档的附加信息。
你可以在搜索结果中使用此元数据来检查补充信息，如文档类别、创建时间或来源。
在下一节我们将实现的内存存储中，我们将诸如方法和正确性等信息作为元数据存储。
Source
The metadatas parameter stores additional information for each document. You can use this metadata in search results to check supplementary information such as document category, creation time, or source. In the memory store we implement in the next section, we store information like approach and correctness as metadata.
6.4.4 实现TaskMemoryManager
Source
6.4.4 Implementing TaskMemoryManager
现在，我们实现TaskMemoryManager，它使用ChromaDB存储和检索GAIA问题解决记录。
该类负责从执行历史中提取结构化记忆、检查重复项，并将其存储到ChromaDB的整个流程。
Source
Now we implement TaskMemoryManager, which stores and retrieves GAIA problem-solving records using ChromaDB. This class handles the entire pipeline of extracting structured memories from execution history, checking for duplicates, and storing them in ChromaDB.
类初始化
Source
Class initialization
TaskMemoryManager构造函数通过依赖注入接收一个LlmClient，用于内存提取和重复检查。
ChromaDB客户端和集合也在此处初始化。
Source
The TaskMemoryManager constructor receives an LlmClient through injection, which is used for memory extraction and duplicate checking. The ChromaDB client and collection are also initialized here.
清单 6.30 TaskMemory Manager 初始化
Source
Listing 6.30 TaskMemory Manager initialization
代码保持原样
import uuid import chromadb from chromadb.utils.embedding_functions import OpenAIEmbeddingFunction class TaskMemoryManager: """Memory manager for GAIA problem-solving learning""" def __init__( self, llm_client: LlmClient, collection_name: str = "task_memories", ): self.llm_client = llm_client # ChromaDB setup self.client = chromadb.Client() embedding_fn = OpenAIEmbeddingFunction( model_name="text-embedding-3-small" ) self.collection = self.client.get_or_create_collection( name=collection_name, embedding_function=embedding_fn )
记忆提取方法
Source
Memory extraction methods
我们实现了一些方法，用于从执行历史中提取结构化的记忆。
_format_execution_history() 方法将事件列表转换为适合大语言模型的文本格式。
它遍历每个事件的内容，并分别格式化消息、工具调用和工具结果。
Source
We implement methods to extract structured memories from execution history. The _format_execution_history() converts the event list into a text format suitable for the LLM. It iterates through each event's content and formats messages, tool calls, and tool results separately.
在_extract_memory()中，我们传入response_format=TaskMemory，以便LLM生成符合TaskMemory模式的JSON。
由于LlmClient会解析此JSON并返回TaskMemory实例，因此无需单独的JSON解析逻辑。
Source
In _extract_memory(), we pass response_format=TaskMemory so the LLM generates JSON matching the TaskMemory schema. Since LlmClient parses this and returns a TaskMemory instance, no separate JSON parsing logic is needed.
清单6.31 记忆提取方法
Source
Listing 6.31 Memory extraction methods
代码保持原样
class TaskMemoryManager: # ... previous code ... async def _extract_memory(self, execution_history: str) -> TaskMemory | None: """Extract structured memory from execution history""" prompt = TASK_MEMORY_EXTRACTION_PROMPT.format( execution_history=execution_history ) try: return await self.llm_client.ask( prompt=prompt, response_format=TaskMemory ) except Exception as e: print(f"Memory extraction failed: {e}") return None def _format_execution_history(self, events: list[Event]) -> str: """Convert event list to text""" lines = [] for event in events: for item in event.content: if isinstance(item, Message): lines.append(f"[{item.role}]: {item.content}") elif isinstance(item, ToolCall): lines.append(f"[Tool Call]: {item.name}({item.arguments})") elif isinstance(item, ToolResult): content_preview = str(item.content[0])[:500] if item.content else "" lines.append(f"[Tool Result]: {item.name} -> {content_preview}") return "\n".join(lines)
重复检查方法
Source
Duplicate check method
此方法检查新记忆是否与现有记忆重复。
如果没有现有搜索结果，则返回False。
它将现有记忆转换为文本，并将其与新记忆一同包含在提示中。
当接收到带有DuplicateCheckResult模式的响应时，可以通过result.decision直接访问决策结果。
如果决策为“SKIP”，则表示该记忆是重复的，不应存储，因此该方法返回True以防止存储。
Source
This method checks whether a new memory duplicates an existing one. If there are no existing search results, it returns False. It converts existing memories to text and includes them, along with the new memory, in the prompt. When a response is received with the DuplicateCheckResult schema, the decision can be accessed directly through result.decision. If the decision is "SKIP", it means the memory is a duplicate and should not be stored, so the method returns True to prevent storage.
清单6.32 重复检查方法
Source
Listing 6.32 Duplicate check method
代码保持原样
class TaskMemoryManager: # ... previous code ... async def _is_duplicate( self, new_memory: TaskMemory, existing_results: dict ) -> bool: """Determine if a new memory duplicates an existing one""" if not existing_results["metadatas"] or not existing_results["metadatas"][0]: return False # Convert existing memories to text existing_texts = [] for meta in existing_results["metadatas"][0]: existing_texts.append( f"task_summary: {meta.get('task_summary')}, " f"- approach: {meta.get('approach')}, " f"is_correct: {meta.get('is_correct')}" ) prompt = DUPLICATE_CHECK_PROMPT.format( existing_memories="\n".join(existing_texts), new_memory=f"task_summary: {new_memory.task_summary}, " f"approach: {new_memory.approach}, " f"is_correct: {new_memory.is_correct}" ) try: result = await self.llm_client.ask( prompt=prompt, response_format=DuplicateCheckResult ) return result.decision == "SKIP" except Exception: return False # Proceed with storage if parsing fails
保存方法
Source
Save method
save()方法将所有组件整合在一起。
它将执行历史转换为文本，使用LLM提取结构化记忆，搜索相似的现有记忆以检查重复项，如果非重复则将该记忆存储在ChromaDB中。
对于文档，它使用to_embedding_text()生成可搜索的文本。
对于元数据，它使用model_dump()将所有TaskMemory字段转换为字典以便存储。
Source
The save() method brings all components together. It converts the execution history to text, extracts structured memory using the LLM, searches for similar existing memories to check for duplicates, and stores the memory in ChromaDB if it is not a duplicate. For documents, it generates searchable text using to_embedding_text(). For metadata, it converts all TaskMemory fields to a dictionary using model_dump() for storage.
清单6.33 TaskMemoryManager save()方法
Source
Listing 6.33 TaskMemoryManager save() method
代码保持原样
class TaskMemoryManager: # ... previous code ... async def save(self, context: ExecutionContext) -> str | None: """ Extract and save memory from execution context. Returns: memory_id if saved, None if ignored as duplicate """ # 1. Convert execution history to text execution_history = self._format_execution_history(context.events) # 2. Extract structured memory using LLM memory = await self._extract_memory(execution_history) if memory is None: return None # 3. Duplicate check - search with the same text used for storage existing = self.collection.query( query_texts=[memory.to_embedding_text()], n_results=3 ) if await self._is_duplicate(memory, existing): return None # 4. Store in ChromaDB memory_id = str(uuid.uuid4()) self.collection.add( ids=[memory_id], documents=[memory.to_embedding_text()], metadatas=[memory.model_dump()] ) return memory_id
搜索方法
Source
Search method
search()方法检索与查询相关的记忆，并将它们作为TaskMemory对象列表返回。
当我们调用collection.query()时，ChromaDB会处理嵌入生成、相似度计算和排序。
通过将结果元数据转换为TaskMemory，我们可以以类型安全的方式访问task_summary、approach、final_answer、is_correct和error_analysis字段。
Source
The search() method retrieves memories related to a query and returns them as a list of TaskMemory objects. When we call collection.query(), ChromaDB handles embedding generation, similarity calculation, and sorting. By converting the result metadata to TaskMemory, we can access the task_summary, approach, final_answer, is_correct, and error_analysis fields in a type-safe way.
清单 6.34 TaskMemoryManager 的 search() 方法
Source
Listing 6.34 TaskMemoryManager search() method
代码保持原样
class TaskMemoryManager: # ... previous code ... async def search(self, query: str, top_k: int = 5) -> list[TaskMemory]: """Search for memories related to the query.""" results = self.collection.query( query_texts=[query], n_results=top_k ) if not results["metadatas"] or not results["metadatas"][0]: return [] return [TaskMemory(**meta) for meta in results["metadatas"][0]]
将MemoryManager集成到智能体中
Source
Integrating MemoryManager into the agent
我们在Agent类中添加了memory_manager。
memory_manager是可选的。
对于不需要长期记忆的简单任务，可以将其保留为None。
在run()方法中，我们将memory_manager传递给ExecutionContext，以便工具可以通过context.memory_manager访问它。
Source
We add memory_manager to the Agent class. The memory_manager is optional. For simple tasks that do not require long-term memory, it can be left as None. In the run() method, we pass the memory_manager to ExecutionContext so that tools can access it via context.memory_manager.

6.4.5 检索记忆
Source
6.4.5 Retrieving memories
使用存储记忆最直观的方式是实现一个检索工具，让智能体在需要时可以调用。
但如果某些记忆应该在大型语言模型看到请求之前就被检索出来呢？
例如，在每次对话开始时检索用户档案信息，或检查之前是否解决过类似问题。
你可以为此实现一个单独的回调函数，但这样与记忆相关的逻辑就会分散在工具和回调之间。
更简洁的方法是让工具本身将上下文注入到大型语言模型的请求中。
Source
The most intuitive way to use stored memories is to implement retrieval as a tool that the agent can call when needed. But what if certain memories should always be retrieved before the LLM sees the request? For example, retrieving user profile information at the start of every conversation or checking whether a similar problem was solved before. You could implement a separate callback for this, but then memory-related logic would be split between a Tool and a callback. A cleaner approach is to let the Tool itself inject context into the LLM request.
基于工具的检索
Source
Tool-based retrieval
我们首先使用一个MemoryTool来检索过去的问题解决记录。
智能体可以调用这个工具来检查类似的问题。
execute()方法会搜索记忆存储，并将结果格式化，以便LLM能够理解哪些方法有效、哪些方法失败。
Source
We start with a MemoryTool that retrieves past problem-solving records. The agent can call this tool to check for similar problems. The execute() method searches the memory store and formats results so the LLM can understand what approaches worked and which ones failed.
清单 6.36 用于显式检索的 MemoryTool
Source
Listing 6.36 MemoryTool for explicit retrieval
代码保持原样
class MemoryTool(BaseTool): """Tool for retrieving past problem-solving records""" def __init__(self): super().__init__( name="recall_memory", description=( "Search for past problem-solving records. " "Use this to check if similar problems were solved before." ), ) async def execute(self, context: ExecutionContext, query: str) -> str: """Search memories and return formatted results""" memories = await context.memory_manager.search(query, top_k=3) if not memories: return "" return self._format_memories(memories) def _format_memories(self, memories: list[TaskMemory]) -> str: """Format memories for display""" results = [] for i, mem in enumerate(memories, 1): status = "Correct" if mem.is_correct else "Incorrect" text = f"""[Record {i}] - Problem: {mem.task_summary} - Approach: {mem.approach} - Answer: {mem.final_answer} - Result: {status}""" if not mem.is_correct and mem.error_analysis: text += f"\n- Error analysis: {mem.error_analysis}" results.append(text) return "\n\n".join(results)
注册此工具后，智能体可以决定何时搜索相关经验。
Source
With this tool registered, the agent can decide when to search for relevant experiences.
通过process_llm_request实现自动注入
Source
Automatic injection with process_llm_request
基于工具的检索在搜索为可选时效果良好。
但对于某些用例，你希望在每个LLM调用之前自动检索记忆。
无需创建单独的回调函数，而是重写BaseTool中的process_llm_request()方法。
该方法在每个LLM请求之前运行，并可直接修改请求。
Source
Tool-based retrieval works well when searching is optional. But for some use cases, you want memories retrieved automatically before every LLM call. Instead of creating a separate callback, override the process_llm_request() method in BaseTool. This method runs before each LLM request and can modify the request directly.
关键在于，你可以在 process_llm_request() 内部复用 execute() 的逻辑。
process_llm_request() 无需重复搜索和格式化代码，只需调用 execute() 并将其结果附加到 LLM 请求中。
Source
The key insight is that you can reuse the execute() logic inside process_llm_request(). Rather than duplicating the search and formatting code, process_llm_request() simply calls execute() and appends its result to the LLM request.
该工具是可由LLM调用还是仅用于自动注入，取决于tool_definition的设置。
如果tool_definition是一个字典，LLM可以显式调用它。
如果tool_definition为None，该工具不会出现在LLM的工具列表中，但process_llm_request()仍会在每次LLM调用前运行。
为简化起见，我们在此通过设置tool_definition=None来使用自动注入。
Source
Whether the tool is callable by the LLM or only used for automatic injection depends on tool_definition. If tool_definition is a dict, the LLM can call it explicitly. If tool_definition is None, the tool won't appear in the LLM's tool list, but process_llm_request() still runs before every LLM call. For simplicity, we use automatic injection here by setting tool_definition=None.
清单 6.37 带自动注入功能的 MemoryTool
Source
Listing 6.37 MemoryTool with automatic injection
代码保持原样
class MemoryTool(BaseTool): # ... execute, _format_memories same as above ... def __init__(self): super().__init__( name="recall_memory", description="...", tool_definition=None, # Automatic injection only ) async def process_llm_request( self, context: ExecutionContext, request: LlmRequest, ) -> None: """Inject relevant memories before LLM call""" user_msgs = [c for c in request.contents if isinstance(c, Message) and c.role == "user"] if not user_msgs: return result = await self.execute(context, user_msgs[-1].content) if not result: return request.append_instructions( f"""The following are records from similar problems solved in the past: <PAST_EXPERIENCES> {result} </PAST_EXPERIENCES> Reference successful approaches and avoid approaches that led to failures.""" )
与前一版本相比，唯一的改动是在init中添加了tool_definition=None。
这使得该工具对LLM不可见，但其process_llm_request()方法仍会在每次LLM调用前运行，自动注入相关记忆。
如果您希望LLM显式调用此工具，只需移除tool_definition=None这一行即可。
Source
The only change from the previous version is adding tool_definition=None in init. This makes the tool invisible to the LLM, but its process_llm_request() method still runs before every LLM call, automatically injecting relevant memories. If you want the LLM to call this tool explicitly instead, simply remove the tool_definition=None line.
集成到智能体中
Source
Integrating into the agent
为了让process_llm_request()正常工作，我们修改了Agent的_prepare_llm_request()方法。
在第4章中，我们使用简单的列表推导式构建了工具列表：
Source
To make process_llm_request() work, we modify the Agent's _prepare_llm_request() method. In chapter 4, we built the tools list with a simple comprehension:
代码保持原样
tools = [t.tool_definition for t in request.tools]
现在我们需要进行两处修改。
首先，过滤掉tool_definition为None的工具，因为有些工具可能仅提供自动注入功能，而无法由LLM调用。
其次，调用每个工具的process_llm_request()方法。
请注意，由于process_llm_request()是异步的，该方法也变为异步。
Source
Now we need two changes. First, filter out tools where tool_definition is None, since some tools may only provide automatic injection without being callable by the LLM. Second, call each tool's process_llm_request() method. Note that the method becomes async since process_llm_request() is asynchronous.
清单6.38 用于工具注入的修改版_prepare_llm_request()
Source
Listing 6.38 Modified _prepare_llm_request() for tool injection
代码保持原样
class Agent: # ... existing code ... async def _prepare_llm_request( self, context: ExecutionContext ) -> LlmRequest: flat_contents = [] for event in context.events: flat_contents.extend(event.content) # Filter tools that should be exposed to the LLM llm_tools = [t for t in self.tools if t.tool_definition is not None] request = LlmRequest( instructions=[self.instructions] if self.instructions else [], contents=flat_contents, tools=llm_tools, tool_choice="auto" if llm_tools else None, ) # Let tools modify the request for tool in self.tools: await tool.process_llm_request(context, request) return request
过滤逻辑允许工具参与process_llm_request()，而无需出现在LLM的工具列表中。
MemoryTool采用这种模式：它设置tool_definition=None，使LLM无法调用它，但其process_llm_request()仍会运行，以自动注入记忆。
Source
The filtering logic allows a tool to participate in process_llm_request() without appearing in the LLM's tool list. MemoryTool uses this pattern: it sets tool_definition=None so the LLM cannot call it, but its process_llm_request() still runs to inject memories automatically.
6.5 总结
Source
6.5 Summary
记忆功能将智能体从一个无状态的工具转变为能够跨交互学习和适应的智能助手。
Source
Memory transforms an agent from a stateless tool into an intelligent assistant that learns and adapts across interactions.
这三种使用模式应对不同的挑战：模式1（一次性执行）在单次运行中管理上下文，模式2（持续执行）在多次运行间维持对话，模式3（长期记忆）在多个会话间保存知识。
Source
The three usage patterns address different challenges: Pattern 1 (One-off Execution) manages context within a single run, Pattern 2 (Continuous Execution) maintains conversation across multiple runs, and Pattern 3 (Long-term Memory) preserves knowledge across sessions.
上下文管理策略遵循分层方法：首先测量令牌数量，对工具结果应用压缩，最后才使用摘要作为最终手段。
核心原则是将存储与呈现分离——ExecutionContext保持不可变，而LlmRequest针对每次调用进行优化。
Source
Context management strategies follow a hierarchical approach: measure tokens first, apply Compaction for tool results, and use Summarization as a last resort. The key principle is separating storage from presentation—ExecutionContext remains immutable while LlmRequest is optimized for each call.
Session和SessionManager通过跨run()调用持久化事件和状态，支持多轮对话。
相同的架构支持异步的人机协同工作流，当执行需要用户批准时暂停，并在确认到达后恢复。
Source
Session and SessionManager enable multi-turn conversations by persisting events and state across run() calls. The same architecture supports asynchronous Human-in-the-Loop workflows, where execution pauses for user approval and resumes when confirmation arrives.
长期记忆结合了写入与检索策略：结构化信息从执行历史中提取，经过重复性检查后存储于向量数据库中，并在新任务相关时进行检索。
Source
Long-term memory combines Write and Retrieval strategies: structured information is extracted from execution history, checked for duplicates, stored in a vector database, and retrieved when relevant to new tasks.
记忆检索可以作为一种显式工具，由代理按需调用；也可以通过process_llm_request()自动注入，在每次LLM调用前添加相关上下文。
Source
Memory retrieval can be implemented as an explicit tool the agent calls on demand, or as automatic injection via process_llm_request() that adds relevant context before every LLM call.
